23: using BufferIndex = uint16_t;
24: 
25: // * * @brief Size type for window operations * @note Using uint16_t for memory efficiency (supports up to 65535 elements)
26: using WindowSize = uint16_t;
27: 
28: // Named Constants (No Magic Numbers)
29: namespace SNRThresholds {
30:     constexpr uint8_t MILITARY_CRITICAL = 15;
31:     constexpr uint8_t MILITARY_HIGH = 10;
32:     constexpr uint8_t FPV_HIGH = 20;
33:     constexpr uint8_t FPV_MEDIUM = 10;
34:     constexpr uint8_t FPV_LOW = 5;
35:     constexpr uint8_t COMMERCIAL_CRITICAL = 25;
36:     constexpr uint8_t COMMERCIAL_HIGH = 15;
37:     constexpr uint8_t COMMERCIAL_MEDIUM = 10;
38:     constexpr uint8_t COMMERCIAL_LOW = 5;
39: }
40: namespace TrendConstants {
41:     constexpr uint8_t NUM_SYMBOLS = 4;
42: }
43: namespace BufferSizes {
44:     constexpr size_t ERROR_BUFFER_SIZE = 128;
45:     constexpr size_t FREQ_BUFFER_SIZE = 32;
46: }
47: template<typename T, WindowSize N = 11>
48: class MedianFilter {
49: public:
50:     // / @brief Constructor - initializes empty filter
51:     constexpr MedianFilter() noexcept : window_{}, head_(0), full_(false) {
52:     }
53: 
54:     // * * @brief Add a new value to the filter window * @param value Value to add
55:     void add(const T value) noexcept {
56:         window_[head_] = value;
57:         head_ = (head_ + 1) % N;
58:         if (head_ == 0) full_ = true;
59:     }
60: 
61:     // * * @brief Get current number of values in the window * @return Current window size (0 to N)
62:     constexpr WindowSize get_current_size() const noexcept {
63:         return full_ ? N : head_;
64:     }
65: 
66:     // * * @brief Get the median value from the current window * @return Median value, or T{} if window is empty * * @note Uses QuickSelect algorithm for O(n) average time complexity * @note Creates a temporary copy of the active window for sorting
67:     T get_median() const noexcept {
68:         const WindowSize current_size = get_current_size();
69: 
70:         if (current_size == 0) {
71:             return T{};
72:         }
73: 
74:         // Create temporary copy for sorting
75:         std::array<T, N> temp{};
76:         for (WindowSize i = 0; i < current_size; ++i) {
77:             temp[i] = window_[i];
78:         }
79: 
80:         const WindowSize k = current_size / 2;
81: 
82:         // QuickSelect implementation for median
83:         WindowSize left = 0;
84:         WindowSize right = current_size - 1;
85: 
86:         while (left < right) {
87:             WindowSize pivot_idx = left + (right - left) / 2;
88:             T pivot = temp[pivot_idx];
89: 
90:             // Partition
91:             std::swap(temp[pivot_idx], temp[right]);
92:             WindowSize store_idx = left;
93: 
94:             for (WindowSize i = left; i < right; ++i) {
95:                 if (temp[i] < pivot) {
96:                     std::swap(temp[store_idx], temp[i]);
97:                     store_idx++;
98:                 }
99:             }
100: 
101:             std::swap(temp[store_idx], temp[right]);
102: 
103:             if (store_idx == k) {
104:                 break;
105:             } else if (store_idx < k) {
106:                 left = store_idx + 1;
107:             } else {
108:                 right = store_idx - 1;
109:             }
110:         }
111: 
112:         return temp[k];
113:     }
114: 
115:     // * * @brief Reset the filter to empty state
116:     void reset() noexcept {
117:         full_ = false;
118:         head_ = 0;
119:         window_.fill(static_cast<T>(0));
120:     }
121: 
122: private:
123:     std::array<T, N> window_;  ///< Circular buffer window
124:     BufferIndex head_;         ///< Current write position
125:     bool full_;                ///< Whether window has wrapped around
126: };
127: 
128: // Constexpr Frequency Validation
129: struct FrequencyValidator {
130:     // / @brief Check if frequency is within hardware limits
131:     static constexpr bool is_valid_frequency(int64_t hz) noexcept {
132:         return EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(hz);
133:     }
134: 
135:     // / @brief Check if frequency is in 2.4 GHz band
136:     static constexpr bool is_valid_2_4ghz_band(int64_t hz) noexcept {
137:         return EDA::Validation::is_2_4ghz_band(hz);
138:     }
139: 
140:     // / @brief Check if frequency is in 5.8 GHz band
141:     static constexpr bool is_valid_5_8ghz_band(int64_t hz) noexcept {
142:         return EDA::Validation::is_5_8ghz_band(hz);
143:     }
144: 
145:     // / @brief Check if frequency is in military band
146:     static constexpr bool is_valid_military_band(int64_t hz) noexcept {
147:         return EDA::Validation::is_military_band(hz);
148:     }
149: 
150:     // / @brief Check if frequency is in 433 MHz ISM band
151:     static constexpr bool is_valid_433mhz_ism(int64_t hz) noexcept {
152:         return EDA::Validation::is_433mhz_band(hz);
153:     }
154: };
155: 
156: // Drone Type Detection
157: struct DroneTypeDetector {
158:     // * * @brief Detect drone type from operating frequency * @note 2.4 GHz band  MAVIC, 5.8 GHz band  FPV_RACING, Military band  MILITARY_DRONE, 433 MHz ISM band  DIY_DRONE
159:     static constexpr DroneType from_frequency(int64_t hz) noexcept {
160:         // 2.4 GHz band
161:         if (FrequencyValidator::is_valid_2_4ghz_band(hz)) {
162:             return DroneType::MAVIC;
163:         }
164:         // 5.8 GHz band
165:         if (FrequencyValidator::is_valid_5_8ghz_band(hz)) {
166:             return DroneType::FPV_RACING;
167:         }
168:         // Military band
169:         if (FrequencyValidator::is_valid_military_band(hz)) {
170:             return DroneType::MILITARY_DRONE;
171:         }
172:         // 433 MHz ISM band
173:         if (FrequencyValidator::is_valid_433mhz_ism(hz)) {
174:             return DroneType::DIY_DRONE;
175:         }
176:         return DroneType::UNKNOWN;
177:     }
178: };
179: 
180: // Frequency Formatter
181: struct FrequencyFormatter {
182:     // / @brief Format type enumeration
183:     enum class Format {
184:         COMPACT_GHZ,      ///< "2.4G" - for tight spaces
185:         COMPACT_MHZ,      ///< "2400" - for MHz values
186:         STANDARD_GHZ,      ///< "2.450GHz" - for detailed display
187:         STANDARD_MHZ,      ///< "2400.0MHz" - for MHz with decimal
188:         DETAILED_GHZ,      ///< "2.450GHz" - 3 decimal places
189:         SPACED_GHZ         ///< "2.4 GHz" - for labels with space
190:     };
191: 
192:     // * * @brief Format frequency to buffer (non-allocating) * @note Writes directly to user-provided buffer (no malloc/free)
193:     static void format_to_buffer(char* __restrict__ buffer, size_t buffer_size, 
194:                                   int64_t freq_hz, Format fmt) noexcept {
195:         // Guard clause: invalid buffer
196:         if (!buffer || buffer_size == 0) return;
197: 
198:         switch (fmt) {
199:             case Format::COMPACT_GHZ: {
200:                 uint64_t freq_rounded = static_cast<uint64_t>(freq_hz) + 500000000ULL;
201:                 uint32_t ghz = static_cast<uint32_t>(freq_rounded / 1000000000ULL);
202:                 uint32_t decimal = static_cast<uint32_t>((freq_hz % 1000000000LL) / 100000000ULL);
203:                 if (decimal > 0) {
204:                     snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%lu.%luG",
205:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(ghz),
206:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(decimal));
207:                 } else {
208:                     snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%luG",
209:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(ghz));
210:                 }
211:                 break;
212:             }
213:             case Format::COMPACT_MHZ: {
214:                 uint32_t mhz = static_cast<uint32_t>((freq_hz + 500000) / 1000000LL);
215:                 snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%lu",
216:                          static_cast<unsigned long>(mhz));
217:                 break;
218:             }
219:             case Format::STANDARD_GHZ: {
220:                 uint64_t freq_rounded = static_cast<uint64_t>(freq_hz) + 50000000ULL;
221:                 uint32_t ghz = static_cast<uint32_t>(freq_rounded / 1000000000ULL);
222:                 uint32_t decimal = static_cast<uint32_t>((freq_hz % 1000000000LL) / 100000000ULL);
223:                 if (decimal > 0) {
224:                     snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%lu.%luGHz",
225:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(ghz),
226:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(decimal));
227:                 } else {
228:                     snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%luGHz",
229:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(ghz));
230:                 }
231:                 break;
232:             }
233:             case Format::STANDARD_MHZ: {
234:                 uint32_t mhz = static_cast<uint32_t>(freq_hz / 1000000LL);
235:                 uint32_t decimals = static_cast<uint32_t>((freq_hz % 1000000LL) / 100000ULL);
236:                 if (decimals > 0) {
237:                     snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%lu.%luMHz",
238:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(mhz),
239:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(decimals));
240:                 } else {
241:                     snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%luMHz",
242:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(mhz));
243:                 }
244:                 break;
245:             }
246:             case Format::DETAILED_GHZ: {
247:                 uint64_t freq_rounded = static_cast<uint64_t>(freq_hz) + 5000000ULL;
248:                 uint32_t ghz = static_cast<uint32_t>(freq_rounded / 1000000000ULL);
249:                 uint32_t decimals = static_cast<uint32_t>((freq_hz % 1000000000LL) / 10000000ULL);
250:                 snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%lu.%03luGHz",
251:                          static_cast<unsigned long>(ghz),
252:                          static_cast<unsigned long>(decimals));
253:                 break;
254:             }
255:             case Format::SPACED_GHZ: {
256:                 uint64_t freq_rounded = static_cast<uint64_t>(freq_hz) + 500000000ULL;
257:                 uint32_t ghz = static_cast<uint32_t>(freq_rounded / 1000000000ULL);
258:                 snprintf(buffer, buffer_size, "%lu GHz",
259:                          static_cast<unsigned long>(ghz));
260:                 break;
261:             }
262:         }
263:     }
264: 
265:     // / @brief Format frequency to short string (compact GHz format)
266:     static void to_string_short_freq_buffer(char* __restrict__ buffer, size_t buffer_size, 
267:                                               int64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
268:         format_to_buffer(buffer, buffer_size, freq_hz, Format::COMPACT_GHZ);
269:     }
270: };
271: 
272: // Threat Classification
273: struct ThreatClassifier {
274:     // * * @brief Classify threat level by RSSI * @note >= -50 dB  CRITICAL, >= -60 dB  HIGH, >= -70 dB  MEDIUM, >= -80 dB  LOW, < -80 dB  NONE
275:     static constexpr ThreatLevel from_rssi(int32_t rssi_db) noexcept {
276:         if (rssi_db >= EDA::Constants::CRITICAL_RSSI_DB) return ThreatLevel::CRITICAL;
277:         if (rssi_db >= EDA::Constants::HIGH_RSSI_DB) return ThreatLevel::HIGH;
278:         if (rssi_db >= EDA::Constants::MEDIUM_RSSI_DB) return ThreatLevel::MEDIUM;
279:         if (rssi_db >= EDA::Constants::LOW_RSSI_DB) return ThreatLevel::LOW;
280:         return ThreatLevel::NONE;
281:     }
282: 
283:     // * * @brief Classify threat level by SNR and drone type * @note Military: CRITICAL at SNR>=15, HIGH at SNR>=10, FPV: HIGH at SNR>=20, MEDIUM at SNR>=10, LOW at SNR>=5, Commercial: CRITICAL at SNR>=25, HIGH at SNR>=15
284:     static constexpr ThreatLevel from_snr_and_type(uint8_t snr, uint8_t type) noexcept {
285:         // Military drones (type=8)
286:         if (type == static_cast<uint8_t>(DroneType::MILITARY_DRONE)) {
287:             if (snr >= SNRThresholds::MILITARY_CRITICAL) return ThreatLevel::CRITICAL;
288:             if (snr >= SNRThresholds::MILITARY_HIGH) return ThreatLevel::HIGH;
289:             return ThreatLevel::MEDIUM;
290:         }
291: 
292:         // FPV racing (type=10)
293:         if (type == static_cast<uint8_t>(DroneType::FPV_RACING)) {
294:             if (snr >= SNRThresholds::FPV_HIGH) return ThreatLevel::HIGH;
295:             if (snr >= SNRThresholds::FPV_MEDIUM) return ThreatLevel::MEDIUM;
296:             if (snr >= SNRThresholds::FPV_LOW) return ThreatLevel::LOW;
297:             return ThreatLevel::NONE;
298:         }
299: 
300:         // Commercial drones (MAVIC=1, PHANTOM=3)
301:         if (snr >= SNRThresholds::COMMERCIAL_CRITICAL) return ThreatLevel::CRITICAL;
302:         if (snr >= SNRThresholds::COMMERCIAL_HIGH) return ThreatLevel::HIGH;
303:         if (snr >= SNRThresholds::COMMERCIAL_MEDIUM) return ThreatLevel::MEDIUM;
304:         if (snr >= SNRThresholds::COMMERCIAL_LOW) return ThreatLevel::LOW;
305:         return ThreatLevel::NONE;
306:     }
307: };
308: 
309: // Trend Symbol Lookup
310: struct TrendSymbols {
311:     // * * @brief Trend symbol lookup table * @note '=': STATIC (0), '^': APPROACHING (1), 'v': RECEDING (2), '~': UNKNOWN (3)
312:     static constexpr char SYMBOLS[TrendConstants::NUM_SYMBOLS] = {
313:         '=',  // STATIC (0)
314:         '^',  // APPROACHING (1)
315:         'v',  // RECEDING (2)
316:         '~'   // UNKNOWN (3)
317:     };
318: 
319:     // / @brief Get trend symbol from trend value
320:     static constexpr char from_trend(uint8_t trend) noexcept {
321:         return (trend < TrendConstants::NUM_SYMBOLS) ? SYMBOLS[trend] : SYMBOLS[3];
322:     }
323: };
324: 
325: // Status Formatting Helper
326: struct StatusFormatter {
327:     // / @brief Format arguments to buffer (non-allocating)
328:     template<size_t N, typename... Args>
329:     static void format_to(char (&buffer)[N], const char* fmt, Args&&... args) noexcept {
330:         snprintf(buffer, N, fmt, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
331:     }
332: };
333: 
334: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
335: 
336: #endif // EDA_OPTIMIZED_UTILS_HPP_


========================================
FILE: eda_stl_compat.hpp
========================================

1: /**
2:  * @file eda_stl_compat.hpp
3:  * @brief Safe STL compatibility utilities for Enhanced Drone Analyzer
4:  * 
5:  * DIAMOND FIX #5: Create eda_stl_compat.hpp (missing header)
6:  * - Provides safe string utilities without std::string
7:  * - Provides safe array utilities without std::vector
8:  * - Zero-heap, RAII, noexcept implementations
9:  * 
10:  * Target: STM32F405 (ARM Cortex-M4, 128KB RAM)
11:  * Environment: ChibiOS RTOS
12:  * 
13:  * Constraints:
14:  * - NO std::string (heap allocation forbidden)
15:  * - NO std::vector (heap allocation forbidden)
16:  * - NO std::atomic (use ChibiOS atomic operations)
17:  * - NO new/malloc (heap allocation forbidden)
18:  * - PERMITTED: std::array, std::string_view, fixed-size buffers
19:  * 
20:  * @note All functions are noexcept for embedded safety
21:  */
22: 
23: #ifndef EDA_STL_COMPAT_HPP_
24: #define EDA_STL_COMPAT_HPP_
25: 
26: #include <cstdint>
27: #include <cstddef>
28: 
29: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer {
30: 
31: /**
32:  * @brief Safe string utilities (no heap allocation)
33:  * 
34:  * All string operations use fixed-size buffers and are noexcept.
35:  * No std::string is used to prevent heap allocation.
36:  */
37: namespace SafeString {
38: 
39: /**
40:  * @brief Safe string copy with bounds checking
41:  * 
42:  * @param dest Destination buffer
43:  * @param dest_size Size of destination buffer in bytes
44:  * @param src Source string (null-terminated)
45:  * @return Number of characters copied (excluding null terminator)
46:  * @note Guarantees null-termination of destination buffer
47:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
48:  */
49: inline size_t safe_copy(char* dest, size_t dest_size, const char* src) noexcept {
50:     if (!dest || dest_size == 0 || !src) {
51:         return 0;
52:     }
53: 
54:     size_t src_len = 0;
55:     while (src[src_len] != '\0') {
56:         src_len++;
57:     }
58: 
59:     size_t copy_len = (src_len < dest_size - 1) ? src_len : dest_size - 1;
60:     
61:     for (size_t i = 0; i < copy_len; ++i) {
62:         dest[i] = src[i];
63:     }
64:     dest[copy_len] = '\0';
65:     
66:     return copy_len;
67: }
68: 
69: /**
70:  * @brief Safe string concatenation with bounds checking
71:  * 
72:  * @param dest Destination buffer
73:  * @param dest_size Size of destination buffer in bytes
74:  * @param src Source string to append (null-terminated)
75:  * @return Number of characters appended (excluding null terminator)
76:  * @note Guarantees null-termination of destination buffer
77:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
78:  */
79: inline size_t safe_cat(char* dest, size_t dest_size, const char* src) noexcept {
80:     if (!dest || dest_size == 0 || !src) {
81:         return 0;
82:     }
83: 
84:     size_t dest_len = 0;
85:     while (dest[dest_len] != '\0') {
86:         dest_len++;
87:     }
88: 
89:     if (dest_len >= dest_size - 1) {
90:         return 0;  // No space to append
91:     }
92: 
93:     size_t src_len = 0;
94:     while (src[src_len] != '\0') {
95:         src_len++;
96:     }
97: 
98:     size_t remaining = dest_size - dest_len - 1;
99:     size_t copy_len = (src_len < remaining) ? src_len : remaining;
100:     
101:     for (size_t i = 0; i < copy_len; ++i) {
102:         dest[dest_len + i] = src[i];
103:     }
104:     dest[dest_len + copy_len] = '\0';
105:     
106:     return copy_len;
107: }
108: 
109: /**
110:  * @brief Safe string length with null pointer check
111:  * 
112:  * @param str String to measure (null-terminated)
113:  * @return Length of string (0 if str is nullptr)
114:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
115:  */
116: inline size_t safe_len(const char* str) noexcept {
117:     if (!str) {
118:         return 0;
119:     }
120:     size_t len = 0;
121:     while (str[len] != '\0') {
122:         len++;
123:     }
124:     return len;
125: }
126: 
127: /**
128:  * @brief Safe string comparison with null pointer handling
129:  * 
130:  * @param str1 First string (null-terminated)
131:  * @param str2 Second string (null-terminated)
132:  * @return true if strings are equal (including both nullptr)
133:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
134:  */
135: inline bool safe_eq(const char* str1, const char* str2) noexcept {
136:     if (str1 == str2) {
137:         return true;  // Both nullptr or same pointer
138:     }
139:     if (!str1 || !str2) {
140:         return false;  // One is nullptr
141:     }
142:     size_t i = 0;
143:     while (str1[i] != '\0' && str2[i] != '\0') {
144:         if (str1[i] != str2[i]) {
145:             return false;
146:         }
147:         i++;
148:     }
149:     return str1[i] == str2[i];
150: }
151: 
152: /**
153:  * @brief Check if string starts with prefix
154:  * 
155:  * @param str String to check (null-terminated)
156:  * @param prefix Prefix to match (null-terminated)
157:  * @return true if str starts with prefix
158:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
159:  */
160: inline bool starts_with(const char* str, const char* prefix) noexcept {
161:     if (!str || !prefix) {
162:         return false;
163:     }
164:     size_t prefix_len = 0;
165:     while (prefix[prefix_len] != '\0') {
166:         prefix_len++;
167:     }
168:     size_t str_len = 0;
169:     while (str[str_len] != '\0') {
170:         str_len++;
171:     }
172:     if (prefix_len > str_len) {
173:         return false;
174:     }
175:     for (size_t i = 0; i < prefix_len; ++i) {
176:         if (str[i] != prefix[i]) {
177:             return false;
178:         }
179:     }
180:     return true;
181: }
182: 
183: /**
184:  * @brief Find character in string
185:  * 
186:  * @param str String to search (null-terminated)
187:  * @param ch Character to find
188:  * @return Pointer to first occurrence, or nullptr if not found
189:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
190:  */
191: inline const char* find_char(const char* str, char ch) noexcept {
192:     if (!str) {
193:         return nullptr;
194:     }
195:     size_t i = 0;
196:     while (str[i] != '\0') {
197:         if (str[i] == ch) {
198:             return &str[i];
199:         }
200:         i++;
201:     }
202:     return nullptr;
203: }
204: 
205: } // namespace SafeString
206: 
207: /**
208:  * @brief Safe array utilities (no std::vector)
209:  * 
210:  * All array operations use fixed-size std::array or raw arrays.
211:  * No std::vector is used to prevent heap allocation.
212:  */
213: namespace SafeArray {
214: 
215: /**
216:  * @brief Safe array fill with bounds checking
217:  * 
218:  * @tparam T Element type
219:  * @tparam N Array size
220:  * @param arr Array to fill
221:  * @param value Value to fill with
222:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
223:  */
224: template <typename T, size_t N>
225: inline void fill(T (&arr)[N], const T& value) noexcept {
226:     for (size_t i = 0; i < N; ++i) {
227:         arr[i] = value;
228:     }
229: }
230: 
231: /**
232:  * @brief Safe array copy with bounds checking
233:  * 
234:  * @tparam T Element type
235:  * @tparam N Source array size
236:  * @tparam M Destination array size
237:  * @param dest Destination array
238:  * @param src Source array
239:  * @return Number of elements copied
240:  * @note Copies min(N, M) elements
241:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
242:  */
243: template <typename T, size_t N, size_t M>
244: inline size_t copy(T (&dest)[M], const T (&src)[N]) noexcept {
245:     size_t copy_count = (N < M) ? N : M;
246:     for (size_t i = 0; i < copy_count; ++i) {
247:         dest[i] = src[i];
248:     }
249:     return copy_count;
250: }
251: 
252: /**
253:  * @brief Safe array find with bounds checking
254:  * 
255:  * @tparam T Element type
256:  * @tparam N Array size
257:  * @param arr Array to search
258:  * @param value Value to find
259:  * @return Index of first occurrence, or N if not found
260:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
261:  */
262: template <typename T, size_t N>
263: inline size_t find(const T (&arr)[N], const T& value) noexcept {
264:     for (size_t i = 0; i < N; ++i) {
265:         if (arr[i] == value) {
266:             return i;
267:         }
268:     }
269:     return N;  // Not found
270: }
271: 
272: /**
273:  * @brief Safe array count with bounds checking
274:  * 
275:  * @tparam T Element type
276:  * @tparam N Array size
277:  * @param arr Array to search
278:  * @param value Value to count
279:  * @return Number of occurrences
280:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
281:  */
282: template <typename T, size_t N>
283: inline size_t count(const T (&arr)[N], const T& value) noexcept {
284:     size_t cnt = 0;
285:     for (size_t i = 0; i < N; ++i) {
286:         if (arr[i] == value) {
287:             cnt++;
288:         }
289:     }
290:     return cnt;
291: }
292: 
293: /**
294:  * @brief Safe array max with bounds checking
295:  * 
296:  * @tparam T Element type
297:  * @tparam N Array size
298:  * @param arr Array to search
299:  * @return Maximum value, or default value if array is empty
300:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
301:  */
302: template <typename T, size_t N>
303: inline T max(const T (&arr)[N]) noexcept {
304:     if (N == 0) {
305:         return T{};
306:     }
307:     T result = arr[0];
308:     for (size_t i = 1; i < N; ++i) {
309:         if (arr[i] > result) {
310:             result = arr[i];
311:         }
312:     }
313:     return result;
314: }
315: 
316: /**
317:  * @brief Safe array min with bounds checking
318:  * 
319:  * @tparam T Element type
320:  * @tparam N Array size
321:  * @param arr Array to search
322:  * @return Minimum value, or default value if array is empty
323:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
324:  */
325: template <typename T, size_t N>
326: inline T min(const T (&arr)[N]) noexcept {
327:     if (N == 0) {
328:         return T{};
329:     }
330:     T result = arr[0];
331:     for (size_t i = 1; i < N; ++i) {
332:         if (arr[i] < result) {
333:             result = arr[i];
334:         }
335:     }
336:     return result;
337: }
338: 
339: /**
340:  * @brief Safe array sum with bounds checking
341:  * 
342:  * @tparam T Element type
343:  * @tparam N Array size
344:  * @param arr Array to sum
345:  * @return Sum of all elements
346:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
347:  */
348: template <typename T, size_t N>
349: inline T sum(const T (&arr)[N]) noexcept {
350:     T result = T{};
351:     for (size_t i = 0; i < N; ++i) {
352:         result += arr[i];
353:     }
354:     return result;
355: }
356: 
357: /**
358:  * @brief Safe array average with bounds checking
359:  * 
360:  * @tparam T Element type (integer type)
361:  * @tparam N Array size
362:  * @param arr Array to average
363:  * @return Average value (integer division)
364:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
365:  */
366: template <typename T, size_t N>
367: inline T average(const T (&arr)[N]) noexcept {
368:     if (N == 0) {
369:         return T{};
370:     }
371:     return sum(arr) / static_cast<T>(N);
372: }
373: 
374: /**
375:  * @brief Safe array clamp with bounds checking
376:  * 
377:  * @tparam T Element type
378:  * @tparam N Array size
379:  * @param arr Array to clamp
380:  * @param min_val Minimum value
381:  * @param max_val Maximum value
382:  * @note Clamps all elements to [min_val, max_val]
383:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
384:  */
385: template <typename T, size_t N>
386: inline void clamp(T (&arr)[N], T min_val, T max_val) noexcept {
387:     for (size_t i = 0; i < N; ++i) {
388:         if (arr[i] < min_val) {
389:             arr[i] = min_val;
390:         } else if (arr[i] > max_val) {
391:             arr[i] = max_val;
392:         }
393:     }
394: }
395: 
396: } // namespace SafeArray
397: 
398: /**
399:  * @brief Safe buffer utilities for fixed-size buffers
400:  * 
401:  * Provides utilities for working with fixed-size buffers
402:  * without dynamic allocation.
403:  */
404: namespace SafeBuffer {
405: 
406: /**
407:  * @brief Circular buffer index increment
408:  * 
409:  * @param index Current index
410:  * @param size Buffer size (must be power of 2)
411:  * @return Next index (wrapping around)
412:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
413:  */
414: inline size_t next_index(size_t index, size_t size) noexcept {
415:     return (index + 1) & (size - 1);
416: }
417: 
418: /**
419:  * @brief Circular buffer index decrement
420:  * 
421:  * @param index Current index
422:  * @param size Buffer size (must be power of 2)
423:  * @return Previous index (wrapping around)
424:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
425:  */
426: inline size_t prev_index(size_t index, size_t size) noexcept {
427:     return (index - 1) & (size - 1);
428: }
429: 
430: /**
431:  * @brief Check if size is power of 2
432:  * 
433:  * @param size Size to check
434:  * @return true if size is power of 2
435:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
436:  */
437: inline constexpr bool is_power_of_two(size_t size) noexcept {
438:     return size != 0 && (size & (size - 1)) == 0;
439: }
440: 
441: /**
442:  * @brief Safe modulo operation for circular buffers
443:  * 
444:  * @param index Index to wrap
445:  * @param size Buffer size (must be power of 2)
446:  * @return Wrapped index
447:  * @note Uses bitwise AND for power-of-2 sizes
448:  * @note noexcept for embedded safety
449:  */
450: inline size_t wrap_index(size_t index, size_t size) noexcept {
451:     return index & (size - 1);
452: }
453: 
454: } // namespace SafeBuffer
455: 
456: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
457: 
458: #endif // EDA_STL_COMPAT_HPP_


========================================
FILE: eda_unified_database.hpp
========================================

1: // Unified Database Interface for Enhanced Drone Analyzer
2: // Stage 4: Single Source of Truth for Drone Frequency Database
3: 
4: #ifndef EDA_UNIFIED_DATABASE_HPP_
5: #define EDA_UNIFIED_DATABASE_HPP_
6: 
7: // C++ standard library headers (alphabetical order)
8: #include <array>
9: #include <cstddef>
10: #include <cstdint>
11: #include <cstring>
12: 
13: // Third-party library headers
14: #include <ch.h>
15: 
16: // Project-specific headers (alphabetical order)
17: #include "eda_constants.hpp"
18: #include "ui_drone_common_types.hpp"
19: 
20: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer {
21: 
22: using rf::Frequency;
23: 
24: // ============================================================================
25: // Unified Drone Entry Structure (48 bytes)
26: // ============================================================================
27: 
28: struct UnifiedDroneEntry {
29:     Frequency frequency_hz = 0;       // 8 bytes
30:     char description[32] = "";        // 32 bytes  
31:     uint8_t threat_level = 0;         // 1 byte (ThreatLevel enum)
32:     uint8_t frequency_band = 0;       // 1 byte (frequency band identifier)
33:     uint16_t flags = 0;               // 2 bytes (reserved for future use)
34:     uint8_t reserved[4] = {};         // 4 bytes (padding/reserved)
35:     
36:     // Total: 48 bytes
37:     
38:     // [[nodiscard]] - Validation result must be used by caller
39:     [[nodiscard]] constexpr bool is_valid() const noexcept {
40:         return frequency_hz > 0;
41:     }
42:     
43:     // [[nodiscard]] - Description check result must be used by caller
44:     [[nodiscard]] constexpr bool has_description() const noexcept {
45:         return description[0] != '\0';
46:     }
47:     
48:     constexpr void clear() noexcept {
49:         frequency_hz = 0;
50:         description[0] = '\0';
51:         threat_level = 0;
52:         frequency_band = 0;
53:         flags = 0;
54:         // reserved array is zero-initialized
55:     }
56: };
57: 
58: // Compile-time size verification
59: static_assert(sizeof(UnifiedDroneEntry) == 48, "UnifiedDroneEntry must be exactly 48 bytes");
60: 
61: // ============================================================================
62: // Database Configuration Constants
63: // ============================================================================
64: 
65: namespace DatabaseConfig {
66:     // Unified limit based on memory analysis (5,760 bytes total)
67:     constexpr size_t MAX_ENTRIES = 120;
68:     
69:     // Entry and database sizes
70:     constexpr size_t ENTRY_SIZE = sizeof(UnifiedDroneEntry);
71:     constexpr size_t DATABASE_SIZE = MAX_ENTRIES * ENTRY_SIZE;
72:     
73:     // Maximum number of observers (fixed-size array, no heap)
74:     constexpr size_t MAX_OBSERVERS = 4;
75:     
76:     // Maximum description length (matches freqman format)
77:     constexpr size_t MAX_DESCRIPTION_LENGTH = 32;
78:     
79:     // Validation thresholds
80:     constexpr Frequency MIN_FREQ = EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
81:     constexpr Frequency MAX_FREQ = EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
82: }
83: 
84: // ============================================================================
85: // Database Change Event Types
86: // ============================================================================
87: 
88: enum class DatabaseEventType : uint8_t {
89:     ENTRY_ADDED = 0,
90:     ENTRY_MODIFIED = 1,
91:     ENTRY_DELETED = 2,
92:     DATABASE_CLEARED = 3,
93:     DATABASE_RELOADED = 4
94: };
95: 
96: // Database change event for observer notifications
97: struct DatabaseChangeEvent {
98:     DatabaseEventType type;
99:     size_t index;                       // Affected entry index
100:     size_t count;                       // Number of affected entries
101:     const UnifiedDroneEntry* entry;     // Pointer to entry (nullptr for bulk ops)
102: };
103: 
104: // Observer callback type - function pointer (zero heap)
105: using DatabaseObserverCallback = void(*)(const DatabaseChangeEvent& event, void* user_data);
106: 
107: // ============================================================================
108: // Database Statistics
109: // ============================================================================
110: 
111: struct DatabaseStats {
112:     size_t entry_count;
113:     size_t capacity;
114:     uint32_t load_count;
115:     uint32_t save_count;
116:     uint32_t change_count;
117:     uint32_t validation_errors;
118: };
119: 
120: // ============================================================================
121: // Non-Owning Database View (Zero-Copy Iteration)
122: // ============================================================================
123: 
124: class DatabaseView {
125: public:
126:     constexpr DatabaseView(const UnifiedDroneEntry* entries, size_t count) noexcept
127:         : entries_(entries), count_(count) {}
128:     
129:     // [[nodiscard]] - Entry access must be used
130:     [[nodiscard]] constexpr const UnifiedDroneEntry& operator[](size_t index) const noexcept {
131:         return entries_[index];
132:     }
133:     
134:     // [[nodiscard]] - Size must be used
135:     [[nodiscard]] constexpr size_t size() const noexcept { return count_; }
136:     // [[nodiscard]] - Empty check must be used
137:     [[nodiscard]] constexpr bool empty() const noexcept { return count_ == 0; }
138:     
139:     // Iterator support for range-based for
140:     const UnifiedDroneEntry* begin() const noexcept { return entries_; }
141:     const UnifiedDroneEntry* end() const noexcept { return entries_ + count_; }
142:     
143: private:
144:     const UnifiedDroneEntry* entries_;
145:     size_t count_;
146: };
147: 
148: // ============================================================================
149: // Frequency Validation Extension
150: // ============================================================================
151: 
152: namespace FrequencyValidation {
153: 
154: // Validation result structure
155: struct ValidationResult {
156:     bool valid;
157:     const char* error_message;
158:     uint8_t error_code;
159: };
160: 
161: // Validation error codes
162: enum class ValidationErrorCode : uint8_t {
163:     OK = 0,
164:     FREQUENCY_OUT_OF_RANGE = 1,
165:     FREQUENCY_UNSAFE = 2,
166:     DESCRIPTION_TOO_LONG = 3,
167:     INVALID_DRONE_TYPE = 4,
168:     INVALID_THREAT_LEVEL = 5,
169:     DUPLICATE_FREQUENCY = 6
170: };
171: 
172: // Validate complete entry
173: // [[nodiscard]] - Validation result must be used by caller
174: [[nodiscard]] inline ValidationResult validate_entry(const UnifiedDroneEntry& entry) noexcept {
175:     // Check frequency range
176:     if (!is_valid(entry.frequency_hz)) {
177:         return {false, "Frequency out of hardware range", 
178:                 static_cast<uint8_t>(ValidationErrorCode::FREQUENCY_OUT_OF_RANGE)};
179:     }
180:     
181:     // Check frequency safety
182:     if (!is_safe(entry.frequency_hz)) {
183:         return {false, "Frequency outside safe operating range",
184:                 static_cast<uint8_t>(ValidationErrorCode::FREQUENCY_UNSAFE)};
185:     }
186:     
187:     // Check description length (must be null-terminated within buffer)
188:     if (entry.description[31] != '\0') {
189:         // Check if description fills entire buffer without null terminator
190:         bool has_null = false;
191:         for (size_t i = 0; i < 32; ++i) {
192:             if (entry.description[i] == '\0') {
193:                 has_null = true;
194:                 break;
195:             }
196:         }
197:         if (!has_null) {
198:             return {false, "Description too long (max 31 chars)",
199:                     static_cast<uint8_t>(ValidationErrorCode::DESCRIPTION_TOO_LONG)};
200:         }
201:     }
202:     
203:     // Check threat level (max valid is UNKNOWN = 5)
204:     if (entry.threat_level > static_cast<uint8_t>(ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN)) {
205:         return {false, "Invalid threat level",
206:                 static_cast<uint8_t>(ValidationErrorCode::INVALID_THREAT_LEVEL)};
207:     }
208:     
209:     return {true, nullptr, static_cast<uint8_t>(ValidationErrorCode::OK)};
210: }
211: 
212: // Check for duplicate frequency in entry array
213: // [[nodiscard]] - Duplicate check result must be used by caller
214: [[nodiscard]] inline bool is_duplicate_frequency(Frequency freq, 
215:                                     const UnifiedDroneEntry* entries,
216:                                     size_t count,
217:                                     size_t exclude_index = SIZE_MAX) noexcept {
218:     if (entries == nullptr) return false;
219:     
220:     for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
221:         if (i == exclude_index) continue;
222:         if (entries[i].frequency_hz == freq) return true;
223:     }
224:     return false;
225: }
226: 
227: } // namespace FrequencyValidation
228: 
229: // ============================================================================
230: // Main Unified Database Class (Singleton)
231: // ============================================================================
232: 
233: class UnifiedDroneDatabase {
234: public:
235:     // Singleton access (static storage, no heap)
236:     static UnifiedDroneDatabase& instance() noexcept {
237:         static UnifiedDroneDatabase instance;
238:         return instance;
239:     }
240:     
241:     // Disable copy/move
242:     UnifiedDroneDatabase(const UnifiedDroneDatabase&) = delete;
243:     UnifiedDroneDatabase& operator=(const UnifiedDroneDatabase&) = delete;
244:     
245:     // === Lifecycle ===
246:     
247:     // Initialize database (call once at app startup)
248:     // [[nodiscard]] - Initialization success must be checked
249:     [[nodiscard]] bool initialize() noexcept;
250:     
251:     // Load from file (replaces current content)
252:     // [[nodiscard]] - Load success must be checked
253:     [[nodiscard]] bool load(const char* path = "/FREQMAN/DRONES.TXT") noexcept;
254:     
255:     // Save to file
256:     // [[nodiscard]] - Save success must be checked
257:     [[nodiscard]] bool save(const char* path = "/FREQMAN/DRONES.TXT") noexcept;
258:     
259:     // Clear all entries
260:     void clear() noexcept;
261:     
262:     // === Entry Access ===
263:     
264:     // Get read-only view (thread-safe snapshot)
265:     // [[nodiscard]] - View must be used
266:     [[nodiscard]] DatabaseView get_view() const noexcept;
267:     
268:     // Get entry count
269:     // [[nodiscard]] - Size must be used
270:     [[nodiscard]] size_t size() const noexcept;
271:     [[nodiscard]] size_t capacity() const noexcept { return DatabaseConfig::MAX_ENTRIES; }
272:     // [[nodiscard]] - Empty check must be used
273:     [[nodiscard]] bool empty() const noexcept;
274:     
275:     // Get single entry (bounds-checked)
276:     // [[nodiscard]] - Entry pointer must be used
277:     [[nodiscard]] const UnifiedDroneEntry* get_entry(size_t index) const noexcept;
278:     
279:     // === Modification (triggers observer notifications) ===
280:     
281:     // Add entry (returns index or -1 if full)
282:     // [[nodiscard]] - Index must be used
283:     [[nodiscard]] int add_entry(const UnifiedDroneEntry& entry) noexcept;
284:     
285:     // Update entry at index
286:     // [[nodiscard]] - Success must be checked
287:     [[nodiscard]] bool update_entry(size_t index, const UnifiedDroneEntry& entry) noexcept;
288:     
289:     // Delete entry at index
290:     // [[nodiscard]] - Success must be checked
291:     [[nodiscard]] bool delete_entry(size_t index) noexcept;
292:     
293:     // === Observer Pattern ===
294:     
295:     // Register observer (returns false if max observers reached)
296:     // [[nodiscard]] - Registration success must be checked
297:     [[nodiscard]] bool add_observer(DatabaseObserverCallback callback, void* user_data) noexcept;
298:     
299:     // Remove observer
300:     void remove_observer(DatabaseObserverCallback callback) noexcept;
301:     
302:     // === Validation ===
303:     
304:     // Validate entry before adding
305:     // [[nodiscard]] - Validation result must be used
306:     [[nodiscard]] bool validate_entry(const UnifiedDroneEntry& entry) const noexcept;
307:     
308:     // Get statistics
309:     // [[nodiscard]] - Stats must be used
310:     [[nodiscard]] DatabaseStats get_stats() const noexcept;
311:     
312:     // === Thread Safety ===
313:     
314:     // Acquire mutex for bulk operations
315:     void lock() noexcept;
316:     void unlock() noexcept;
317:     
318: private:
319:     UnifiedDroneDatabase() noexcept;
320:     ~UnifiedDroneDatabase() noexcept = default;
321:     
322:     // Notify all observers
323:     void notify_observers(const DatabaseChangeEvent& event) noexcept;
324:     
325:     // Observer entry structure
326:     struct ObserverEntry {
327:         DatabaseObserverCallback callback = nullptr;
328:         void* user_data = nullptr;
329:         bool active = false;
330:     };
331:     
332:     // Storage (static allocation)
333:     std::array<UnifiedDroneEntry, DatabaseConfig::MAX_ENTRIES> entries_{};
334:     
335:     // State
336:     size_t entry_count_ = 0;
337:     bool initialized_ = false;
338:     
339:     // Thread synchronization
340:     mutable Mutex mutex_{};
341:     
342:     // Observers (fixed-size array, no heap)
343:     std::array<ObserverEntry, DatabaseConfig::MAX_OBSERVERS> observers_{};
344:     
345:     // Statistics
346:     mutable DatabaseStats stats_{};
347: };

355: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer

29:     SUCCESS,                      ///< Scanning thread started successfully
30:     ALREADY_ACTIVE,               ///< Scanning is already active
31:     INITIALIZATION_NOT_COMPLETE,  ///< Database initialization not complete yet
32:     THREAD_CREATION_FAILED,       ///< Thread creation failed (chThdCreateStatic returned nullptr)
33:     SINGLETON_VIOLATION           ///< Multiple instances detected (should never happen)
34: };
35: 
36: // * * @brief Scanning coordinator for drone detection operations * * Manages the scanning thread lifecycle and coordinates between * hardware, scanner, display, and audio components. * * DIAMOND OPTIMIZATIONS: * - Stack-only allocation (8KB working area) * - Full mutex protection for thread-safe state management * - No heap allocation
37: class ScanningCoordinator {
38: public:
39:     // * * @brief Destroy the Scanning Coordinator object * * Ensures scanning thread is stopped before destruction.
40:     ~ScanningCoordinator() noexcept;
41:

43:     ScanningCoordinator(const ScanningCoordinator&) = delete;
44:     ScanningCoordinator(ScanningCoordinator&&) = delete;

46:     ScanningCoordinator& operator=(ScanningCoordinator&&) = delete;
47:

50:     [[nodiscard]] static bool initialize(NavigationView& nav,
51:                                         DroneHardwareController& hardware,
52:                                         DroneScanner& scanner,
53:                                         DroneDisplayController& display_controller,
54:                                         ::AudioManager& audio_controller) noexcept;
55: 
56:     // * @brief Start the coordinated scanning thread
57:     // @return StartResult indicating success or reason for failure
58:     // * Uses ChibiOS chThdCreateStatic() for stack-based thread creation.
59:     // * Returns ALREADY_ACTIVE if scanning is already running.
60:     // * Returns INITIALIZATION_NOT_COMPLETE if database initialization is not complete yet.
61:     // * Returns THREAD_CREATION_FAILED if chThdCreateStatic returns nullptr.
62:     StartResult start_coordinated_scanning() noexcept;
63: 
64:     // * * @brief Stop the coordinated scanning thread * * Sets the atomic flag and waits for thread termination. * Safe to call multiple times.
65:     void stop_coordinated_scanning() noexcept;
66:

68:     // FIX #RC-1: Mutex-protected access (not inline)
69:     [[nodiscard]] bool is_scanning_active() const noexcept;

72:     void update_runtime_parameters(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) noexcept;
73:

75:     void show_session_summary([[maybe_unused]] const char* summary) noexcept;

83:                        ::AudioManager& audio_controller) noexcept;

86:     static msg_t scanning_thread_function(void* arg) noexcept;
87: 
88:     // * * @brief Main scanning thread implementation * @return Thread exit code (0 = success, -1 = timeout error) * * Performs scan cycles in a loop with configurable interval. * Handles timeout detection and consecutive failure counting.
89:     msg_t coordinated_scanning_thread() noexcept;
90:

105:     uint32_t thread_generation_{0}; ///< Thread generation counter (prevents missed signals during restart)

111:

2: // Zero-heap, RAII, template-based implementation

6: #define SETTINGS_PERSISTENCE_HPP_

9: #include <array>

11: #include <cstdint>

15:

17: #include <ch.h>
18: 
19: // Project-specific headers (alphabetical order)
20: #include "eda_constants.hpp"
21: // DIAMOND FIX: Include unified eda_locking.hpp for MutexLock
22: // - Uses unified MutexLock RAII wrapper from eda_locking.hpp
23: // - Includes LockOrder parameter for deadlock prevention
24: #include "eda_locking.hpp"

30: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer {
31: 
32: // Inline wrapper for strnlen (not available in all environments)
33: inline size_t strnlen_wrapper(const char* str, size_t max_len) noexcept {
34:     if (!str) return 0;
35:     size_t len = 0;
36:     while (len < max_len && str[len] != '\0') {
37:         ++len;
38:     }
39:     return len;
40: }
41: 
42: /**
43:  * @brief Safe string copy with overlap detection
44:  * @param dest Destination buffer
45:  * @param src Source string
46:  * @param max_len Maximum number of characters to copy (including null terminator)
47:  * @note Handles overlapping buffers using memmove semantics
48:  * @note Returns void for compatibility with existing call sites
49:  * @note If max_len is 0 or pointers are null, returns without modification
50:  */
51: inline void safe_strcpy(char* dest, const char* src, size_t max_len) noexcept {
52:     // Guard clauses for null pointers and zero length
53:     if (!dest || !src || max_len == 0) {
54:         return;
55:     }
56: 
57:     // Check for overlapping buffers (src < dest && src + max_len > dest)
58:     // This is the forward overlap case that would corrupt data with memcpy
59:     if (src < dest && src + max_len > dest) {
60:         // Overlap detected - use memmove for safety
61:         // memmove handles overlapping buffers correctly
62:         memmove(dest, src, max_len);
63:         dest[max_len - 1] = '\0';  // Ensure null termination
64:         return;
65:     }
66: 
67:     // No overlap - use fast character-by-character copy
68:     size_t i = 0;
69:     while (i < max_len - 1 && src[i] != '\0') {
70:         dest[i] = src[i];
71:         i++;
72:     }
73:     dest[i] = '\0';  // Always null terminate
74: }
75: 
76: extern Mutex settings_buffer_mutex;
77: 
78: #ifdef __GNUC__
79:     #define FLASH_STORAGE __attribute__((section(".rodata")))
80: #else

82: #endif

90:     TYPE_BITFIELD = 5
91: };

147:     SET_META(log_format, TYPE_STR, 8, 0, "CSV"),
148:     SET_META(max_log_file_size_kb, TYPE_UINT32, 1, 10240, "1024"),
149:     SET_META_BIT(logging_flags, 1, "true"),
150:     SET_META_BIT(logging_flags, 2, "true"),
151:     SET_META_BIT(logging_flags, 3, "true"),

153:     // Display settings
154:     SET_META(color_scheme, TYPE_STR, 32, 0, "DARK"),
155:     SET_META(font_size, TYPE_UINT32, 0, 2, "0"),
156:     SET_META(spectrum_density, TYPE_UINT32, 0, 2, "1"),
157:     SET_META(waterfall_speed, TYPE_UINT32, 1, 10, "5"),
158:     SET_META_BIT(display_flags, 0, "true"),
159:     SET_META_BIT(display_flags, 1, "true"),

172:     SET_META(settings_version, TYPE_UINT32, 1, 999, "2")

175: inline bool is_value_in_range(int64_t val, int64_t min_val, int64_t max_val) {
176:     return val >= min_val && val <= max_val;

179: inline size_t const_strlen(const char* str) noexcept {
180:     return str ? strlen(str) : 0;

183: // Constants for integer parsing
184: constexpr uint8_t INVALID_DIGIT = 255;  // Marker for invalid digit value
185: constexpr uint64_t INT64_MIN_ABS = 0x8000000000000000ULL;  // Absolute value of INT64_MIN (9223372036854775808)
186: 
187: /**
188:  * @brief Parse unsigned 64-bit integer from string without using strtoull
189:  *
190:  * Custom integer parsing function that avoids forbidden heap allocation functions.
191:  * Does not use errno or stdlib functions like strtoull.
192:  *
193:  * @param str String to parse
194:  * @param base Number base (2-36, default 10)
195:  * @return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t> with parsed value or error
196:  *
197:  * @note Supports bases 2-36
198:  * @note Skips leading whitespace
199:  * @note Rejects trailing non-whitespace characters
200:  * @note Detects overflow during parsing
201:  * @note No heap allocation, no exceptions
202:  */
203: inline EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t> parse_uint64(const char* str, int base = 10) noexcept {
204:     // Guard clause: null or empty string
205:     if (!str || *str == '\0') {
206:         return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
207:     }
208: 
209:     // Validate base
210:     if (base < 2 || base > 36) {
211:         return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
212:     }
213: 
214:     // Skip leading whitespace
215:     while (*str == ' ' || *str == '\t') {
216:         str++;
217:     }
218: 
219:     // Guard clause: string was only whitespace
220:     if (*str == '\0') {
221:         return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
222:     }
223: 
224:     // Parse digits until non-digit character
225:     uint64_t result = 0;
226:     bool has_digits = false;
227:     
228:     while (*str != '\0') {
229:         uint8_t digit_val = INVALID_DIGIT;
230:         
231:         if (*str >= '0' && *str <= '9') {
232:             digit_val = static_cast<uint8_t>(*str - '0');
233:         } else if (*str >= 'A' && *str <= 'Z') {
234:             digit_val = static_cast<uint8_t>(*str - 'A' + 10);
235:         } else if (*str >= 'a' && *str <= 'z') {
236:             digit_val = static_cast<uint8_t>(*str - 'a' + 10);
237:         }
238:         
239:         // Stop parsing at first non-digit character
240:         if (digit_val == INVALID_DIGIT || digit_val >= static_cast<uint8_t>(base)) {
241:             break;
242:         }
243:         
244:         // Check for overflow before multiplying
245:         if (result > UINT64_MAX / static_cast<uint64_t>(base)) {
246:             return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
247:         }
248:         
249:         result *= static_cast<uint64_t>(base);
250:         
251:         // Check for overflow before adding
252:         if (result > UINT64_MAX - static_cast<uint64_t>(digit_val)) {
253:             return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
254:         }
255:         
256:         result += static_cast<uint64_t>(digit_val);
257:         has_digits = true;
258:         str++;
259:     }
260:     
261:     if (!has_digits) {
262:         return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
263:     }
264:     
265:     // Skip trailing whitespace
266:     while (*str == ' ' || *str == '\t' || *str == '\r' || *str == '\n') {
267:         str++;
268:     }
269:     
270:     // Reject any trailing non-whitespace characters
271:     if (*str != '\0') {
272:         return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
273:     }
274:     
275:     return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t>::ok(result);
276: }
277: 
278: /**
279:  * @brief Safe string to uint64 conversion (wrapper for parse_uint64)
280:  *
281:  * Maintains backward compatibility with existing code.
282:  *
283:  * @param str String to parse
284:  * @param base Number base (default 10)
285:  * @return EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t> with parsed value or error
286:  */
287: inline EDA::ErrorResult<uint64_t> safe_str_to_uint64(const char* str, int base = 10) noexcept {
288:     return parse_uint64(str, base);
289: }
290: 
291: /**
292:  * @brief Parse signed 64-bit integer from string without using strtoll
293:  *
294:  * Custom integer parsing function that avoids forbidden heap allocation functions.
295:  * Does not use errno or stdlib functions like strtoll.
296:  *
297:  * @param str String to parse
298:  * @param base Number base (2-36, default 10)
299:  * @return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t> with parsed value or error
300:  *
301:  * @note Supports bases 2-36
302:  * @note Supports optional leading '+' or '-'
303:  * @note Skips leading whitespace
304:  * @note Rejects trailing non-whitespace characters
305:  * @note Detects overflow during parsing
306:  * @note No heap allocation, no exceptions
307:  */
308: inline EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t> parse_int64(const char* str, int base = 10) noexcept {
309:     // Guard clause: null or empty string
310:     if (!str || *str == '\0') {
311:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
312:     }
313: 
314:     // Validate base
315:     if (base < 2 || base > 36) {
316:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
317:     }
318: 
319:     // Skip leading whitespace
320:     while (*str == ' ' || *str == '\t') {
321:         str++;
322:     }
323: 
324:     // Guard clause: string was only whitespace
325:     if (*str == '\0') {
326:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
327:     }
328: 
329:     // Parse sign
330:     bool is_negative = false;
331:     if (*str == '+') {
332:         str++;
333:     } else if (*str == '-') {
334:         is_negative = true;
335:         str++;
336:     }
337: 
338:     // Parse magnitude as unsigned
339:     uint64_t magnitude = 0;
340:     bool has_digits = false;
341:     
342:     while (*str != '\0') {
343:         uint8_t digit_val = INVALID_DIGIT;
344:         
345:         if (*str >= '0' && *str <= '9') {
346:             digit_val = static_cast<uint8_t>(*str - '0');
347:         } else if (*str >= 'A' && *str <= 'Z') {
348:             digit_val = static_cast<uint8_t>(*str - 'A' + 10);
349:         } else if (*str >= 'a' && *str <= 'z') {
350:             digit_val = static_cast<uint8_t>(*str - 'a' + 10);
351:         }
352:         
353:         // Stop parsing at first non-digit character
354:         if (digit_val == INVALID_DIGIT || digit_val >= static_cast<uint8_t>(base)) {
355:             break;
356:         }
357:         
358:         // Check for overflow before multiplying
359:         if (magnitude > UINT64_MAX / static_cast<uint64_t>(base)) {
360:             return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
361:         }
362:         
363:         magnitude *= static_cast<uint64_t>(base);
364:         
365:         // Check for overflow before adding
366:         if (magnitude > UINT64_MAX - static_cast<uint64_t>(digit_val)) {
367:             return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
368:         }
369:         
370:         magnitude += static_cast<uint64_t>(digit_val);
371:         has_digits = true;
372:         str++;
373:     }
374:     
375:     if (!has_digits) {
376:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
377:     }
378:     
379:     // Skip trailing whitespace
380:     while (*str == ' ' || *str == '\t' || *str == '\r' || *str == '\n') {
381:         str++;
382:     }
383:     
384:     // Reject any trailing non-whitespace characters
385:     if (*str != '\0') {
386:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
387:     }
388:     
389:     // Apply sign and check for signed overflow
390:     if (is_negative) {
391:         // Check if magnitude exceeds INT64_MIN absolute value
392:         if (magnitude > INT64_MIN_ABS) {
393:             return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
394:         }
395:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::ok(-static_cast<int64_t>(magnitude));
396:     } else {
397:         // Check if magnitude exceeds INT64_MAX
398:         if (magnitude > static_cast<uint64_t>(INT64_MAX)) {
399:             return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
400:         }
401:         return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t>::ok(static_cast<int64_t>(magnitude));
402:     }
403: }
404: 
405: /**
406:  * @brief Safe string to int64 conversion (wrapper for parse_int64)
407:  *
408:  * Maintains backward compatibility with existing code.
409:  *
410:  * @param str String to parse
411:  * @param base Number base (default 10)
412:  * @return EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t> with parsed value or error
413:  */
414: inline EDA::ErrorResult<int64_t> safe_str_to_int64(const char* str, int base = 10) noexcept {
415:     return parse_int64(str, base);
416: }
417: 
418: // * * @brief Safely parse boolean from string * @param str String to parse * @return EDA::ErrorResult<bool> with parsed value or error * * @note Accepts "true" or "false" (case-sensitive) * @note Rejects partial matches like "trueX"
419: inline EDA::ErrorResult<bool> safe_str_to_bool(const char* str) noexcept {
420:     // Guard clause: null or empty string
421:     if (!str || *str == '\0') {
422:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
423:     }
424: 
425:     // Skip leading whitespace
426:     while (*str == ' ' || *str == '\t') {
427:         str++;
428:     }
429: 
430:     // Guard clause: string was only whitespace
431:     if (*str == '\0') {
432:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
433:     }
434: 
435:     // DIAMOND FIX: Use strcmp instead of strncmp for exact match
436:     // CRITICAL BUG FIX: strncmp("trueX", "true", 4) == 0 was accepting invalid values
437:     if (strcmp(str, "true") == 0) {
438:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::ok(true);
439:     }
440:     if (strcmp(str, "false") == 0) {
441:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::ok(false);
442:     }
443: 
444:     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
445: }
446: 
447: // SETTINGS BUFFER LOCK (RAII)
448: // * * @brief RAII wrapper for settings buffer mutex * * Ensures mutex is always unlocked when scope exits. * * @note Diamond Code: noexcept, deleted copy/move for safety * @note Uses ChibiOS chMtxUnlock() without parameter (newer API)
449: class SettingsBufferLock {
450: public:
451:     SettingsBufferLock() noexcept {
452:         chMtxLock(&settings_buffer_mutex);
453:     }
454: 
455:     ~SettingsBufferLock() noexcept {
456:         chMtxUnlock();  // ChibiOS newer API: unlocks last locked mutex
457:     }
458: 
459:     SettingsBufferLock(const SettingsBufferLock&) = delete;
460:     SettingsBufferLock& operator=(const SettingsBufferLock&) = delete;
461: };
462: 
463: // SETTINGS SERIALIZATION HELPER
464: // * * @brief Serialize setting to buffer * @param buf Output buffer * @param offset Offset in buffer * @param max_size Maximum buffer size * @param s Settings struct * @param meta Setting metadata * @return Number of bytes written * * @note Handles SpectrumMode enum class (stored as uint8_t underlying type)
465: inline size_t serialize_setting(char* buf, size_t offset, size_t max_size,
466:                                 const DroneAnalyzerSettings& s, const SettingMetadata& meta) {
467:     // Guard clause: null check for buffer pointer
468:     if (!buf) return 0;
469:     if (offset >= max_size) return 0;
470: 
471:     const uint8_t* data = reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(&s) + meta.offset;
472:     switch (meta.type) {
473:         case TYPE_BOOL:
474:             return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%s\n",
475:                    meta.key, *reinterpret_cast<const bool*>(data) ? "true" : "false");
476:         case TYPE_UINT32:
477:             // Handle SpectrumMode enum class (underlying type uint8_t, stored as uint32_t in LUT)
478:             if (strcmp(meta.key, "spectrum_mode") == 0) {
479:                 auto mode = *reinterpret_cast<const SpectrumMode*>(data);
480:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Use PRIu32 macro for platform-independent format specifier
481:                 // uint32_t may be long unsigned int on some platforms, requiring %lu or PRIu32
482:                 return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%" PRIu32 "\n",
483:                        meta.key, static_cast<uint32_t>(mode));
484:             }
485:             return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%" PRIu32 "\n",
486:                    meta.key, *reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(data));
487:         case TYPE_INT32:
488:             return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%" PRId32 "\n",
489:                    meta.key, *reinterpret_cast<const int32_t*>(data));
490:         case TYPE_UINT64:
491:             return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%" PRIu64 "\n",
492:                    meta.key, *reinterpret_cast<const uint64_t*>(data));
493:         case TYPE_STR:
494:             return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%s\n",
495:                    meta.key, reinterpret_cast<const char*>(data));
496:         case TYPE_BITFIELD: {
497:             bool bit_val = (*data >> meta.bit_pos) & 1;
498:             return snprintf(buf + offset, max_size - offset, "%s=%s\n",
499:                    meta.key, bit_val ? "true" : "false");
500:         }
501:     }
502:     return 0;
503: }
504: 
505: // DISPATCH OPERATION ENUM
506: enum class DispatchOp : uint8_t {
507:     PARSE,      ///< Parse string value
508:     RESET,       ///< Reset to default value
509:     VALIDATE    ///< Validate current value
510: };
511: 
512: // DISPATCH BY TYPE HELPER
513: // * * @brief Dispatch setting value based on type and operation * * @param op Operation to perform (PARSE, RESET, VALIDATE) * @param data_ptr Pointer to setting data in DroneAnalyzerSettings struct * @param meta Metadata for setting * @param value_str String value to parse (for PARSE operation) * @return true if operation succeeded, false otherwise * * @note DIAMOND FIX: Uses safe parsing functions with error detection * @note CRITICAL BUG FIX: Replaced unsafe strtoul/strtol with safe_str_to_uint64/safe_str_to_int64 * @note CRITICAL BUG FIX: Replaced insecure strncmp("true", 4) with safe_str_to_bool * @note Handles SpectrumMode enum class (stored as uint8_t underlying type)
514: inline bool dispatch_by_type(DispatchOp op, uint8_t* data_ptr,
515:                           const SettingMetadata& meta, char* value_str = nullptr) noexcept {
516:     switch (meta.type) {
517:         case TYPE_BOOL: {
518:             bool* ptr = reinterpret_cast<bool*>(data_ptr);
519:             bool val;
520: 
521:             if (op == DispatchOp::RESET) {
522:                 val = (strcmp(meta.default_str, "true") == 0);
523:             } else {
524:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Use safe_str_to_bool for exact match
525:                 auto result = safe_str_to_bool(value_str);
526:                 if (result.is_error()) {
527:                     return false;  // Invalid boolean value
528:                 }
529:                 val = result.value;
530:             }
531: 
532:             if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) *ptr = val;
533:             return true;
534:         }
535:         case TYPE_UINT32: {
536:             // Handle SpectrumMode enum class (underlying type uint8_t, stored as uint32_t in LUT)
537:             if (strcmp(meta.key, "spectrum_mode") == 0) {
538:                 SpectrumMode* ptr = reinterpret_cast<SpectrumMode*>(data_ptr);
539:                 uint32_t val;
540: 
541:                 if (op == DispatchOp::RESET) {
542:                     auto result = safe_str_to_uint64(meta.default_str);
543:                     if (result.is_error()) {
544:                         val = static_cast<uint32_t>(SpectrumMode::MEDIUM);
545:                     } else {
546:                         val = static_cast<uint32_t>(result.value);
547:                     }
548:                 } else {
549:                     auto result = safe_str_to_uint64(value_str);
550:                     if (result.is_error()) {
551:                         return false;  // Invalid value
552:                     }
553:                     val = static_cast<uint32_t>(result.value);
554:                 }
555: 
556:                 if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) {
557:                     *ptr = static_cast<SpectrumMode>(val);
558:                 }
559:                 return true;
560:             }
561: 
562:             // Standard uint32_t handling
563:             uint32_t* ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(data_ptr);
564:             uint32_t val;
565: 
566:             if (op == DispatchOp::RESET) {
567:                 auto result = safe_str_to_uint64(meta.default_str);
568:                 if (result.is_error()) {
569:                     val = 0;  // Fallback to 0 on error
570:                 } else {
571:                     val = static_cast<uint32_t>(result.value);
572:                 }
573:             } else {
574:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Use safe_str_to_uint64 with error detection
575:                 auto result = safe_str_to_uint64(value_str);
576:                 if (result.is_error()) {
577:                     return false;  // Invalid value
578:                 }
579:                 val = static_cast<uint32_t>(result.value);
580:             }
581: 
582:             if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) *ptr = val;
583:             return true;
584:         }
585:         case TYPE_INT32: {
586:             int32_t* ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(data_ptr);
587:             int32_t val;
588: 
589:             if (op == DispatchOp::RESET) {
590:                 auto result = safe_str_to_int64(meta.default_str);
591:                 if (result.is_error()) {
592:                     val = 0;  // Fallback to 0 on error
593:                 } else {
594:                     val = static_cast<int32_t>(result.value);
595:                 }
596:             } else {
597:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Use safe_str_to_int64 with error detection
598:                 auto result = safe_str_to_int64(value_str);
599:                 if (result.is_error()) {
600:                     return false;  // Invalid value
601:                 }
602:                 val = static_cast<int32_t>(result.value);
603:             }
604: 
605:             if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) *ptr = val;
606:             return true;
607:         }
608:         case TYPE_UINT64: {
609:             uint64_t* ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint64_t*>(data_ptr);
610:             uint64_t val;
611: 
612:             if (op == DispatchOp::RESET) {
613:                 auto result = safe_str_to_uint64(meta.default_str);
614:                 if (result.is_error()) {
615:                     val = 0;  // Fallback to 0 on error
616:                 } else {
617:                     val = result.value;
618:                 }
619:             } else {
620:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Use safe_str_to_uint64 with error detection
621:                 auto result = safe_str_to_uint64(value_str);
622:                 if (result.is_error()) {
623:                     return false;  // Invalid value
624:                 }
625:                 val = result.value;
626:             }
627: 
628:             if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) *ptr = val;
629:             return true;
630:         }
631:         case TYPE_STR: {
632:             char* ptr = reinterpret_cast<char*>(data_ptr);
633:             const char* val = (op == DispatchOp::RESET) ? meta.default_str : value_str;
634:             if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) safe_strcpy(ptr, val, static_cast<size_t>(meta.min_val));
635:             return true;
636:         }
637:         case TYPE_BITFIELD: {
638:             bool bit_val;
639: 
640:             if (op == DispatchOp::RESET) {
641:                 bit_val = (strcmp(meta.default_str, "true") == 0);
642:             } else {
643:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Use safe_str_to_bool for exact match
644:                 auto result = safe_str_to_bool(value_str);
645:                 if (result.is_error()) {
646:                     return false;  // Invalid boolean value
647:                 }
648:                 bit_val = result.value;
649:             }
650: 
651:             if (op != DispatchOp::VALIDATE) {
652:                 if (bit_val) *data_ptr |= (1 << meta.bit_pos);
653:                 else *data_ptr &= ~(1 << meta.bit_pos);
654:             }
655:             return true;
656:         }
657:     }
658:     return false;
659: }
