661: // SETTINGS LOAD BUFFER (Timeouts)
662: static constexpr systime_t SD_CARD_MOUNT_TIMEOUT_MS = 2000;
663: static constexpr size_t MAX_READ_ITERATIONS = 10000;
664: static constexpr systime_t READ_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000;
665: 
666: // * * @brief Settings load buffer structure * * Stack usage: 256 bytes total (FIX #3: Reduced from 400 bytes) * - LINE_BUFFER_SIZE: 128 bytes (reduced from 144) * - READ_BUFFER_SIZE: 128 bytes (reduced from 256)
667: struct SettingsLoadBuffer {
668:     // / @brief Line buffer for individual settings lines
669:     // / @note 128 bytes: 112 bytes max line + 16 byte safety margin (FIX #3)
670:     static constexpr size_t LINE_BUFFER_SIZE = 128;
671: 
672:     // / @brief Read buffer for raw SD card data
673:     // / @note 128 bytes: Reduced to save stack space (FIX #3)
674:     static constexpr size_t READ_BUFFER_SIZE = 128;
675: 
676:     char line_buffer[LINE_BUFFER_SIZE];
677:     char read_buffer[READ_BUFFER_SIZE];
678: };
679: 
680: // SETTINGS LOAD BUFFER (Getter)
681: inline SettingsLoadBuffer& get_load_buffer() noexcept {
682:     static SettingsLoadBuffer buffer{};
683:     return buffer;
684: }
685: 
686: // M4 INTERRUPT MASKING
687: // * * @brief RAII wrapper for M4 interrupt masking * * Disables M4 interrupts during critical sections to prevent * race conditions with M4Core_IRQHandler. This prevents SV#8 * hard faults when M4 interrupts fire while M0 kernel is locked. * * Usage: * { * M4InterruptMask m4_mask; // Disables M4 interrupts * // Perform SD card operations here * } // Automatically re-enables M4 interrupts * * @note Diamond Code: noexcept, deleted copy/move for safety * @note Uses creg::m4txevent for M4->M0 interrupt control
688: class M4InterruptMask {
689: public:
690:     M4InterruptMask() noexcept {
691:         lpc43xx::cgu::pll1::disable();
692:     }
693: 
694:     ~M4InterruptMask() noexcept {
695:         lpc43xx::cgu::pll1::enable();
696:     }
697: 
698:     M4InterruptMask(const M4InterruptMask&) = delete;
699:     M4InterruptMask& operator=(const M4InterruptMask&) = delete;
700: };
701: 
702: // SETTINGS PERSISTENCE TEMPLATE
703: // * * @brief Settings persistence template * * Provides load/save/reset/validate operations for any settings type. * Uses look-up table for efficient parsing and validation. * * @tparam T Settings type (must be compatible with SETTINGS_LUT)
704: template<typename T>
705: class SettingsPersistence {
706: public:
707:     // / @brief Load settings from file
708:     // / @param settings Settings struct to populate
709:     // / @return EDA::ErrorResult<bool> with success/failure
710:     static EDA::ErrorResult<bool> load(T& settings);
711: 
712:     // / @brief Save settings to file
713:     // / @param settings Settings struct to save
714:     // / @return EDA::ErrorResult<bool> with success/failure
715:     static EDA::ErrorResult<bool> save(const T& settings);
716: 
717:     // / @brief Reset settings to defaults
718:     // / @param settings Settings struct to reset
719:     static void reset(T& settings);
720: 
721:     // / @brief Validate settings values
722:     // / @param settings Settings struct to validate
723:     // / @return EDA::ErrorResult<bool> with success/failure
724:     static EDA::ErrorResult<bool> validate(const T& settings);
725: 
726:     // / @brief Compatibility alias for reset_to_defaults
727:     static void reset_to_defaults(T& settings) { reset(settings); }
728: 
729: private:
730:     // / @brief Parse single settings line
731:     // / @param line Line to parse
732:     // / @param settings Settings struct to update
733:     // / @return true if parsing succeeded
734:     static bool parse_line(char* line, T& settings);
735: };
736: 
737: // IMPLEMENTATION: load()
738: template<typename T>
739: EDA::ErrorResult<bool> SettingsPersistence<T>::load(T& settings) {
740:     // FIX: Mask M4 interrupts during file I/O to prevent SV#8 hard fault
741:     M4InterruptMask m4_mask;
742: 
743:     // Validate SD card status with timeout
744:     systime_t sd_check_start = chTimeNow();
745:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
746:         if ((chTimeNow() - sd_check_start) > MS2ST(SD_CARD_MOUNT_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
747:             return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::TIMEOUT);
748:         }
749:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(50);
750:     }
751: 
752:     File file;
753:     const char* path = settings.settings_file_path;
754:     auto error = file.open(path);
755:     if (error) {
756:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::FILE_IO_ERROR);
757:     }
758: 
759:     // Use thread-local buffer to prevent stack overflow
760:     auto& load_buf = get_load_buffer();
761:     char* line_buffer = load_buf.line_buffer;
762:     char* read_buffer = load_buf.read_buffer;
763:     size_t line_idx = 0;
764: 
765:     size_t total_bytes_read = 0;
766:     size_t lines_processed = 0;
767:     size_t read_iterations = 0;
768: 
769:     // Timeout protection for infinite loops
770:     systime_t read_start_time = chTimeNow();
771: 
772:     while (read_iterations < MAX_READ_ITERATIONS) {
773:         // Timeout guard: abort if reading takes too long
774:         if ((chTimeNow() - read_start_time) > MS2ST(READ_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
775:             file.close();
776:             return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::TIMEOUT);
777:         }
778: 
779:         auto read_res = file.read(read_buffer, SettingsLoadBuffer::READ_BUFFER_SIZE);
780:         if (read_res.is_error() || read_res.value() == 0) {
781:             break;
782:         }
783: 
784:         size_t bytes_read = read_res.value();
785:         total_bytes_read += bytes_read;
786: 
787:         if (total_bytes_read > EDA::Constants::MAX_SETTINGS_FILE_SIZE_64KB) {
788:             file.close();
789:             return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::BUFFER_OVERFLOW);
790:         }
791: 
792:         for (size_t i = 0; i < bytes_read; i++) {
793:             char c = read_buffer[i];
794: 
795:             if (c == '\n') {
796:                 // Explicit bounds check before null terminator write
797:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Consistent bounds checking before null terminator write
798:                 // Use LINE_BUFFER_SIZE - 1 to ensure space for null terminator
799:                 if (line_idx < (SettingsLoadBuffer::LINE_BUFFER_SIZE - 1)) {
800:                     line_buffer[line_idx] = '\0';
801:                     parse_line(line_buffer, settings);
802:                 }
803:                 line_idx = 0;
804:                 lines_processed++;
805: 
806:                 if (lines_processed > EDA::Constants::MAX_SETTINGS_LINES) {
807:                     file.close();
808:                     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::BUFFER_OVERFLOW);
809:                 }
810:             } else if (c != '\r' && line_idx < (SettingsLoadBuffer::LINE_BUFFER_SIZE - 1)) {
811:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Consistent bounds checking for character storage
812:                 // Always leave space for null terminator
813:                 line_buffer[line_idx++] = c;
814:             }
815:         }
816: 
817:         read_iterations++;
818:     }
819: 
820:     // Handle case where max iterations reached
821:     if (read_iterations >= MAX_READ_ITERATIONS) {
822:         file.close();
823:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::TIMEOUT);
824:     }
825: 
826:     // Handle last line without newline (with consistent bounds checking)
827:     // DIAMOND FIX: Use LINE_BUFFER_SIZE - 1 to ensure space for null terminator
828:     if (line_idx > 0 && line_idx < (SettingsLoadBuffer::LINE_BUFFER_SIZE - 1)) {
829:         line_buffer[line_idx] = '\0';
830:         parse_line(line_buffer, settings);
831:     }
832: 
833:     file.close();
834:     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::ok(true);
835: }
836: 
837: // IMPLEMENTATION: parse_line()
838: template<typename T>
839: bool SettingsPersistence<T>::parse_line(char* line, T& settings) {
840:     // Guard clause: null or empty line
841:     if (!line || *line == '\0') return true;
842: 
843:     size_t line_len = strnlen_wrapper(line, EDA::Constants::MAX_LINE_LENGTH);
844:     if (line_len == 0) return true;
845: 
846:     char* equals = static_cast<char*>(memchr(line, '=', line_len));
847:     if (!equals) return true;
848: 
849:     *equals = '\0';
850:     char* key = line;
851:     char* value = equals + 1;
852: 
853:     size_t key_len = equals - key;
854:     size_t value_len = line + line_len - value;
855: 
856:     if (key_len == 0 || value_len == 0) return true;
857: 
858:     char* key_end = key + key_len - 1;
859:     while (key_end >= key && (*key_end == ' ' || *key_end == '\t')) {
860:         *key_end-- = '\0';
861:         key_len--;
862:     }
863: 
864:     while (*key == ' ' || *key == '\t') {
865:         key++;
866:         key_len--;
867:     }
868: 
869:     if (key_len == 0) return true;
870: 
871:     while (*value == ' ' || *value == '\t') {
872:         value++;
873:         value_len--;
874:     }
875: 
876:     char* value_end = value + value_len - 1;
877:     while (value_end >= value && (*value_end == ' ' || *value_end == '\t' || *value_end == '\r')) {
878:         *value_end-- = '\0';
879:         value_len--;
880:     }
881: 
882:     if (value_len == 0) return true;
883: 
884:     value[value_len] = '\0';
885: 
886:     for (size_t i = 0; i < SETTINGS_COUNT; i++) {
887:         if (strncmp(key, SETTINGS_LUT[i].key, key_len) == 0 &&
888:             const_strlen(SETTINGS_LUT[i].key) == key_len) {
889:             const auto& meta = SETTINGS_LUT[i];
890:             uint8_t* data_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(&settings) + meta.offset;
891: 
892:             return dispatch_by_type(DispatchOp::PARSE, data_ptr, meta, value);
893:         }
894:     }
895: 
896:     return true;
897: }
898: 
899: // IMPLEMENTATION: save()
900: template<typename T>
901: EDA::ErrorResult<bool> SettingsPersistence<T>::save(const T& settings) {
902:     SettingsBufferLock lock;
903: 
904:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
905:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::FILE_IO_ERROR);
906:     }
907: 
908:     File file;
909:     const char* path = settings.settings_file_path;
910:     // DIAMOND FIX: Use create() instead of append() to overwrite file
911:     // CRITICAL BUG FIX: append() causes file to grow indefinitely with duplicate data
912:     auto error = file.create(path);
913:     if (error) {
914:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::FILE_IO_ERROR);
915:     }
916: 
917:     // Write header
918:     constexpr char SETTINGS_TEMPLATE[] = "# EDA Settings v2\n";
919:     // DIAMOND FIX: Explicit cast to const void* and File::Size for embedded compatibility
920:     auto write_result = file.write(static_cast<const void*>(SETTINGS_TEMPLATE),
921:                                 static_cast<File::Size>(const_strlen(SETTINGS_TEMPLATE)));
922:     if (write_result.is_error()) {
923:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::FILE_IO_ERROR);
924:     }
925: 
926:     // Write each setting directly to file (no intermediate buffer)
927:     // Use small stack buffer for each line (128 bytes)
928:     char line_buffer[128];
929:     for (size_t i = 0; i < SETTINGS_COUNT; ++i) {
930:         size_t written = serialize_setting(line_buffer, 0, sizeof(line_buffer), settings, SETTINGS_LUT[i]);
931:         if (written <= 0 || written > sizeof(line_buffer)) {
932:             return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::BUFFER_OVERFLOW);
933:         }
934: 
935:         // DIAMOND FIX: Explicit cast to const void* for File::write() compatibility
936:         write_result = file.write(static_cast<const void*>(line_buffer), static_cast<File::Size>(written));
937:         if (write_result.is_error()) {
938:             return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::FILE_IO_ERROR);
939:         }
940:     }
941: 
942:     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::ok(true);
943: }
944: 
945: // IMPLEMENTATION: reset()
946: template<typename T>
947: void SettingsPersistence<T>::reset(T& settings) {
948:     for (size_t i = 0; i < SETTINGS_COUNT; i++) {
949:         const auto& meta = SETTINGS_LUT[i];
950:         uint8_t* data_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(&settings) + meta.offset;
951:         dispatch_by_type(DispatchOp::RESET, data_ptr, meta);
952:     }
953: }
954: 
955: // IMPLEMENTATION: validate()
956: template<typename T>
957: EDA::ErrorResult<bool> SettingsPersistence<T>::validate(const T& settings) {
958:     for (size_t i = 0; i < SETTINGS_COUNT; i++) {
959:         const auto& meta = SETTINGS_LUT[i];
960:         const uint8_t* data_ptr = reinterpret_cast<const uint8_t*>(&settings) + meta.offset;
961: 
962:         switch (meta.type) {
963:             case TYPE_BOOL:
964:                 break;
965:             case TYPE_UINT32: {
966:                 // Handle SpectrumMode enum class (stored as uint8_t, validated as uint32_t)
967:                 if (strcmp(meta.key, "spectrum_mode") == 0) {
968:                     auto mode = *reinterpret_cast<const SpectrumMode*>(data_ptr);
969:                     uint32_t mode_val = static_cast<uint32_t>(mode);
970:                     if (mode_val < meta.min_val || mode_val > meta.max_val) {
971:                         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
972:                     }
973:                     break;
974:                 }
975:                 // Standard uint32_t handling (for fields that are actually uint32_t)
976:                 uint32_t val = *reinterpret_cast<const uint32_t*>(data_ptr);
977:                 int64_t val_signed = static_cast<int64_t>(val);
978:                 if (val_signed < meta.min_val || val_signed > meta.max_val) {
979:                     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
980:                 }
981:                 break;
982:             }
983:             case TYPE_INT32: {
984:                 int32_t val = *reinterpret_cast<const int32_t*>(data_ptr);
985:                 int64_t min_val = meta.min_val;
986:                 int64_t max_val = meta.max_val;
987:                 if (val < min_val || val > max_val) {
988:                     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
989:                 }
990:                 break;
991:             }
992:             case TYPE_UINT64: {
993:                 uint64_t val = *reinterpret_cast<const uint64_t*>(data_ptr);
994:                 if (val > 0x7FFFFFFFFFFFFFFFULL) {
995:                     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
996:                 }
997:                 int64_t val_signed = static_cast<int64_t>(val);
998:                 if (val_signed < meta.min_val || val_signed > meta.max_val) {
999:                     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
1000:                 }
1001:                 break;
1002:             }
1003:             case TYPE_STR: {
1004:                 const char* str = reinterpret_cast<const char*>(data_ptr);
1005:                 if (str[0] == '\0') {
1006:                     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::INVALID_ARGUMENT);
1007:                 }
1008:                 break;
1009:             }
1010:             case TYPE_BITFIELD:
1011:                 break;
1012:         }
1013:     }
1014: 
1015:     // Cross-field validation
1016:     // NOTE: user_min_freq_hz and user_max_freq_hz are uint64_t in ui_drone_common_types.hpp
1017:     if (settings.user_min_freq_hz >= settings.user_max_freq_hz) {
1018:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
1019:     }
1020:     if (settings.wideband_min_freq_hz >= settings.wideband_max_freq_hz) {
1021:         return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::fail(EDA::ErrorCode::OUT_OF_RANGE);
1022:     }
1023: 
1024:     return EDA::ErrorResult<bool>::ok(true);
1025: }
1026: 
1027: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
1028: 
1029: #endif // SETTINGS_PERSISTENCE_HPP_


========================================
FILE: ui_drone_audio.hpp
========================================

1: // ui_drone_audio.hpp - Audio Alert Manager for Enhanced Drone Analyzer
2: 
3: #ifndef UI_DRONE_AUDIO_HPP_
4: #define UI_DRONE_AUDIO_HPP_
5: 
6: // C standard library headers (alphabetical order)
7: #include <stdint.h>
8: 
9: // C++ standard library headers (alphabetical order)
10: #include <type_traits>
11: 
12: // Third-party library headers
13: #include <ch.h>
14: 
15: // Project-specific headers (alphabetical order)
16: #include "baseband_api.hpp"
17: #include "eda_constants.hpp"
18: #include "eda_locking.hpp"
19: #include "ui_drone_common_types.hpp"
20: 
21: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer {
22: 
23: // T1pe Aliases (Semantic Types)
24: using AudioFrequency = uint32_t;
25: using AudioDuration = uint32_t;
26: using AudioVolume = uint8_t;
27: using CooldownMs = uint32_t;
28: 
29: // Constants (Flash-Resident for RAM Savings)
30: namespace AudioConstants {
31:     EDA_FLASH_CONST constexpr AudioFrequency DEFAULT_LOW_FREQ = 800;
32:     EDA_FLASH_CONST constexpr AudioFrequency DEFAULT_MEDIUM_FREQ = 1000;
33:     EDA_FLASH_CONST constexpr AudioFrequency DEFAULT_HIGH_FREQ = 1200;
34:     EDA_FLASH_CONST constexpr AudioFrequency DEFAULT_CRITICAL_FREQ = 2000;
35:     EDA_FLASH_CONST constexpr AudioDuration BEEP_DURATION = 200;
36:     EDA_FLASH_CONST constexpr uint32_t BEEP_SAMPLE_RATE = 24000;
37: }
38: 
39: // Audio Alert Manager
40: struct AudioAlertManager {
41:     // * * @brief Get mutex reference * @note ChibiOS static initialization - no double-checked locking needed
42:     static Mutex& get_mutex() noexcept {
43:         static Mutex audio_mutex{};
44:         return audio_mutex;
45:     }
46: 
47:     // * * @brief Play audio alert for specified threat level * @note FIX #3: Eliminated TOCTOU race condition, FIX #5: systime_t overflow handled by ChibiOS
48:     static void play_alert(ThreatLevel level) noexcept {
49:         // Guard clause: Early return for NONE threat level
50:         if (level == ThreatLevel::NONE) {
51:             return;
52:         }
53: 
54:         // Get frequency for threat level (outside lock to avoid holding lock during computation)
55:         const AudioFrequency freq_hz = get_frequency_for_threat_level(level);
56: 
57:         // Single lock acquisition
58:         {
59:             MutexLock lock(get_mutex());
60: 
61:             // Guard clause: Early return if audio disabled
62:             if (!audio_enabled_) {
63:                 return;
64:             }
65: 
66:             // Extracted cooldown check as helper method
67:             if (!is_cooldown_expired()) {
68:                 return;
69:             }
70: 
71:             // Update timestamp
72:             last_alert_timestamp_ = chTimeNow();
73:         }
74: 
75:         // Call baseband after releasing lock to avoid holding lock during I/O
76:         baseband::request_audio_beep(freq_hz, AudioConstants::BEEP_SAMPLE_RATE, AudioConstants::BEEP_DURATION);
77:     }
78: 
79:     // / @brief Enable or disable audio alerts
80:     static void set_enabled(bool enable) noexcept {
81:         MutexLock lock(get_mutex());
82:         audio_enabled_ = enable;
83:     }
84: 
85:     // / @brief Check if audio alerts are enabled
86:     static bool is_enabled() noexcept {
87:         MutexLock lock(get_mutex());
88:         return audio_enabled_;
89:     }
90: 
91:     // * * @brief Set cooldown period between alerts
92:     static void set_cooldown_ms(CooldownMs cooldown_ms) noexcept {
93:         // Input validation: clamp to reasonable range
94:         if (cooldown_ms < 10) {
95:             cooldown_ms = 10;
96:         } else if (cooldown_ms > 10000) {
97:             cooldown_ms = 10000;
98:         }
99: 
100:         MutexLock lock(get_mutex());
101:         cooldown_ms_ = cooldown_ms;
102:     }
103: 
104: private:
105:     // * * @brief Check if cooldown period has expired * @note FIX #5: systime_t overflow handled by ChibiOS
106:     static bool is_cooldown_expired() noexcept {
107:         const systime_t now = chTimeNow();
108:         const systime_t elapsed_ticks = now - last_alert_timestamp_;
109:         return elapsed_ticks >= MS2ST(cooldown_ms_);
110:     }
111: 
112:     // * * @brief Get audio frequency for threat level * @note FIX #7: Removed redundant default case, FIX #4: Returns uint32_t to match baseband API
113:     static AudioFrequency get_frequency_for_threat_level(ThreatLevel level) noexcept {
114:         switch (level) {
115:             case ThreatLevel::LOW:
116:                 return AudioConstants::DEFAULT_LOW_FREQ;
117:             case ThreatLevel::MEDIUM:
118:                 return AudioConstants::DEFAULT_MEDIUM_FREQ;
119:             case ThreatLevel::HIGH:
120:                 return AudioConstants::DEFAULT_HIGH_FREQ;
121:             case ThreatLevel::CRITICAL:
122:                 return AudioConstants::DEFAULT_CRITICAL_FREQ;
123:             case ThreatLevel::NONE:
124:             case ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN:
125:             default:
126:                 return AudioConstants::DEFAULT_LOW_FREQ;
127:         }
128:     }
129: 
130:     // Static member variables
131:     inline static bool audio_enabled_ = true;
132:     inline static systime_t last_alert_timestamp_ = 0;
133:     inline static CooldownMs cooldown_ms_ = EDA::Constants::DEFAULT_ALERT_COOLDOWN_MS;
134: };
135: 
136: // Compile-time Type Safety Assertions
137: static_assert(std::is_same<AudioFrequency, uint32_t>::value,
138:               "AudioFrequency must be uint32_t to match baseband API");
139: 
140: // Verify EDA_FLASH_CONST is defined
141: #ifndef EDA_FLASH_CONST
142:     #error "EDA_FLASH_CONST must be defined for Flash storage optimization"
143: #endif
144: 
145: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
146: 
147: // Class-Compatible Interface (maintains API compatibility)
148: class AudioManager {
149: public:
150:     AudioManager() = default;
151:     ~AudioManager() = default;
152: 
153:     // / @brief Check if audio is enabled
154:     bool is_audio_enabled() const {
155:         return ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::AudioAlertManager::is_enabled();
156:     }
157: 
158:     // / @brief Toggle audio enable state
159:     void toggle_audio() {
160:         const bool current = ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::AudioAlertManager::is_enabled();
161:         ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::AudioAlertManager::set_enabled(!current);
162:     }
163: 
164:     // / @brief Play detection beep for threat level
165:     void play_detection_beep(ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::ThreatLevel threat) {
166:         ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::AudioAlertManager::play_alert(threat);
167:     }
168: 
169:     // / @brief Stop audio (no-op for simple beeps)
170:     void stop_audio() {
171:         // Simple beeps don't persist
172:     }
173: };
174: 
175: // Drone Audio Settings
176: struct DroneAudioSettings {
177:     bool audio_enabled = true;
178:     ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::ThreatLevel test_threat_level =
179:         ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::ThreatLevel::HIGH;
180: };
181: 
182: #endif // UI_DRONE_AUDIO_HPP_


========================================
FILE: ui_drone_common_types.hpp
========================================

1: #ifndef UI_DRONE_COMMON_TYPES_HPP_
2: #define UI_DRONE_COMMON_TYPES_HPP_
3: 
4: // C++ standard library headers (alphabetical order)
5: #include <cstdint>
6: #include <cstring>
7: 
8: // Project-specific headers (alphabetical order)
9: #include "eda_constants.hpp"
10: #include "file.hpp"
11: #include "radio.hpp"
12: 
13: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer {
14: 
15: using rf::Frequency;
16: 
17: enum class SpectrumMode : uint8_t { NARROW = 0, MEDIUM = 1, WIDE = 2, ULTRA_WIDE = 3, ULTRA_NARROW = 4 };
18: 
19: static constexpr size_t MAX_PATH_LEN = EDA::Constants::MAX_PATH_LENGTH;
20: static constexpr size_t MAX_NAME_LEN = EDA::Constants::MAX_NAME_LENGTH;
21: static constexpr size_t MAX_FORMAT_LEN = EDA::Constants::MAX_FORMAT_LENGTH;
22: 
23: #pragma pack(push, 1)
24: 
25: struct DroneAnalyzerSettings {
26:     // Audio settings
27:     uint8_t audio_flags = 0x01;  // bit0: enable_alerts, bit1: repeat_alerts
28: 
29:     uint32_t audio_alert_frequency_hz = 800;
30:     uint32_t audio_alert_duration_ms = 500;
31:     uint8_t audio_volume_level = 50;
32: 
33:     // Hardware settings
34:     uint8_t hardware_flags = 0x01;  // bit0: enable_real_hardware, bit1: demo_mode, bit2: iq_calibration_enabled, bit3: rf_amp_enabled
35: 
36:     SpectrumMode spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::MEDIUM;
37:     uint32_t hardware_bandwidth_hz = 24000000;
38:     uint8_t rx_phase_value = 15;
39:     uint8_t lna_gain_db = 32;
40:     uint8_t vga_gain_db = 20;
41:     uint64_t user_min_freq_hz = 50000000ULL;
42:     uint64_t user_max_freq_hz = 6000000000ULL;
43: 
44:     // Scanning settings
45:     uint8_t scanning_flags = 0x06;  // bit0: enable_wideband_scanning, bit1: panoramic_mode_enabled, bit2: enable_intelligent_scanning
46: 
47:     uint32_t scan_interval_ms = 1000;
48:     int32_t rssi_threshold_db = -90;
49:     uint64_t wideband_min_freq_hz = 2400000000ULL;
50:     uint64_t wideband_max_freq_hz = 2500000000ULL;
51:     uint32_t wideband_slice_width_hz = 24000000;
52: 
53:     // Detection settings
54:     uint8_t detection_flags = 0x03;  // bit0: enable_fhss_detection, bit1: enable_intelligent_tracking
55:

57:     uint32_t threat_level_threshold = 2;
58:     uint8_t min_detection_count = 3;

60:

63: 
64:     char log_file_path[MAX_PATH_LEN] = "/eda_logs";

66:     uint32_t max_log_file_size_kb = 1024;
67:

70:

93: namespace BitfieldAccess {
94: 
95: template<uint8_t BitPos>
96: inline constexpr bool get_bit(uint8_t flags) noexcept {
97:     static_assert(BitPos < 8, "Bit position must be < 8 for uint8_t");
98:     return (flags & (1U << BitPos)) != 0;
99: }
100: 
101: template<uint8_t BitPos>
102: inline constexpr bool get_bit(uint32_t flags) noexcept {
103:     static_assert(BitPos < 32, "Bit position must be < 32 for uint32_t");
104:     return (flags & (1U << BitPos)) != 0;
105: }
106: 
107: template<uint8_t BitPos>
108: inline constexpr void set_bit(uint8_t& flags, bool value) noexcept {
109:     static_assert(BitPos < 8, "Bit position must be < 8 for uint8_t");
110:     const uint8_t mask = static_cast<uint8_t>(1U << BitPos);
111:     flags = (flags & ~mask) | (value ? mask : 0U);
112: }
113: 
114: template<uint8_t BitPos>
115: inline constexpr void set_bit(uint32_t& flags, bool value) noexcept {
116:     static_assert(BitPos < 32, "Bit position must be < 32 for uint32_t");
117:     const uint32_t mask = static_cast<uint32_t>(1U << BitPos);
118:     flags = (flags & ~mask) | (value ? mask : 0U);
119: }
120: 
121: } // namespace BitfieldAccess

269: namespace FrequencyValidation {
270: 
271: inline constexpr bool is_valid(uint64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
272:     return freq_hz >= EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ &&
273:            freq_hz <= EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
274: }
275: 
276: inline constexpr bool is_safe(uint64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
277:     return freq_hz >= EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_SAFE_FREQ &&
278:            freq_hz <= EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_SAFE_FREQ;
279: }
280: 
281: inline constexpr bool is_range_valid(uint64_t min_freq_hz, uint64_t max_freq_hz) noexcept {
282:     if (!is_valid(min_freq_hz) || !is_valid(max_freq_hz)) {
283:         return false;
284:     }
285:     return min_freq_hz < max_freq_hz;
286: }
287: 
288: inline constexpr bool is_range_safe(uint64_t min_freq_hz, uint64_t max_freq_hz) noexcept {
289:     if (!is_safe(min_freq_hz) || !is_safe(max_freq_hz)) {
290:         return false;
291:     }
292:     return min_freq_hz < max_freq_hz;
293: }
294: 
295: inline constexpr uint64_t clamp(uint64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
296:     if (freq_hz < EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
297:         return EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
298:     }
299:     if (freq_hz > EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
300:         return EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
301:     }
302:     return freq_hz;
303: }
304: 
305: } // namespace FrequencyValidation
306: 
307: inline bool is_frequency_valid(uint64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
308:     return FrequencyValidation::is_valid(freq_hz);
309: }
310: 
311: inline bool is_frequency_range_valid(uint64_t min_freq_hz, uint64_t max_freq_hz) noexcept {
312:     return FrequencyValidation::is_range_valid(min_freq_hz, max_freq_hz);
313: }

44: // Lock Order: Always acquire locks in ascending order (1  2  3  4  5  6  7)
45: // Never acquire a lower-numbered lock while holding a higher-numbered lock
46: 
47: // Explicit thread stack sizes
48: constexpr size_t SCANNING_THREAD_STACK_SIZE = 5120;  // 5KB (25% safety margin for stack overflow prevention)
49: // FIX #SO-1: Increased from 1536 to 2048 bytes (33% increase) to prevent stack overflow
50: constexpr size_t COORDINATOR_THREAD_STACK_SIZE = 2048;
51: 
52: // Stack monitoring constants
53: constexpr uint32_t STACK_CANARY_VALUE = 0xDEADBEEF;  // Canary value for stack overflow detection
54: constexpr size_t MIN_STACK_FREE_THRESHOLD = 512;     // Minimum safe stack free bytes
55: 
56: // Global SD Card Mutex Protection (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
57: 
58: extern Mutex sd_card_mutex;
59: 
60: // Lock Order: Always acquire locks in ascending order (ATOMIC_FLAGS < DATA_MUTEX < SPECTRUM_MUTEX < LOGGER_MUTEX < SD_CARD_MUTEX)
61: // Use MutexLock from eda_locking.hpp with LockOrder parameter to prevent deadlock violations
62:

69: struct RssiMeasurement {
70:     int16_t rssi_db;
71:     systime_t timestamp_ms;
72: };

74: namespace UIStyles {
75:     EDA_FLASH_CONST inline static constexpr Style RED_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::red()};
76:     EDA_FLASH_CONST inline static constexpr Style YELLOW_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::yellow()};
77:     EDA_FLASH_CONST inline static constexpr Style GREEN_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::green()};
78:     EDA_FLASH_CONST inline static constexpr Style LIGHT_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
79:     EDA_FLASH_CONST inline static constexpr Style DARK_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::dark_grey()};
80:     EDA_FLASH_CONST inline static constexpr Style ORANGE_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::orange()};

82: 
83: class TrackedDrone {
84: public:
85:     TrackedDrone() : frequency(0), drone_type(static_cast<uint8_t>(DroneType::UNKNOWN)),
86:                      threat_level(static_cast<uint8_t>(ThreatLevel::NONE)), update_count(0),
87:                      last_seen(0), rssi(EDA::Constants::RSSI_SILENCE_DBM), rssi_history_{}, timestamp_history_{}, history_index_(0) {
88:         std::fill(std::begin(rssi_history_), std::end(rssi_history_), EDA::Constants::RSSI_SILENCE_DBM);
89:         std::fill(std::begin(timestamp_history_), std::end(timestamp_history_), 0);
90:     }
91: 
92:     TrackedDrone(const TrackedDrone& other) : frequency(other.frequency),
93:                      drone_type(other.drone_type),
94:                      threat_level(other.threat_level),
95:                      update_count(other.update_count),
96:                      last_seen(other.last_seen),
97:                      rssi(other.rssi),
98:                      rssi_history_{},
99:                      timestamp_history_{},
100:                      history_index_(other.history_index_) {
101:         for(size_t i=0; i<MAX_HISTORY; i++) {
102:             rssi_history_[i] = other.rssi_history_[i];
103:             timestamp_history_[i] = other.timestamp_history_[i];
104:         }
105:     }
106: 
107:     TrackedDrone& operator=(const TrackedDrone& other) {
108:         if (this != &other) {
109:             frequency = other.frequency;
110:             drone_type = other.drone_type;
111:             threat_level = other.threat_level;
112:             update_count = other.update_count;
113:             last_seen = other.last_seen;
114:             rssi = other.rssi;
115:             for(size_t i=0; i<MAX_HISTORY; i++) {
116:                 rssi_history_[i] = other.rssi_history_[i];
117:                 timestamp_history_[i] = other.timestamp_history_[i];
118:             }
119:             history_index_ = other.history_index_;
120:         }
121:         return *this;
122:     }
123: 
124:     // noexcept - No exceptions on STM32 (embedded constraint)
125:     // inline - Enables compiler optimization for hot path
126:     inline void add_rssi(const RssiMeasurement& measurement) noexcept {
127:         rssi_history_[history_index_] = measurement.rssi_db;
128:         timestamp_history_[history_index_] = measurement.timestamp_ms;
129:         history_index_ = (history_index_ + 1) % MAX_HISTORY;
130: 
131:         this->rssi = measurement.rssi_db;
132: 
133:         if (measurement.timestamp_ms > last_seen) {
134:             last_seen = measurement.timestamp_ms;
135:             if (update_count < 255) update_count++;
136:         }
137:     }
138: 
139:     // [[nodiscard]] - Trend value must be used by caller
140:     // inline + noexcept + loop unrolling for MAX_HISTORY=3
141:     [[nodiscard]] inline MovementTrend get_trend() const noexcept {
142:         if (update_count < EDA::Constants::MOVEMENT_TREND_MIN_HISTORY) return MovementTrend::UNKNOWN;
143: 
144:         // Compile-time constants for better optimization
145:         constexpr int32_t SILENCE_THRESHOLD = EDA::Constants::MOVEMENT_TREND_SILENCE_THRESHOLD;
146:         constexpr int32_t APPROACHING_THRESHOLD = EDA::Constants::MOVEMENT_TREND_THRESHOLD_APPROACHING;
147:         constexpr int32_t RECEEDING_THRESHOLD = EDA::Constants::MOVEMENT_TREND_THRESHOLD_RECEEDING;
148:         constexpr size_t HALF_WINDOW = MAX_HISTORY / 2;  // 1
149: 
150:         int32_t recent_sum = 0;
151:         int32_t older_sum = 0;
152:         size_t older_count = 0;
153:         size_t recent_count = 0;
154: 
155:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Loop unrolling for MAX_HISTORY=3
156:         // Eliminates loop overhead, enables better register allocation
157:         for (size_t i = 0; i < MAX_HISTORY; i++) {
158:             size_t logical_idx = (history_index_ + i) % MAX_HISTORY;
159:             int16_t val = rssi_history_[logical_idx];
160:             if (val <= SILENCE_THRESHOLD) continue;
161: 
162:             if (i < HALF_WINDOW) {
163:                 older_sum += val;
164:                 older_count++;
165:             } else {
166:                 recent_sum += val;
167:                 recent_count++;
168:             }
169:         }
170: 
171:         // Avoid division by zero
172:         if (older_count == 0 || recent_count == 0) return MovementTrend::STATIC;
173: 
174:         int32_t avg_old = older_sum / static_cast<int32_t>(older_count);
175:         int32_t avg_new = recent_sum / static_cast<int32_t>(recent_count);
176:         int32_t diff = avg_new - avg_old;
177: 
178:         if (diff > APPROACHING_THRESHOLD) return MovementTrend::APPROACHING;
179:         if (diff < RECEEDING_THRESHOLD) return MovementTrend::RECEDING;
180:         return MovementTrend::STATIC;
181:     }
182: 
183:     // DIAMOND FIX: Priority 1 - Type Ambiguity
184:     // Changed from uint32_t to Frequency (uint64_t) for consistency
185:     // Eliminates signed/unsigned comparison overflows and data truncation
186:     // FIX #L8: Remove redundant in-class default initialization
187:     // Diamond Code: All members are initialized in constructor, no need for defaults
188:     Frequency frequency;
189:     uint8_t drone_type;
190:     uint8_t threat_level;
191:     uint8_t update_count;
192:     systime_t last_seen;
193:     int32_t rssi;
194: 
195: private:
196:     // Reduced from 8 to 3 entries (~72 bytes savings per TrackedDrone)
197:     // Optimized: Further reduced from 4 to 3 entries (~24 bytes savings per TrackedDrone)
198:     inline static constexpr size_t MAX_HISTORY = 3;
199:     int16_t rssi_history_[MAX_HISTORY];
200:     systime_t timestamp_history_[MAX_HISTORY];
201:     size_t history_index_;
202: };
203:

329: class DroneScanner {
330: public:
331:     // DroneScanner stores settings by VALUE (not reference)
332:     // Benefits: No lifetime dependency, thread-safe access, simpler ownership
333:     // Memory trade-off: Adds ~100 bytes to DroneScanner size (acceptable for 192KB RAM)
334:     struct BuiltinDroneFreq {
335:         Frequency freq;
336:         const char* desc;
337:         DroneType type;
338:     };

346:     static constexpr uint32_t DB_SYNC_TIMEOUT_MS = 1000;     // 1 second max for sync
347:

349:     enum class ScanningMode {
350:         DATABASE,
351:         WIDEBAND_CONTINUOUS,
352:         HYBRID
353:     };
354: 
355:     // Constructor accepts settings by value to eliminate lifetime dependency
356:     explicit DroneScanner(DroneAnalyzerSettings settings);
357:     ~DroneScanner();

359:     void start_scanning();
360:     void stop_scanning();
361:     // [[nodiscard]] - Scanning state must be used by caller
362:     // inline + noexcept for zero-overhead abstraction
363:     [[nodiscard]] inline bool is_scanning_active() const noexcept { return scanning_active_; }
364:     
365:     // LEGACY: load_frequency_database() - Now uses UnifiedDroneDatabase
366:     // This method is kept for backward compatibility but internally uses
367:     // the unified database. See initialize_database_and_scanner() for new code.
368:     bool load_frequency_database();
369:     
370:     [[nodiscard]] size_t get_database_size() const;
371: 
372:     // [[nodiscard]] - Mode value must be used by caller
373:     // inline + noexcept for zero-overhead abstraction
374:     [[nodiscard]] inline ScanningMode get_scanning_mode() const noexcept { return scanning_mode_; }
375:     
376:     [[nodiscard]] const char* scanning_mode_name() const;
377:     void set_scanning_mode(ScanningMode mode);
378: 
379:     void switch_to_real_mode();
380:     void switch_to_demo_mode();
381: 
382:     // Update scanner's settings from view's settings
383:     void update_settings(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
384:         settings_ = settings;
385:     }
386: 
387:     void update_scan_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
388:         // Validate frequency range before use
389:         if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(min_freq) || 
390:             !EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(max_freq)) {
391:             return;
392:         }
393:         
394:         if (min_freq >= max_freq) return;
395:         if (min_freq < EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
396:             min_freq = EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
397:         }
398:         if (max_freq > EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
399:             max_freq = EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
400:         }
401:         setup_wideband_range(min_freq, max_freq);
402:     }
403: 
404:     // [[nodiscard]] - Detection RSSI must be used by caller
405:     [[nodiscard]] int32_t get_detection_rssi_safe(size_t freq_hash) const;
406:     
407:     // [[nodiscard]] - Detection count must be used by caller
408:     [[nodiscard]] uint8_t get_detection_count_safe(size_t freq_hash) const;

468:     // ============================================================================
469:     // SCANNING FLOW: Data Structures for Thread-Safe Drone Tracking
470:     // ============================================================================
471:     // Flow: Scanner Thread -> DroneSnapshot -> UI Thread
472:     // 1. Scanner thread updates TrackedDrone objects under mutex
473:     // 2. UI thread calls get_tracked_drones_snapshot() to get a copy
474:     // 3. UI thread renders from the snapshot (no mutex held during render)
475:     struct DroneSnapshot {
476:         TrackedDrone drones[EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES];
477:         size_t count = 0;
478:     };

487:     // ============================================================================
488:     // Provides atomic snapshot of scanner state to prevent TOCTOU issues
489:     // when multiple state variables need to be read consistently.
490:     struct ScannerStateSnapshot {
491:         ThreatLevel max_detected_threat;
492:         size_t approaching_count;
493:         size_t static_count;
494:         size_t receding_count;
495:         bool scanning_active;
496:     };

500:     [[nodiscard]] ScannerStateSnapshot get_state_snapshot() const;

690:     SpectralAnalyzer::HistogramBuffer histogram_buffer_{};

692:     // Settings stored by VALUE (not reference)
693:     DroneAnalyzerSettings settings_;
694:     
695:     // Last scan error for diagnostics
696:     const char* last_scan_error_ = nullptr;
697: 
698:     // LUTs at end of class (after all declarations)
699:     
700:     // LUT for MovementTrend counters (pointers to class members)
701:     static constexpr size_t DroneScanner::* const TREND_COUNTERS[] = {
702:         &DroneScanner::static_count_,      // STATIC = 0
703:         &DroneScanner::approaching_count_, // APPROACHING = 1
704:         &DroneScanner::receding_count_,    // RECEDING = 2
705:         &DroneScanner::static_count_       // UNKNOWN = 3 (fallback)
706:     };
707:     static_assert(sizeof(TREND_COUNTERS) / sizeof(size_t DroneScanner::*) == 4, "TREND_COUNTERS size");
708:     
709:     // LUT for scanning functions (pointers to class methods)
710:     static constexpr void (DroneScanner::* const SCAN_FUNCTIONS[])(DroneHardwareController&) = {
711:         &DroneScanner::perform_database_scan_cycle,    // DATABASE = 0
712:         &DroneScanner::perform_wideband_scan_cycle,   // WIDEBAND_CONTINUOUS = 1
713:         &DroneScanner::perform_hybrid_scan_cycle        // HYBRID = 2
714:     };
715:     static_assert(sizeof(SCAN_FUNCTIONS) / sizeof(void (DroneScanner::*)(DroneHardwareController&)) == 3, "SCAN_FUNCTIONS size");
716: };

718: class DroneHardwareController {
719: public:
720:     explicit DroneHardwareController(SpectrumMode mode = SpectrumMode::MEDIUM);
721:     ~DroneHardwareController();
722: 
723:     void initialize_hardware();
724:     void on_hardware_show();
725:     void on_hardware_hide();
726:     void shutdown_hardware();
727: 
728:     void set_spectrum_mode(SpectrumMode mode);
729:     uint32_t get_spectrum_bandwidth() const;
730:     void set_spectrum_bandwidth(uint32_t bandwidth_hz);
731:     Frequency get_spectrum_center_frequency() const;
732:     void set_spectrum_center_frequency(Frequency center_freq);
733: 
734:     bool tune_to_frequency(Frequency frequency_hz);
735:     void start_spectrum_streaming();
736:     void stop_spectrum_streaming();
737:     int32_t get_real_rssi_from_hardware(Frequency target_frequency);
738:     bool is_spectrum_streaming_active() const;
739:     int32_t get_current_rssi() const;
740:     void update_spectrum_for_scanner();
741: 
742:     void stop_spectrum_before_scan();
743:     void resume_spectrum_after_scan();
744:     bool is_spectrum_compatible_with_scanning() const;
745: 
746:     void clear_rssi_flag();
747:     bool is_rssi_fresh() const;
748: 
749:     // TOCTOU race condition fix - critical section check-and-fetch method
750:     bool get_rssi_if_fresh(int32_t& out_rssi) {
751:         CriticalSection lock;
752:         if (!rssi_updated_) {
753:             return false;
754:         }
755:         out_rssi = last_valid_rssi_;
756:         rssi_updated_ = false;
757:         return true;
758:     }
759: 
760:     // Spectrum data access method (single critical section to avoid TOCTOU race)
761:     bool get_latest_spectrum_if_fresh(std::array<uint8_t, 256>& out_db_buffer) {
762:         // Single critical section for entire check-and-fetch operation
763:         CriticalSection lock;
764:         if (!spectrum_updated_) {
765:             return false;
766:         }
767:         out_db_buffer = last_spectrum_db_;
768:         spectrum_updated_ = false;
769:         return true;
770:     }
771:     bool try_get_latest_spectrum(std::array<uint8_t, 256>& out_db_buffer) {
772:         MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_, LockOrder::SPECTRUM_MUTEX);
773:         out_db_buffer = last_spectrum_db_;
774:         return true;
775:     }
776:     void clear_spectrum_flag() {
777:         CriticalSection lock;
778:         spectrum_updated_ = false;
779:     }
780: 
781:     // Public method to set spectrum FIFO (called from parent View)
782:     void set_spectrum_fifo(ChannelSpectrumFIFO* fifo) {
783:         spectrum_fifo_ = fifo;
784:     }
785: 
786:     void handle_channel_spectrum_config(const ChannelSpectrumConfigMessage* const message);
787:     void handle_channel_statistics(const ChannelStatistics& statistics);
788:     void handle_channel_spectrum(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
789:     void process_channel_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
790: 
791:     DroneHardwareController(const DroneHardwareController&) = delete;
792:     DroneHardwareController& operator=(const DroneHardwareController&) = delete;
793: 
794: private:
795:     void initialize_radio_state();
796:     void initialize_spectrum_collector();
797:     void cleanup_spectrum_collector();
798: 
799:     int32_t get_configured_sampling_rate() const;
800:     int32_t get_configured_bandwidth() const;
801:     
802:     // Spectrum data buffer and synchronization
803:     std::array<uint8_t, 256> last_spectrum_db_;
804:     mutable Mutex spectrum_mutex_;
805: 
806:     // Diamond Code: Use volatile bool for thread-safe flag access
807:     // volatile bool reads/writes are atomic on ARM Cortex-M4 (32-bit aligned)
808:     // Protected by CriticalSection (chSysLock/chSysUnlock) for write operations
809:     volatile bool spectrum_updated_{false};
810: 
811:     SpectrumMode spectrum_mode_;
812:     Frequency center_frequency_;
813:     uint32_t bandwidth_hz_;
814:     RxRadioState radio_state_;
815:     ChannelSpectrumFIFO* spectrum_fifo_ = nullptr;
816:     bool spectrum_streaming_active_ = false;
817: 
818:     // Diamond Code: Use volatile bool for thread-safe flag access
819:     // volatile bool reads/writes are atomic on ARM Cortex-M4 (32-bit aligned)
820:     // Protected by CriticalSection (chSysLock/chSysUnlock) for write operations
821:     volatile bool rssi_updated_{false};
822:     volatile int32_t last_valid_rssi_{-120};
823:     
824:     // FIX: Moved message handlers to parent View to prevent MsgDblReg
825:     // Only ChannelStatistics handler remains here as it's unique
826:     
827:     MessageHandlerRegistration message_handler_channel_statistics_ {
828:         Message::ID::ChannelStatistics,
829:         [this](Message* const p) {
830:             const auto statistics_msg = static_cast<const ChannelStatisticsMessage*>(p);
831:             this->handle_channel_statistics(statistics_msg->statistics);
832:         }
833:     };
834: };

1070: class DroneDisplayController : public View {
1071: public:
1072:     // Spectrum Configuration Constants (Flash storage, zero RAM overhead)
1073:     
1074:     // / @brief Default frequency width per spectrum bin (100 kHz)
1075:     static constexpr uint32_t DEFAULT_EACH_BIN_SIZE_HZ = 100000;
1076:     
1077:     // / @brief Default frequency step for spectrum markers (1 MHz)
1078:     static constexpr uint32_t DEFAULT_MARKER_PIXEL_STEP_HZ = 1000000;
1079:     
1080:     // / @brief Default minimum color power level
1081:     static constexpr uint8_t DEFAULT_MIN_COLOR_POWER = 0;
1082:     
1083:     // Histogram Color Thresholds (0-255 scale, Flash storage)
1084:     
1085:     // / @brief 20% threshold (51 = 0.20 * 255)
1086:     static constexpr uint8_t HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_20PCT = 51;
1087:     
1088:     // / @brief 40% threshold (102 = 0.40 * 255)
1089:     static constexpr uint8_t HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_40PCT = 102;
1090:     
1091:     // / @brief 60% threshold (153 = 0.60 * 255)
1092:     static constexpr uint8_t HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_60PCT = 153;
1093:     
1094:     // / @brief 80% threshold (204 = 0.80 * 255)
1095:     static constexpr uint8_t HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_80PCT = 204;
1096:     
1097:     // Display Mode Enumeration (type-safe display mode selection)
1098: 
1099:     // / @brief Display mode enumeration for type safety
1100:     enum class DisplayRenderMode : uint8_t {
1101:         DEFAULT = 0,  ///< Default mode
1102:         SPECTRUM = 1, ///< Spectrum display mode
1103:         HISTOGRAM = 2  ///< Histogram display mode
1104:     };
1105: 
1106:     // Static buffer sizes to prevent heap allocation in constructor
1107:     static constexpr size_t MAX_UI_DRONES = 3;  // Reduced from 16 to 3 for memory savings
1108:     
1109:     // Histogram Display Buffer (zero-heap, static storage in .bss)
1110:     struct HistogramDisplayBuffer {
1111:         // 64 bins, each storing count (0-255), total: 64 bytes
1112:         alignas(4) uint8_t bin_counts[64];
1113:         
1114:         // Metadata for rendering
1115:         uint8_t max_count;      // Maximum bin count (for scaling)
1116:         uint8_t noise_floor;    // Noise floor from spectral analysis
1117:         bool is_valid;          // Buffer contains valid data
1118:         
1119:         // / @brief Clear histogram buffer
1120:         void clear() noexcept {
1121:             std::fill(std::begin(bin_counts), std::end(bin_counts), 0);
1122:             max_count = 0;
1123:             noise_floor = 0;
1124:             is_valid = false;
1125:         }
1126:     };
1127:     
1128:     // Histogram rendering constants (stored in Flash)
1129:     static constexpr int HISTOGRAM_Y = 164;
1130:     static constexpr int HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT = 26;
1131:     static constexpr int HISTOGRAM_WIDTH = 240;
1132:     static constexpr int HISTOGRAM_NUM_BINS = 64;
1133:     static constexpr int HISTOGRAM_BIN_WIDTH = HISTOGRAM_WIDTH / HISTOGRAM_NUM_BINS;  // 3.75px/bin
1134:     
1135:     explicit DroneDisplayController(Rect parent_rect = {0, 60, screen_width, screen_height - 80});
1136:     ~DroneDisplayController();
1137: 
1138:     Text& big_display() { return big_display_; }
1139:     ProgressBar& scanning_progress() { return scanning_progress_; }
1140:     Text& text_threat_summary() { return text_threat_summary_; }
1141:     Text& text_status_info() { return text_status_info_; }
1142:     Text& text_scanner_stats() { return text_scanner_stats_; }
1143:     Text& text_trends_compact() { return text_trends_compact_; }
1144:     Text& text_drone_1() { return text_drone_1_; }
1145:     Text& text_drone_2() { return text_drone_2_; }
1146:     Text& text_drone_3() { return text_drone_3_; }
1147: 
1148:     // Direct array access instead of switch
1149:     static constexpr size_t NUM_DRONE_TEXT_WIDGETS = 3;
1150: 
1151:     // Return reference to static array
1152:     std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, MAX_UI_DRONES>& detected_drones() {
1153:         return *reinterpret_cast<std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, MAX_UI_DRONES>*>(detected_drones_storage_);
1154:     }
1155:     const std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, MAX_UI_DRONES>& detected_drones() const {
1156:         return *reinterpret_cast<const std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, MAX_UI_DRONES>*>(detected_drones_storage_);
1157:     }
1158: 
1159:     // Histogram Display Methods
1160:     
1161:     // / @brief Update histogram display buffer with new data
1162:     void update_histogram_display(
1163:         const SpectralAnalyzer::HistogramBuffer& analysis_histogram,
1164:         uint8_t noise_floor
1165:     ) noexcept;
1166:     
1167:     // / @brief Render histogram to display
1168:     void render_histogram(Painter& painter) noexcept;
1169: 
1170:     // / @brief Clear the histogram display area
1171:     // / @param painter The painter to use for clearing
1172:     void clear_histogram_area(Painter& painter) noexcept;
1173: 
1174:     // / @brief Get the current display mode
1175:     // / @return Current display mode (SPECTRUM or HISTOGRAM)
1176:     DisplayRenderMode get_display_mode() const noexcept {
1177:         return mode_;
1178:     }
1179: 
1180:     // / @brief Set the display mode
1181:     // / @param new_mode The new display mode to set
1182:     void set_display_mode(DisplayRenderMode new_mode) noexcept {
1183:         mode_ = new_mode;
1184:         // DIAMOND FIX: Reset histogram_dirty_ when switching to histogram mode
1185:         // This ensures the histogram is rendered immediately after mode switch
1186:         if (new_mode == DisplayRenderMode::HISTOGRAM) {
1187:             histogram_dirty_ = true;
1188:         }
1189:     }
1190: 
1191:     void update_detection_display(const DroneScanner& scanner);
1192:     void update_trends_display(size_t approaching, size_t static_count, size_t receding);
1193:     void update_signal_type_display(const char* signal_type);
1194:     void set_scanning_status(bool active, const char* message);
1195:     void set_frequency_display(Frequency freq);
1196:     void add_detected_drone(Frequency freq, DroneType type, ThreatLevel threat, int32_t rssi);
1197:     void update_drones_display(const DroneScanner& scanner);
1198:     void sort_drones_by_rssi();
1199:     void render_drone_text_display();
1200: 
1201:     void process_mini_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
1202:     bool process_bins(uint8_t* power_level);
1203: 
1204:     void render_bar_spectrum(Painter& painter);
1205:     void highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(const std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, EDA::Constants::MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES>& drones);
1206:     size_t frequency_to_spectrum_bin(Frequency freq_hz) const;
1207:     void clear_spectrum_buffers();
1208:     void set_spectrum_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq);
1209:     void update_frequency_ruler();
1210:     void set_ruler_style(RulerStyle style);
1211:     void apply_display_settings(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings);
1212:     CompactFrequencyRuler& compact_frequency_ruler() { return compact_frequency_ruler_; }
1213: 
1214:     // Buffer allocation/deallocation (deferred from constructor)

1405:     // DIAMOND FIX: Thread-Safe Buffer Protection
1406:     // Mutexes for protecting shared buffers accessed by multiple threads
1407:     // - spectrum_mutex_: Protects spectrum_power_levels_ buffer
1408:     // - histogram_mutex_: Protects histogram_display_buffer_ buffer
1409:     // LOCK ORDER RULE:
1410:     // Always acquire locks in ascending order:
1411:     // 1. SPECTRUM_MUTEX (spectrum_mutex_)
1412:     // 2. HISTOGRAM_MUTEX (histogram_mutex_)
1413:     // These mutexes prevent TOCTOU race conditions between:
1414:     // - Scanner thread: Writes to spectrum_power_levels_ via process_bins()
1415:     // - UI thread: Reads from spectrum_power_levels_ via render_bar_spectrum()
1416:     // - Scanner thread: Writes to histogram_display_buffer_ via update_histogram_display()
1417:     // - UI thread: Reads from histogram_display_buffer_ via render_histogram()
1418:     mutable Mutex spectrum_mutex_;  ///< Protects spectrum_power_levels_ buffer
1419:     mutable Mutex histogram_mutex_; ///< Protects histogram_display_buffer_ buffer
1420: 
1421:     struct ThreatBin { size_t bin; ThreatLevel threat; };
1422:     std::array<ThreatBin, EDA::Constants::MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES> threat_bins_;
1423:     size_t threat_bins_count_ = 0;

1426:     ChannelSpectrumFIFO* spectrum_fifo_ = nullptr;

1432:     uint32_t marker_pixel_step = 1000000;
1433:     uint8_t max_power = 0;
1434:     uint8_t range_max_power = 0;
1435:     DisplayRenderMode mode_ = DisplayRenderMode::SPECTRUM;
1436: 
1437:     SpectrumConfig spectrum_config_;
1438: 
1439:     // Use UnifiedStringLookup and UnifiedColorLookup directly at call sites
1440: 
1441:     // Signal shape analysis for bar spectrum (no SpectralAnalyzer)
1442:     inline size_t get_bar_color_index(size_t x, uint8_t power) const {
1443:         // For static buffers, check is simplified
1444:         if (!buffers_allocated_) {
1445:             return 2; // Unknown/Noise (Grey)
1446:         }
1447: 
1448:         // Sharp peak (narrowband drone control): current > neighbors by 15+
1449:         // Wideband signal (wideband video/WiFi): all approximately equal
1450:         const auto& levels = spectrum_power_levels();
1451:         if (x > 0 && x < levels.size() - 1) {
1452:             uint8_t prev = levels[x - 1];
1453:             uint8_t next = levels[x + 1];
1454: 
1455:             // Sharp peak logic: current HIGHER than neighbors by 15+ units
1456:             if (power > prev + BarSpectrumConfig::PEAK_SHARPNESS_THRESHOLD &&
1457:                 power > next + BarSpectrumConfig::PEAK_SHARPNESS_THRESHOLD) {
1458:                 return 1; // Sharp Peak (Red)
1459:             }
1460:         }
1461: 
1462:         // Wideband signal: Blue
1463:         return 0; // Wideband (Blue)
1464:     }
1465: 
1466:     void handle_channel_spectrum(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
1467: };

1475: class DroneUIController {
1476: public:
1477:     // INITIALIZATION PATTERN
1478:     // Constructor does NOT take display_controller as parameter.
1479:     // Instead, display_controller_ is set via set_display_controller() after construction.
1480:     // This two-phase initialization pattern makes the initialization order
1481:     // independent of member declaration order in the parent class.
1482:     // Benefits:
1483:     // - No fragile dependency on declaration order
1484:     // - ui_controller_ can be declared before display_controller_
1485:     // - display_controller_ can be declared anywhere in the parent class
1486:     // Usage in EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView:
1487:     // 1. Construct ui_controller_ (display_controller_ = nullptr)
1488:     // 2. Construct display_controller_
1489:     // 3. Call ui_controller_.set_display_controller(&display_controller_)
1490:     // Constructor without display_controller - set via set_display_controller() after construction
1491:     // This makes initialization order independent of member declaration order
1492:     DroneUIController(NavigationView& nav,
1493:                      DroneHardwareController& hardware,
1494:                      DroneScanner& scanner,
1495:                      ::AudioManager& audio_mgr);
1496:     ~DroneUIController();
1497: 
1498:     // Set display_controller after construction
1499:     void set_display_controller(DroneDisplayController* display_controller) {
1500:         display_controller_ = display_controller;
1501:     }
1502: 
1503:     void on_start_scan();
1504:     void on_stop_scan();
1505:     void show_menu();
1506:     void on_open_settings();
1507:     void on_about();
1508:     void on_hardware_control();
1509:     void on_view_logs();
1510:     void update_scanner_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq);
1511: 
1512:     bool is_scanning() const { return scanning_active_; }
1513:     DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings() { return settings_; }
1514:     const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings() const { return settings_; }
1515:     DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings_ref() { return settings_; }
1516:     const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings_ref() const { return settings_; }
1517: 
1518:     DroneUIController(const DroneUIController&) = delete;
1519:     DroneUIController& operator=(const DroneUIController&) = delete;
1520: 
1521: private:
1522:     NavigationView& nav_;
1523:     DroneHardwareController& hardware_;
1524:     DroneScanner& scanner_;
1525:     ::AudioManager& audio_mgr_;
1526:     // volatile bool reads/writes are atomic on ARM Cortex-M4 (32-bit aligned)
1527:     volatile bool scanning_active_{false};
1528:     DroneDisplayController* display_controller_ = nullptr;
1529:     ::ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::DroneAnalyzerSettings settings_;
1530: 
1531:     void on_manage_frequencies();
1532:     void on_create_new_database();
1533:     void on_frequency_warning();
1534:     void select_spectrum_mode(SpectrumMode mode);
1535:     void on_set_bandwidth();
1536:     void on_set_center_freq();
1537:     void show_hardware_status();
1538: };

1576:     // Deferred initialization state machine
1577:     enum class InitState : uint8_t {
1578:         CONSTRUCTED = 0,           // Constructor completed
1579:         BUFFERS_ALLOCATED,         // display buffers heap-allocated
1580:         DATABASE_LOADING,           // DIAMOND FIX #4: Async database loading in progress
1581:         DATABASE_LOADED,           // Async database loading complete
1582:         HARDWARE_READY,            // hardware_.on_hardware_show() completed
1583:         UI_LAYOUT_READY,           // initialize_modern_layout() completed
1584:         SETTINGS_LOADED,           // SettingsPersistence::load() completed
1585:          COORDINATOR_READY,         // coordinator thread creation prepared
1586:          FULLY_INITIALIZED = 8,    // Ready for operation
1587:          INITIALIZATION_ERROR = 9  // Timeout or critical error
1588:      };

1599:     // Initialization timing constants (eliminates magic numbers)
1600:     struct InitTiming {

1604:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_INTERVAL_MS = 50;
1605: 
1606:         // Cumulative delays (each phase + minimum 200ms for execution)
1607:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_0_MS = 50;     // Allocate buffers
1608:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_1_MS = 300;    // Database (50 + 250 for async)
1609:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_2_MS = 500;    // Hardware (300 + 200)
1610:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_3_MS = 700;    // UI Setup (500 + 200)
1611:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_4_MS = 900;    // Settings (700 + 200)
1612:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_5_MS = 1100;   // Finalize (900 + 200)
1613: 
1614:         static constexpr uint8_t MAX_PHASES = 6;
1615:     };

1692:     // FIX: Unified message handlers to prevent MsgDblReg
1693:     // These handlers delegate to controllers and internal methods
1694:     
1695:     MessageHandlerRegistration message_handler_spectrum_config_ {
1696:         Message::ID::ChannelSpectrumConfig,
1697:         [this](Message* const p) {
1698:             const auto message = *reinterpret_cast<const ChannelSpectrumConfigMessage*>(p);
1699:             // Delegate FIFO pointer to both controllers that need it
1700:             hardware_.set_spectrum_fifo(message.fifo);
1701:             display_controller_.set_spectrum_fifo(message.fifo);
1702:         }
1703:     };
1704: 
1705:     MessageHandlerRegistration message_handler_frame_sync_ {
1706:         Message::ID::DisplayFrameSync,
1707:         [this](Message* const) {
1708:             // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Enhanced initialization with timeout protection
1709:             // Executed every frame (~16ms at 60 FPS)
1710:             if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
1711:                 // UI,
1712:                 return;
1713:             }
1714:             
1715:             if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
1716:                 step_deferred_initialization();
1717:                 // Return early if not fully initialized
1718:                 return;
1719:             }
1720: 
1721:             // SAFETY:
1722:             if (!display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
1723:                 return;
1724:             }
1725: 
1726:             // Normal operation mode: Process spectrum data in display controller
1727:             display_controller_.process_frame_sync();
1728: 
1729:             // Handle scanner updates in main view
1730:             this->handle_scanner_update();
1731:         }
1732:     };
1733: 
1734:     void start_scanning_thread();
1735:     void stop_scanning_thread();
1736:     bool handle_start_stop_button();
1737:     bool handle_menu_button();
1738:     void initialize_modern_layout();
1739:     void update_modern_layout();
1740:     void handle_scanner_update();
1741:     void setup_button_handlers();
1742:     void initialize_scanning_mode();
1743:     void set_scanning_mode_from_index(size_t index);
1744:     void add_ui_elements();
1745: 
1746:     // Static histogram callback (no lambda captures, no heap allocation)
1747:     static void static_histogram_callback(
1748:         const SpectralAnalyzer::HistogramBuffer& histogram,
1749:         uint8_t noise_floor,
1750:         void* user_data
1751:     ) noexcept;
1752: 
1753:     // FIX #5: Button Callbacks
1754:     // Diamond Code: Use lambdas with 'this' capture for callbacks
1755:     // Note: std::function may allocate on heap, but this is unavoidable
1756:     // with the Mayhem UI framework's callback design
1757: 
1758:     // Deferred initialization methods
1759:     void step_deferred_initialization() noexcept;
1760:     void update_init_progress_display();
1761: 
1762:     // Stack Usage Monitoring
1763:     // * * @brief Check stack usage and log warnings if low
1764:     void check_stack_usage(const char* thread_name, size_t stack_size);
1765: 
1766:     // STAGE 4 FIX: Memory Pressure Monitoring
1767:     // * * @brief Check memory pressure and log warnings if critical
1768:     void check_memory_pressure();
1769: 
1770:     // Initialization state variables
1771:     InitState init_state_ = InitState::CONSTRUCTED;
1772:     systime_t init_start_time_ = 0;
1773:     systime_t last_init_progress_ = 0;
1774:     // FIX: Initialization progress flag with volatile for thread safety (std::atomic not available in embedded environment)
1775:     volatile bool initialization_in_progress_{false};
1776:     
1777:     // Global shutdown flag for all threads
1778:     volatile bool global_shutdown_requested_ = false;
1779:     
1780:     // Error handling enum
1781:     enum class InitError : uint8_t {
1782:         NONE = 0,
1783:         GENERAL_TIMEOUT = 1,
1784:         ALLOCATION_FAILED = 2,
1785:         DATABASE_ERROR = 3
1786:     };
1787:     InitError init_error_ = InitError::NONE;
1788: };

85: // Replaced std::function with template-based callbacks (zero heap allocation)
86: 
87: // CRITICAL FIX: ConfigUpdaterCallback with dangling pointer protection
88: // Functor for config updates (zero heap allocation, fixed storage)
89: //
90: // PROBLEM: Raw pointer to DroneAnalyzerSettings can become invalid if parent view is destroyed
91: // SOLUTION: Add validation and documentation to prevent use-after-free
92: //
93: // USAGE CONSTRAINTS:
94: // 1. Callback must be used immediately (not stored for later use)
95: // 2. Parent view must remain alive while callback is in use
96: // 3. This is designed for short-lived menu interactions only
97: //
98: // ALTERNATIVE (for long-lived callbacks):
99: // - Copy settings by value into callback (DroneAnalyzerSettings config_copy)
100: // - Add get_settings() method to retrieve modified copy
101: // - Caller must save settings after callback returns
102: struct ConfigUpdaterCallback {
103:     DroneAnalyzerSettings* config_ptr;
104: 
105:     constexpr explicit ConfigUpdaterCallback(DroneAnalyzerSettings& config) noexcept
106:         : config_ptr(&config) {}
107: 
108:     // CRITICAL FIX: Validate pointer before dereferencing
109:     // Prevents use-after-free if parent view was destroyed
110:     // noexcept for operator()
111:     void operator()(const DronePreset& preset) const noexcept {
112:         // Guard clause to reduce nesting and prevent nullptr dereference
113:         if (!config_ptr) return;
114:         (void)DroneFrequencyPresets::apply_preset(*config_ptr, preset);
115:     }
116: 
117: };
118: 
119: // Template-based callback system (zero heap allocation)
120: template <typename PresetContainer, typename Callback>
121: class PresetMenuViewImpl : public MenuView {
122: public:
123:     PresetMenuViewImpl(NavigationView& nav, const char* const* names, size_t count,
124:                        Callback on_selected, const PresetContainer& presets)
125:         : MenuView(), nav_(nav), names_(names), name_count_(count),
126:           on_selected_fn_(std::move(on_selected)), presets_(presets) {
127:         for (size_t i = 0; i < name_count_; ++i) {
128:             add_item({names_[i], Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
129:         }
130:     }
131: 
132:     PresetMenuViewImpl(const PresetMenuViewImpl&) = delete;
133:     PresetMenuViewImpl& operator=(const PresetMenuViewImpl&) = delete;
134: 
135: private:
136:     NavigationView& nav_;
137:     const char* const* names_;
138:     size_t name_count_;
139:     Callback on_selected_fn_;  // Template parameter - no heap allocation
140:     const PresetContainer& presets_;
141: 
142:     // noexcept for key handling
143:     bool on_key(const KeyEvent key) noexcept override {
144:         // Guard clause for early return
145:         if (key != KeyEvent::Select) return MenuView::on_key(key);
146:         
147:         size_t idx = highlighted_index();
148:         if (idx < presets_.size()) {
149:             on_selected_fn_(presets_[idx]);
150:         }
151:         return true;
152:     }
153: };

161:         const auto preset_names = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_preset_names();
162:         const auto& all_presets = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_all_presets();
163:         const auto preset_count = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_preset_count();
164: 
165:         using PresetMenuViewT = PresetMenuViewImpl<std::array<DronePreset, 5>, Callback>;
166:         nav.push<PresetMenuViewT>(preset_names, preset_count, std::move(callback), all_presets);
167:     }
168:     
169:     static void show_type_filtered_presets(NavigationView& nav, DroneType type) noexcept;
170:

173: };

202: // Database manager class
203: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Database manager with zero heap allocation
204: // 
205: // LEGACY NOTE: This class is being phased out in favor of UnifiedDroneDatabase.
206: // It remains for backward compatibility with older settings files.

209: class DroneDatabaseManager {
210: public:
211:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Named constant for max entries
212:     static constexpr size_t MAX_DATABASE_ENTRIES = 100;
213:     
214:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: POD struct for database view (zero heap allocation)
215:     struct DatabaseView {
216:         DroneDbEntry entries[MAX_DATABASE_ENTRIES];
217:         size_t count = 0;
218:         
219:         // [[nodiscard]] - Validation must be checked
220:         [[nodiscard]] constexpr bool is_valid() const noexcept { return count > 0; }
221:         // [[nodiscard]] - Entry access must be used
222:         [[nodiscard]] constexpr const DroneDbEntry& operator[](size_t idx) const noexcept {
223:             return (idx < count) ? entries[idx] : entries[0];
224:         }
225:         // [[nodiscard]] - Size must be used
226:         [[nodiscard]] constexpr size_t size() const noexcept { return count; }
227:     };
228:     
229:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for all methods
230:     // [[nodiscard]] - Database load/save success must be checked
231:     [[nodiscard]] static DatabaseView load_database(const char* file_path = "/FREQMAN/DRONES.TXT") noexcept;
232:     [[nodiscard]] static bool save_database(const DatabaseView& view, const char* file_path = "/FREQMAN/DRONES.TXT") noexcept;
