187: DroneScanner::~DroneScanner() {
188:     stop_scanning();
189:     cleanup_database_and_scanner();
190:     // ChibiOS mutexes auto-cleaned with the object
191: }
192: 
193: void DroneScanner::initialize_wideband_scanning() {
194:     wideband_scan_data_.reset();
195:     setup_wideband_range(WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MIN, WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MAX);
196: }
197: 
198: void DroneScanner::setup_wideband_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
199:     Frequency safe_min = std::max(min_freq, EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ);
200:     Frequency safe_max = std::min(max_freq, EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ);
201: 
202:     // Swap to ensure min <= max
203:     if (safe_min > safe_max) {
204:         safe_min = safe_max;
205:         safe_max = std::max(min_freq, EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ);
206:     }
207: 
208:     wideband_scan_data_.min_freq = safe_min;
209:     wideband_scan_data_.max_freq = safe_max;
210: 
211:     Frequency scanning_range = safe_max - safe_min;
212:     const uint64_t width_u64 = static_cast<uint64_t>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz);
213:     if (scanning_range > static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz)) {
214:         // Check for overflow BEFORE addition
215:         if (scanning_range < EDA::Constants::NEGATIVE_RANGE_INDICATOR) {
216:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_SLICE_COUNT_MIN;
217:         } else {
218:             const uint64_t range_u64 = static_cast<uint64_t>(scanning_range);
219: 
220:             // Check for overflow
221:             if (UINT64_MAX - range_u64 < width_u64) {
222:                 wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_SLICE_COUNT_MIN;
223:             } else {
224:                 // Use constexpr ceil_div_u64 for compiler optimization
225:                 uint64_t range_plus_width = range_u64 + width_u64;
226:                 uint64_t slices_calc = ceil_div_u64(range_plus_width, width_u64);
227:                 // Check if result exceeds size_t max
228:                 if (slices_calc > static_cast<uint64_t>(SIZE_MAX)) {
229:                     wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES;
230:                 } else {
231:                     wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = static_cast<size_t>(slices_calc);
232:                 }
233:             }
234:         }
235: 
236:         if (wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb > WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES) {
237:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES;
238:         }
239:         
240:         // Check for overflow in multiplication
241:         const uint64_t slices_nb_u64 = static_cast<uint64_t>(wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb);
242:         if (slices_nb_u64 > 0 && UINT64_MAX / slices_nb_u64 < width_u64) {
243:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES;
244:         }
245:         
246:         // Check for INT64_MAX overflow before casting to Frequency
247:         const uint64_t product = slices_nb_u64 * width_u64;
248:         if (product > static_cast<uint64_t>(INT64_MAX)) {
249:             return;
250:         }
251:         Frequency slices_span = static_cast<Frequency>(product);
252:         Frequency offset = ((scanning_range - slices_span) / 2) + (settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz / 2);
253:         Frequency center_frequency = safe_min + offset;
254: 
255:         std::generate_n(wideband_scan_data_.slices,
256:                        wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb,
257:                        [&center_frequency, slice_index = 0, this]() mutable -> WidebandSlice {
258:                            WidebandSlice slice;
259:                            slice.center_frequency = center_frequency;
260:                            slice.index = slice_index++;
261:                            if (center_frequency <= static_cast<Frequency>(INT64_MAX) - static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz)) {
262:                                center_frequency += settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz;
263:                            }
264:                            return slice;
265:                        });
266:     } else {
267:         wideband_scan_data_.slices[0].center_frequency = (safe_max + safe_min) / 2;
268:         wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_SLICE_COUNT_MIN;
269:     }
270:     wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter = 0;
271: }
272: 
273: void DroneScanner::start_scanning() {
274:     bool is_scanning = scanning_active_;
275:     if (is_scanning) return;
276: 
277:     scanning_active_ = true;
278:     scan_cycles_ = 0;
279:     total_detections_ = 0;
280: }
281: 
282: void DroneScanner::stop_scanning() {
283:     bool is_scanning = scanning_active_;
284:     if (!is_scanning) return;
285: 
286:     scanning_active_ = false;
287: 
288:     if (scanning_thread_ != nullptr) {
289:         chThdWait(scanning_thread_);
290:         scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
291:     }
292: 
293:     remove_stale_drones();
294: }
295: 
296: // ============================================================================
297: // SCANNING FLOW: Database Loading
298: // ============================================================================
299: // Flow: on_show() -> init_phase_load_database() -> initialize_database_async()
300: //       -> db_loading_thread_loop() -> UnifiedDroneDatabase
301: // 
302: // Stage 4 Integration: This legacy method now delegates to UnifiedDroneDatabase
303: // for the actual frequency data. The FreqmanDB is kept for file I/O compatibility.
304: // 
305: // TODO: Future refactoring should fully migrate to UnifiedDroneDatabase
306: // and remove the dual-database complexity.
307: bool DroneScanner::load_frequency_database() {
308:     current_db_index_ = 0;
309: 
310:     freqman_load_options options;
311:     options.max_entries = 150;
312:     options.load_freqs = true;
313:     options.load_ranges = true;
314:     options.load_hamradios = true;
315:     options.load_repeaters = true;
316: 
317:     if (!freq_db_ptr_ || !freq_db_constructed_) {
318:         return false;
319:     }
320: 
321:     auto db_path = get_freqman_path(settings_.freqman_path);
322: 
323:     {
324:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
325: 
326:         bool sd_loaded = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
327: 
328:         if (!sd_loaded || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
329:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
330: 
331:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
332:                 freqman_entry entry{};
333:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
334:                 entry.description = item.desc;
335:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
336:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
337:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
338:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
339:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
340:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
341:             }
342: 
343:             sync_database();
344:         }
345:     }
346: 
347:     if (freq_db_ptr_->entry_count() > 100) {
348:         handle_scan_error("Large database loaded");
349:     }
350: 
351:     freq_db_loaded_ = true;
352:     return !freq_db_ptr_->empty();
353: }
354: 
355: // Stage 4: Database observer callback for real-time sync
356: void DroneScanner::database_change_callback(const DatabaseChangeEvent& event, void* user_data) {
357:     auto* scanner = static_cast<DroneScanner*>(user_data);
358:     if (scanner == nullptr) return;
359:     
360:     switch (event.type) {
361:         case DatabaseEventType::ENTRY_ADDED:
362:         case DatabaseEventType::ENTRY_DELETED:
363:         case DatabaseEventType::DATABASE_RELOADED:
364:             // Signal scanner to reload frequency list
365:             scanner->database_needs_reload_ = true;
366:             break;
367:         default:
368:             break;
369:     }
370: }
371: 
372: void DroneScanner::register_database_observer() {
373:     auto& db = UnifiedDroneDatabase::instance();
374:     (void)db.add_observer(&DroneScanner::database_change_callback, this);
375: }
376: 
377: void DroneScanner::unregister_database_observer() {
378:     auto& db = UnifiedDroneDatabase::instance();
379:     db.remove_observer(&DroneScanner::database_change_callback);
380: }
381: 
382: size_t DroneScanner::get_database_size() const {
383:     return freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
384: }
385: 
386: void DroneScanner::set_scanning_mode(ScanningMode mode) {
387:     scanning_mode_ = mode;
388:     stop_scanning();
389:     reset_scan_cycles();
390: 
391:     if (scanning_mode_ == ScanningMode::DATABASE || scanning_mode_ == ScanningMode::HYBRID) {
392:         load_frequency_database();
393:     }
394: }
395: 
396: const char* DroneScanner::scanning_mode_name() const {
397:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanning_mode_);
398:     return (idx < 3) ? SCANNING_MODE_NAMES[idx] : "Unknown";
399: }
400: 
401: // ============================================================================
402: // SCANNING FLOW: Main Scan Cycle
403: // ============================================================================
404: // Flow: perform_scan_cycle() -> SCAN_FUNCTIONS LUT -> perform_database_scan_cycle()
405: //       or perform_wideband_scan_cycle() or perform_hybrid_scan_cycle()
406: //
407: // Adaptive Scanning: Scan interval adjusts based on threat level:
408: // - CRITICAL threat: FAST_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS (50ms)
409: // - HIGH threat: HIGH_THREAT_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS (100ms)
410: // - MEDIUM threat: NORMAL_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS (200ms)
411: // - No detections: Progressive slowdown up to VERY_SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS (2000ms)
412: //
413: // LUT-based dispatch: SCAN_FUNCTIONS array provides O(1) dispatch to scan method
414: void DroneScanner::perform_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
415:     // Guard clause: Early return if not scanning
416:     bool is_scanning = scanning_active_;
417:     if (!is_scanning) return;
418: 
419:     // Stage 4: Check if database needs reload due to observer notification
420:     if (database_needs_reload_) {
421:         database_needs_reload_ = false;
422:         load_frequency_database();
423:     }
424: 
425:     using namespace EDA::Constants;
426:     uint32_t base_interval = DEFAULT_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
427:     uint32_t adaptive_interval = base_interval;
428: 
429:     size_t current_detections = get_total_detections();
430:     ThreatLevel max_threat = get_max_detected_threat();
431:     size_t tracked_count = tracked_count_;
432: 
433:     if (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::CRITICAL) {
434:         adaptive_interval = FAST_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
435:     } else if (max_threat == ThreatLevel::HIGH) {
436:         adaptive_interval = HIGH_THREAT_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
437:     } else if (max_threat == ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) {
438:         adaptive_interval = NORMAL_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
439:     } else if (current_detections > 0 && tracked_count > 0) {
440:         adaptive_interval = SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
441:     } else if (current_detections == 0 && scan_cycles_ > PROGRESSIVE_SLOWDOWN_DIVISOR) {
442:         uint32_t cycles_value = get_scan_cycles();
443:         uint32_t cycles_clamped = (cycles_value < 39) ? cycles_value : 39;
444:         uint32_t slowdown_multiplier = SLOWDOWN_MULTIPLIER_LUT[cycles_clamped];
445:         uint32_t interval_calc = base_interval * slowdown_multiplier;
446:         adaptive_interval = (interval_calc < VERY_SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS) ? interval_calc : VERY_SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
447:     }
448: 
449:     // Additional adjustment for high detection density
450:     static constexpr size_t HIGH_DENSITY_DETECTION_THRESHOLD = EDA::Constants::HIGH_DENSITY_DETECTION_THRESHOLD;
451:     if (current_detections > HIGH_DENSITY_DETECTION_THRESHOLD) {
452:         adaptive_interval = (adaptive_interval < HIGH_DENSITY_SCAN_CAP_MS) ? adaptive_interval : HIGH_DENSITY_SCAN_CAP_MS;
453:     }
454:     
455:     chThdSleepMilliseconds(adaptive_interval);
456: 
457:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanning_mode_);
458:     if (mode_idx < 3) {
459:         (this->*DroneScanner::SCAN_FUNCTIONS[mode_idx])(hardware);
460:     }
461: 
462:     {
463:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
464:         scan_cycles_++;
465:     }
466: 
467:     is_scanning = scanning_active_;
468:     if (is_scanning) {
469:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(adaptive_interval);
470:     }
471: }
472: 
473: // ============================================================================
474: // SCANNING FLOW: Database Scan Cycle
475: // ============================================================================
476: // Flow: perform_database_scan_cycle() -> hardware.tune_to_frequency() -> 
477: //       hardware.get_current_rssi() -> process_rssi_detection()
478: //
479: // Hardware Tuning Sequence:
480: // 1. Validate frequency range (MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ to MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ)
481: // 2. Tune radio via receiver_model.set_target_frequency()
482: // 3. Wait for PLL stabilization (PLL_STABILIZATION_ITERATIONS * PLL_STABILIZATION_DELAY_MS)
483: // 4. Acquire RSSI measurement with timeout (RSSI_TIMEOUT_MS)
484: // 5. Process detection if signal captured
485: //
486: // Memory Optimization: Uses class member buffers (entries_to_scan_) instead of
487: // stack allocation to prevent stack overflow on STM32F405 (192KB RAM)
488: void DroneScanner::perform_database_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
489:     // Stack overflow detection check
490:     if (!check_stack_canary()) {
491:         // Stack overflow detected - reinitialize canary to prevent further corruption
492:         init_stack_canary();
493:     }
494: 
495:     size_t total_entries = 0;
496: 
497:     {
498:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
499:         if (!freq_db_ptr_ || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
500:             if (scan_cycles_ % EDA::Constants::SCAN_CYCLE_CHECK_INTERVAL == 0) {
501:                 handle_scan_error("Database is empty");
502:             }
503:             return;
504:         }
505:         total_entries = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
506:     }
507: 
508:     const size_t batch_size = std::min(static_cast<size_t>(EDA::Constants::MAX_SCAN_BATCH_SIZE), total_entries);
509: 
510:     // Use class member variable instead of stack allocation (heap-free)
511:     auto& entries_to_scan = entries_to_scan_;
512:     size_t entries_count = 0;
513: 
514:     {
515:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
516:         if (freq_db_ptr_) {
517:             size_t db_entry_count = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
518:             if (db_entry_count > 0) {
519:                 for (size_t i = 0; i < batch_size; ++i) {
520:                     size_t idx = (current_db_index_ + i) % db_entry_count;
521:                     if (idx < db_entry_count && entries_count < entries_to_scan.size()) {
522:                         entries_to_scan[entries_count++] = (*freq_db_ptr_)[idx];
523:                     }
524:                 }
525:                 current_db_index_ = (current_db_index_ + batch_size) % db_entry_count;
526:             }
527:         }
528:     }
529: 
530:     static constexpr int PLL_STABILIZATION_ITERATIONS = EDA::Constants::PLL_STABILIZATION_ITERATIONS;
531:     static constexpr uint32_t PLL_STABILIZATION_DELAY_MS = EDA::Constants::PLL_STABILIZATION_DELAY_MS;
532:     
533:     const Frequency MIN_VALID_FREQ = EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
534:     const Frequency MAX_VALID_FREQ = EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
535: 
536:     for (size_t i = 0; i < entries_count; ++i) {
537:         const auto& entry = entries_to_scan[i];
538: 
539:         // Guard clause: check scanning flag
540:         bool is_scanning = scanning_active_;
541:         if (!is_scanning) return;
542: 
543:         Frequency target_freq_hz = entry.frequency_a;
544: 
545:         // Guard clause: validate frequency range
546:         if (target_freq_hz < MIN_VALID_FREQ || target_freq_hz > MAX_VALID_FREQ) continue;
547: 
548:         // Guard clause: hardware tuning validation
549:         if (!hardware.tune_to_frequency(target_freq_hz)) continue;
550: 
551:         // Wait for PLL stabilization
552:         for (int w = 0; w < PLL_STABILIZATION_ITERATIONS; w++) {
553:             is_scanning = scanning_active_;
554:             if (!is_scanning) return;
555:             chThdSleepMilliseconds(PLL_STABILIZATION_DELAY_MS);
556:         }
557: 
558:         hardware.clear_rssi_flag();
559: 
560:         // Optimized polling: check condition first, then sleep
561:         systime_t deadline = chTimeNow() + MS2ST(EDA::Constants::RSSI_TIMEOUT_MS);
562:         bool signal_captured = false;
563: 
564:         if (hardware.is_rssi_fresh()) {
565:             signal_captured = true;
566:         } else {
567:             constexpr uint32_t OPTIMIZED_POLL_DELAY_MS = 10;
568:             while (chTimeNow() < deadline) {
569:                 chThdSleepMilliseconds(OPTIMIZED_POLL_DELAY_MS);
570:                 if (hardware.is_rssi_fresh()) {
571:                     signal_captured = true;
572:                     break;
573:                 }
574:             }
575:         }
576: 
577:         // Guard clause: only process if signal captured
578:         if (!signal_captured) {
579:             last_scanned_frequency_ = target_freq_hz;
580:             continue;
581:         }
582: 
583:         int32_t real_rssi = hardware.get_current_rssi();
584:         process_rssi_detection(entry, real_rssi);
585:         last_scanned_frequency_ = target_freq_hz;
586:     }
587: }
588: 
589: void DroneScanner::perform_wideband_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
590:     if (wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb == 0) {
591:         setup_wideband_range(WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MIN, WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MAX);
592:     }
593:     
594:     const WidebandSlice& current_slice = wideband_scan_data_.slices[wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter];
595:     
596:     // 1. Tune to slice center
597:     if (hardware.tune_to_frequency(current_slice.center_frequency)) {
598: 
599:         // 2. Wait for PLL stabilization
600:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(EDA::Constants::PLL_STABILIZATION_DELAY_MS);
601:         
602:         if (!hardware.is_spectrum_streaming_active()) {
603:             hardware.start_spectrum_streaming();
604:         }
605:         
606:         // 3. Get spectrum data from M0 coprocessor
607:         auto& spectrum_data = spectrum_data_;
608:         
609:         // Optimized waiting: adaptive timeout with absolute deadline
610:         systime_t current_time = chTimeNow();
611:         systime_t deadline = current_time + MS2ST(EDA::Constants::SPECTRUM_TIMEOUT_MS);
612:         
613:         // Check for overflow
614:         if (deadline < current_time) {
615:             deadline = DiamondFixes::ConfidenceConstants::MAX_SYSTIME_VALUE;  // Max systime_t value
616:         }
617:         
618:         bool spectrum_received = false;
619: 
620:         // Optimized polling: check condition first
621:         if (hardware.get_latest_spectrum_if_fresh(spectrum_data)) {
622:             spectrum_received = true;
623:         } else {
624:             while (chTimeNow() < deadline) {
625:                 chThdSleepMilliseconds(EDA::Constants::CHECK_INTERVAL_MS);
626: 
627:                 if (hardware.get_latest_spectrum_if_fresh(spectrum_data)) {
628:                     spectrum_received = true;
629:                     break;
630:                 }
631:             }
632:         }
633: 
634:         // 4. Perform spectral analysis
635:         if (spectrum_received) {
636:             auto analysis_result = SpectralAnalyzer::analyze(
637:                 spectrum_data,
638:                 {hardware.get_spectrum_bandwidth(), current_slice.center_frequency},
639:                 histogram_buffer_
640:             );
641:             
642:             // Invoke histogram callback (thread-safe)
643:             if (histogram_callback_) {
644:                 histogram_callback_(histogram_buffer_, analysis_result.noise_floor, histogram_callback_user_data_);
645:             }
646:             
647:             // 5. Process detection
648:             if (analysis_result.is_valid && analysis_result.signature != SignalSignature::NOISE) {
649:                 freqman_entry detection_entry{
650:                     .frequency_a = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
651:                     .frequency_b = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
652:                     .description = "Spectral Detection",
653:                     .type = freqman_type::Single,
654:                 };
655: 
656:                 ThreatLevel threat_level = SpectralAnalyzer::get_threat_level(analysis_result.signature, analysis_result.snr);
657:                 DroneType drone_type = SpectralAnalyzer::get_drone_type(current_slice.center_frequency, analysis_result.signature);
658: 
659:                 process_spectral_detection(detection_entry, analysis_result, threat_level, drone_type);
660:             }
661:         } else {
662:             // Fallback to RSSI-based detection
663:             int32_t slice_rssi = hardware.get_real_rssi_from_hardware(current_slice.center_frequency);
664:             if (slice_rssi > WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB) {
665:                 freqman_entry fallback_entry{
666:                     .frequency_a = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
667:                     .frequency_b = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
668:                     .description = "RSSI Fallback",
669:                     .type = freqman_type::Single,
670:                 };
671:                 wideband_detection_override(fallback_entry, slice_rssi, WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB);
672:             }
673:         }
674: 
675:         last_scanned_frequency_ = current_slice.center_frequency;
676:     } else {
677:         if (scan_cycles_ % 100 == 0) {
678:             handle_scan_error("Hardware tuning failed in wideband mode");
679:         }
680:     }
681: 
682:     // Transition to next slice
683:     size_t next_slice_idx = get_next_slice_with_intelligence();
684:     wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter = next_slice_idx;
685: }
686: 
687: size_t DroneScanner::get_next_slice_with_intelligence() {
688:     (void)settings_;
689:     size_t current = wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter;
690:     size_t next = (current + 1) % wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb;
691:     return next;
692: }
693: 
694: void DroneScanner::wideband_detection_override(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi, int32_t threshold_override) {
695:     if (rssi >= threshold_override) {
696:         process_wideband_detection_with_override(entry, rssi, DEFAULT_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB, threshold_override);
697:     }
698: }
699: 
700: void DroneScanner::process_wideband_detection_with_override(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi,
701:                                                            int32_t original_threshold, int32_t wideband_threshold) {
702:     (void)original_threshold;  // Intentionally unused - kept for API compatibility
703: 
704:     if (!EDA::Validation::validate_rssi(rssi) ||
705:         !EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
706:         return;
707:     }
708: 
709:     bool should_log = false;
710:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
711:     DroneType detected_type = DroneType::UNKNOWN;
712:     ThreatLevel threat_level = ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN;
713: 
714:     // Validate frequency before division
715:     if (entry.frequency_a == EDA::Constants::ZERO_FREQUENCY) {
716:         return;
717:     }
718:     
719:     // Threat level logic
720:     if (rssi > -70) threat_level = ThreatLevel::HIGH;
721:     else if (rssi > -80) threat_level = ThreatLevel::LOW;
722:     else threat_level = ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN;
723:     if (entry.frequency_a >= 2'400'000'000 && entry.frequency_a <= 2'500'000'000) {
724:         threat_level = std::max(threat_level, ThreatLevel::MEDIUM);
725:     }
726: 
727:     // Critical section
728:     {
729:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
730: 
731:         // Increment total_detections_ with mutex protection
732:         total_detections_++;
733: 
734:         // Use bitwise AND with HASH_MASK for efficient modulo operation
735:         constexpr size_t FREQ_HASH_DIVISOR = 100000;
736:         const size_t freq_hash_raw = static_cast<size_t>(entry.frequency_a / FREQ_HASH_DIVISOR);
737:         const size_t freq_hash = freq_hash_raw & DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_MASK;
738:         int32_t effective_threshold = wideband_threshold;
739: 
740:         if (detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash) < wideband_threshold) {
741:             effective_threshold = wideband_threshold + HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
742:         }
743: 
744:         if (rssi >= effective_threshold) {
745:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
746:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
747:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, current_count, rssi});
748: 
749:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
750:                 should_log = true;
751: 
752:                 log_entry_to_write = {
753:                     chTimeNow(),
754:                     static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a),
755:                     rssi,
756:                     threat_level,
757:                     detected_type,
758:                     current_count,
759:                     DiamondFixes::ConfidenceConstants::RSSI_CONFIDENCE,  // 85% confidence as integer
760:                     0,   // width_bins - default value
761:                     0,   // signal_width_hz - default value
762:                     0    // snr - default value
763:                 };
764: 
765:                 update_tracked_drone({detected_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(rssi), threat_level});
766:             }
767:         } else {
768:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
769:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
770:             if (current_count > 0) {
771:                 current_count--;
772:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi});
773:             } else {
774:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, 0, -120});
775:             }
776:         }
777:     }
778:     // End critical section
779: 
780:     // Logging
781:     if (should_log && detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
782:         detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write);
783:     }
784: }
785: 
786: void DroneScanner::process_spectral_detection(const freqman_entry& entry,
787:                                              const SpectralAnalysisResult& analysis_result,
788:                                              ThreatLevel threat_level, DroneType drone_type) {
789:     if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
790:         return;
791:     }
792: 
793:     bool should_log = false;
794:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
795: 
796:     {
797:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
798: 
799:         total_detections_++;
800: 
801:         // Guard clause: Prevent division by zero
802:         if (entry.frequency_a == EDA::Constants::ZERO_FREQUENCY) {
803:             return;
804:         }
805:         size_t freq_hash = DiamondFixes::safe_frequency_hash(entry.frequency_a);
806:         int32_t effective_threshold = WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB;
807: 
808:         if (detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash) < WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB) {
809:             effective_threshold = WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB + HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
810:         }
811: 
812:         // Use the maximum value from spectral analysis as the effective RSSI
813:         int32_t effective_rssi = static_cast<int32_t>(analysis_result.max_val);
814: 
815:         if (effective_rssi >= effective_threshold) {
816:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
817:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
818:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, current_count, effective_rssi});
819: 
820:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
821:                 should_log = true;
822: 
823:                 log_entry_to_write = {
824:                     chTimeNow(),
825:                     static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a),
826:                     effective_rssi,
827:                     threat_level,
828:                     drone_type,
829:                     current_count,
830:                     DiamondFixes::ConfidenceConstants::SPECTRAL_CONFIDENCE,  // 90% confidence for spectral analysis
831:                     analysis_result.width_bins,        // Calibration: signal width in bins
832:                     analysis_result.signal_width_hz,   // Calibration: signal width in Hz
833:                     analysis_result.snr               // Calibration: Signal-to-Noise Ratio
834:                 };
835: 
836:                 update_tracked_drone({drone_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(effective_rssi), threat_level});
837:             }
838:         } else {
839:             // Counter decrement logic...
840:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
841:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
842:             if (current_count > 0) {
843:                 current_count--;
844:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi});
845:             } else {
846:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, 0, -120});
847:             }
848:         }
849:     }
850:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
851: 
852:     // 3. Logging
853:     if (should_log && detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
854:         detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write);
855:     }
856: }
857: 
858: void DroneScanner::perform_hybrid_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
859:     // Diamond Code Fix: Use constant instead of magic number
860:     if (scan_cycles_ % EDA::Constants::HYBRID_SCAN_DIVISOR == 0) {
861:         perform_wideband_scan_cycle(hardware);
862:     } else {
863:         perform_database_scan_cycle(hardware);
864:     }
865: }
866: 
867: // ============================================================================
868: // SCANNING FLOW: Detection Processing
869: // ============================================================================
870: // Flow: process_rssi_detection() -> DetectionRingBuffer -> update_tracked_drone()
871: //       -> detection_logger_.log_detection_async()
872: //
873: // Detection Algorithm:
874: // 1. Validate RSSI and frequency using DiamondCore utilities
875: // 2. Filter by drone bands (433MHz, 868/915MHz, 2.4GHz, 5.8GHz)
876: // 3. Classify threat level using ThreatClassifier::from_rssi()
877: // 4. Update detection ring buffer with hysteresis
878: // 5. Update tracked drone list if detection count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT
879: // 6. Log detection asynchronously (non-blocking)
880: //
881: // Thread Safety: Uses MutexLock for all shared data access
882: // Memory: Uses class member buffers to avoid stack allocation
883: void DroneScanner::process_rssi_detection(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi) {
884:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Using DiamondCore validation utilities
885:     // Guard clause: RSSI validation (using DiamondCore RSSI utilities)
886:     if (!EDA::Validation::validate_rssi(rssi)) {
887:         return;
888:     }
889: 
890:     // Guard clause: Frequency validation (using DiamondCore validation)
891:     if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
892:         return;
893:     }
894: 
895:     // Guard clause: Drone band filtering (433MHz - 5.8GHz)
896:     if (!EDA::Validation::is_433mhz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
897:         !EDA::Validation::is_2_4ghz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
898:         !EDA::Validation::is_5_8ghz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
899:         !EDA::Validation::is_military_band(entry.frequency_a)) {
900:         return;
901:     }
902: 
903:     // Determine parameters (locally)
904:     DroneType detected_type = DroneType::UNKNOWN;
905:     ThreatLevel threat_level = ThreatClassifier::from_rssi(rssi);
906: 
907:     // Simple database search (with mutex protection to prevent race with load_frequency_database)
908:     {
909:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
910:         // FIX: Use freq_db_ptr_ instead of freq_db_
911:         if (!freq_db_ptr_) return;
912:         for (size_t i = 0; i < freq_db_ptr_->entry_count(); ++i) {
913:             if ((*freq_db_ptr_)[i].frequency_a == entry.frequency_a) {
914:                 detected_type = DroneType::MAVIC;
915:                 threat_level = std::max(threat_level, ThreatLevel::MEDIUM);
916:                 break;
917:             }
918:         }
919:     }
920: 
921:     // Flag and data for deferred logging
922:     bool should_log = false;
923:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
924: 
925:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
926:     {
927:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
928: 
929:         // Diamond Code: Increment total_detections_ with mutex protection for thread safety
930:         // volatile uint32_t reads/writes are atomic on ARM Cortex-M4 (32-bit aligned)
931:         total_detections_++;
932: 
933:         // Guard clause: Prevent division by zero
934:         if (entry.frequency_a == EDA::Constants::ZERO_FREQUENCY) {
935:             return;
936:         }
937:         size_t freq_hash = DiamondFixes::safe_frequency_hash(entry.frequency_a);
938:         int32_t prev_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
939:         int32_t base_threshold = -90;
940: 
941:         if (rssi > -100 && rssi < -80) {
942:             base_threshold = -100;
943:         } else if (rssi > -80) {
944:             base_threshold = -90;
945:         }
946: 
947:         if (prev_rssi < base_threshold) {
948:             base_threshold += HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
949:         }
950: 
951:         if (rssi >= base_threshold) {
952:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
953:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
954: 
955:             // Write to buffer (safe)
956:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, current_count, rssi});
957: 
958:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
959:                 // We DON'T write log here. We only prepare data.
960:                 should_log = true;
961: 
962:                 // Prepare log data
963:                 log_entry_to_write.timestamp = chTimeNow();
964:                 // DIAMOND FIX: Type Consistency - Use uint64_t for frequency
965:                 log_entry_to_write.frequency_hz = static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a);
966:                 log_entry_to_write.rssi_db = rssi;
967:                 log_entry_to_write.threat_level = threat_level;
968:                 log_entry_to_write.drone_type = detected_type;
969:                 log_entry_to_write.detection_count = current_count;
970:                 log_entry_to_write.confidence_percent = 85;
971:                 // (  RSSI )
972:                 log_entry_to_write.width_bins = 0;
973:                 log_entry_to_write.signal_width_hz = 0;
974:                 log_entry_to_write.snr = 0;
975: 
976:                 // Update drone tracking for UI
977:                 update_tracked_drone({detected_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(rssi), threat_level});
978:             }
979:         } else {
980:             // "Leaky bucket" logic
981:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
982:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
983: 
984:             if (current_count > 0) {
985:                 current_count--;
986:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi});
987:             } else {
988:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection({freq_hash, 0, -120});
989:             }
990:         }
991:     }
992:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
993:     // Mutex released. UI can redraw.
994: 
995:         // Perform heavy I/O operations
996:     if (should_log) {
997:         // Only log every 200ms to prevent I/O blocking while maintaining responsiveness
998:         systime_t now = chTimeNow();
999: 
1000:         // FIX #15: Use consistent memory ordering
1001:         systime_t last_time = last_detection_log_time_;
1002: 
1003:         // Use chTimeNow() directly for timing - no CH_CFG_ST_FREQUENCY dependency
1004:         // DIAMOND FIX: Priority 2 - Replace magic number with constant
1005:         if (now - last_time > EDA::Constants::LOG_WRITE_INTERVAL_MS) { // 200ms delay (10x more frequent than before)
1006:             if (detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
1007:                 // log_detection_async returns false if buffer is full
1008:                 // so built-in protection against hanging is already inside the logger.
1009:                 if (detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write)) {
1010:                     last_detection_log_time_ = now;
1011:                 }
1012:             }
1013:         }
1014:     }
1015: }
1016: 
1017: void DroneScanner::send_drone_detection_message(const DetectionParams& params) {
1018:     // Only update internal data - UI will read via snapshot
1019:     update_tracked_drone(params);
1020: }
1021: 
1022: // ============================================================================
1023: // SCANNING FLOW: Tracked Drone Update
1024: // ============================================================================
1025: // Flow: update_tracked_drone() -> TrackedDrone::add_rssi() -> update_tracking_counts()
1026: //
1027: // Tracked Drone Management:
1028: // - MAX_TRACKED_DRONES (10) fixed-size array (zero heap allocation)
1029: // - Each TrackedDrone stores MAX_HISTORY (3) RSSI samples for trend calculation
1030: // - Oldest entry replaced when array is full
1031: //
1032: // Thread Safety: Called from scanner thread, data protected by data_mutex
1033: // Memory: Uses placement new on static storage (tracked_drones_storage_)
1034: void DroneScanner::update_tracked_drone(const DetectionParams& params) {
1035:     // Only update internal data - UI will read via snapshot
1036:     // Single mutex lock acquisition at the start
1037:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1038:     
1039:     Frequency frequency = params.frequency_hz;
1040:     DroneType type = params.type;
1041:     int32_t rssi = params.rssi_db;
1042:     ThreatLevel threat_level = params.threat_level;
1043:     
1044:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1045:         if (DiamondFixes::frequency_equal(tracked_drones()[i].frequency, frequency) && tracked_drones()[i].update_count > 0) {
1046:             tracked_drones()[i].add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1047:             tracked_drones()[i].drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1048:             tracked_drones()[i].threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1049:             update_tracking_counts();
1050:             return;
1051:         }
1052:     }
1053: 
1054:     if (tracked_count_ < EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES) {
1055:         TrackedDrone new_drone;
1056:         new_drone.frequency = static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency);
1057:         new_drone.drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1058:         new_drone.threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1059:         new_drone.add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1060:         tracked_drones()[tracked_count_] = new_drone;
1061:         tracked_count_++;
1062:         update_tracking_counts();
1063:         return;
1064:     }
1065: 
1066:     // Array full - replace oldest entry
1067:     size_t oldest_index = 0;
1068:     systime_t oldest_time = tracked_drones()[0].last_seen;
1069: 
1070:     for (size_t i = 1; i < tracked_count_; i++) {
1071:         if (tracked_drones()[i].last_seen < oldest_time) {
1072:             oldest_time = tracked_drones()[i].last_seen;
1073:             oldest_index = i;
1074:         }
1075:     }
1076: 
1077:     TrackedDrone& oldest_drone = tracked_drones()[oldest_index];
1078:     oldest_drone = TrackedDrone();
1079:     oldest_drone.frequency = static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency);
1080:     oldest_drone.drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1081:     oldest_drone.threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1082:     oldest_drone.add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1083: }
1084: 
1085: void DroneScanner::remove_stale_drones() {
1086:     // Stack overflow detection check
1087:     if (!check_stack_canary()) {
1088:         // Stack overflow detected - reinitialize canary to prevent further corruption
1089:         init_stack_canary();
1090:     }
1091: 
1092:     const systime_t STALE_TIMEOUT = EDA::Constants::STALE_DRONE_TIMEOUT_MS;
1093:     systime_t current_time = chTimeNow();
1094: 
1095:     // Single lock for atomicity of identify-and-remove operation
1096:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1097: 
1098:     stale_indices_.fill(0);
1099:     size_t stale_count = 0;
1100: 
1101:     // Step 1: Identify stale drones
1102:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1103:         if (tracked_drones()[i].update_count > 0 &&
1104:             (current_time - tracked_drones()[i].last_seen) > STALE_TIMEOUT) {
1105:             stale_indices_[stale_count++] = i;
1106:         }
1107:     }
1108: 
1109:     // Step 2: Exit early if no stale drones
1110:     if (stale_count == 0) return;
1111: 
1112:     // Step 3: Compact array
1113:     size_t write_index = 0;
1114:     size_t num_valid = 0;
1115: 
1116:     // Use class member variable instead of stack allocation (heap-free)
1117:     // Reset is_stale array
1118:     for (size_t i = 0; i < EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1119:         is_stale_[i] = 0;
1120:     }
1121:     for (size_t i = 0; i < stale_count; ++i) {
1122:         if (stale_indices_[i] < tracked_count_) {
1123:             is_stale_[stale_indices_[i]] = 1;
1124:         }
1125:     }
1126: 
1127:     for (size_t read_index = 0; read_index < tracked_count_; ++read_index) {
1128:         if (!is_stale_[read_index]) {
1129:             if (write_index != read_index) {
1130:                 tracked_drones()[write_index] = tracked_drones()[read_index];
1131:             }
1132:             write_index++;
1133:             num_valid++;
1134:         }
1135:     }
1136:     tracked_count_ = num_valid;
1137: 
1138:     // Step 4: Update tracking counts
1139:     if (tracked_count_ > 0) {
1140:         update_tracking_counts();
1141:     } else {
1142:         approaching_count_ = 0;
1143:         receding_count_ = 0;
1144:         static_count_ = 0;
1145:     }
1146: }
1147: 
1148: // LUT lookup for update_tracking_counts() (saves ~60 bytes Flash)
1149: void DroneScanner::update_tracking_counts() {
1150:     approaching_count_ = 0;
1151:     receding_count_ = 0;
1152:     static_count_ = 0;
1153: 
1154:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1155:         if (tracked_drones()[i].update_count < 2) continue;
1156: 
1157:         MovementTrend trend = tracked_drones()[i].get_trend();
1158:         // LUT lookup for O(1) time
1159:         uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(trend);
1160:         if (idx < 4) {
1161:             (this->*DroneScanner::TREND_COUNTERS[idx])++;
1162:         }
1163:     }
1164: }
1165: 
1166: void DroneScanner::reset_scan_cycles() {
1167:     scan_cycles_ = 0;
1168: }
1169: 
1170: void DroneScanner::switch_to_real_mode() {
1171:     is_real_mode_ = true;
1172: }
1173: 
1174: void DroneScanner::switch_to_demo_mode() {
1175:     is_real_mode_ = false;
1176: }
1177: 
1178: void DroneScanner::initialize_database_and_scanner() {
1179:     // Aligned storage for FreqmanDB (compile-time size, no heap fragmentation)
1180: 
1181:     // Runtime alignment verification before reinterpret_cast
1182:     if (reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(freq_db_storage_) % alignof(FreqmanDB) != 0) {
1183:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1184:         handle_scan_error("Memory: freq_db_storage_ alignment error");
1185:         return;
1186:     }
1187: 
1188:     // Use reinterpret_cast on aligned buffer
1189:     freq_db_ptr_ = reinterpret_cast<FreqmanDB*>(freq_db_storage_);
1190: 
1191:     // Guard clause: validate reinterpret_cast succeeded
1192:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1193:         handle_scan_error("Memory: FreqmanDB reinterpret_cast failed");
1194:         return;
1195:     }
1196: 
1197:     // Mark freq_db as constructed
1198:     freq_db_constructed_ = true;
1199: 
1200:     // Runtime alignment verification for tracked_drones storage
1201:     if (reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(tracked_drones_storage_) % alignof(TrackedDrone) != 0) {
1202:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones_storage_ alignment error");
1203:         // Only call destructor if construction succeeded
1204:         if (freq_db_constructed_) {
1205:             freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1206:             freq_db_constructed_ = false;
1207:         }
1208:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1209:         return;
1210:     }
1211: 
1212:     // Create TrackedDrone array in static storage
1213:     tracked_drones_ptr_ = new (tracked_drones_storage_)
1214:         std::array<TrackedDrone, EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>();
1215:     if (!tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1216:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones placement new failed");
1217:         // Only call destructor if construction succeeded
1218:         if (freq_db_constructed_) {
1219:             freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1220:             freq_db_constructed_ = false;
1221:         }
1222:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1223:         return;
1224:     }
1225:     
1226:     // Mark tracked_drones as constructed
1227:     tracked_drones_constructed_ = true;
1228: 
1229:     // TrackedDrone
1230:     for (auto& drone : *tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1231:         drone = TrackedDrone();  // Default construct
1232:     }
1233: 
1234:     // Initialize database with built-in frequencies as fallback
1235:     // This ensures scanner has valid data even if SD card is not ready
1236:     {
1237:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1238: 
1239:         // Try to open DRONES database first
1240:         auto db_path = get_freqman_path(settings_.freqman_path);
1241:         bool db_opened = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
1242: 
1243:         if (!db_opened || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
1244:             // If database doesn't exist or is empty, try to create it with built-in frequencies
1245:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
1246: 
1247:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
1248:                 // FIX: Validate frequency before adding to database
1249:                 if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(item.freq)) {
1250:                     continue;  // Skip invalid frequencies
1251:                 }
1252:                 
1253:                 freqman_entry entry{};
1254:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
1255:                 entry.description = item.desc;
1256:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
1257:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
1258:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
1259:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
1260:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
1261:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
1262:             }
1263: 
1264:             current_db_index_ = 0;
1265:         }
1266: 
1267:         freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1268:     }
1269: 
1270:     // Mark initialization as complete
1271:     initialization_complete_ = true;
1272: }
1273: 
1274: void DroneScanner::sync_database() {
1275:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1276:     
1277:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1278:         return;
1279:     }
1280:     
1281:     // FreqmanDB auto-syncs on every write operation
1282: }
1283: 
1284: void DroneScanner::cleanup_database_and_scanner() {
1285:     sync_database();
1286: 
1287:     bool was_loading = db_loading_active_;
1288:     db_loading_active_ = false;
1289:     if (was_loading) {
1290:         if (db_loading_thread_ != nullptr) {
1291:             chThdWait(db_loading_thread_);
1292:             db_loading_thread_ = nullptr;
1293:         }
1294:     }
1295: 
1296:     // Stop detection logger worker thread
1297:     detection_logger_.stop_worker();
1298: 
1299:     // Explicit destructor calls for placement new
1300:     // Only call destructor if construction succeeded
1301:     if (tracked_drones_ptr_ != nullptr && tracked_drones_constructed_) {
1302:         tracked_drones_ptr_->std::array<TrackedDrone, EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>::~array();
1303:         tracked_drones_constructed_ = false;
1304:         tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1305:     }
1306: 
1307:     // Only call destructor if construction succeeded
1308:     if (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr && freq_db_constructed_) {
1309:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1310:         freq_db_constructed_ = false;
1311:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1312:     }
1313:     
1314:     // Clear detection ring buffer
1315:     detection_ring_buffer_.clear();
1316:     
1317:     // ChibiOS mutexes auto-cleaned with the object
1318: }
1319: 
1320: // Async database loading to prevent UI freeze
1321: msg_t DroneScanner::db_loading_thread_entry(void* arg) {
1322:     static_cast<DroneScanner*>(arg)->db_loading_thread_loop();
1323:     return 0;
1324: }
1325: 
1326: void DroneScanner::db_loading_thread_loop() {
1327:     // Use same static storage for async initialization
1328:     // Check if already initialized
1329:     if (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr || tracked_drones_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1330:         handle_scan_error("DB already initialized");
1331:         db_loading_active_ = false;
1332:         return;
1333:     }
1334: 
1335:     // Use reinterpret_cast on aligned buffer
1336:     if (reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(freq_db_storage_) % alignof(FreqmanDB) != 0) {
1337:         handle_scan_error("Memory: freq_db_storage_ alignment error (async)");
1338:         db_loading_active_ = false;
1339:         return;
1340:     }
1341:     freq_db_ptr_ = reinterpret_cast<FreqmanDB*>(freq_db_storage_);
1342:     // FIX #M1: Remove meaningless null check after reinterpret_cast
1343:     // reinterpret_cast from a valid pointer never returns nullptr
1344:     // Alignment check above is sufficient
1345: 
1346:     // Runtime alignment verification for tracked_drones_storage_
1347:     if (reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(tracked_drones_storage_) % alignof(std::array<TrackedDrone, EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>) != 0) {
1348:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones_storage_ alignment error (async)");
1349:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1350:         db_loading_active_ = false;
1351:         return;
1352:     }
1353: 
1354:     // Use reinterpret_cast on aligned buffer
1355:     tracked_drones_ptr_ = reinterpret_cast<std::array<TrackedDrone, EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>*>(tracked_drones_storage_);
1356:     // FIX #M2: Remove meaningless null check after reinterpret_cast
1357:     // reinterpret_cast from a valid pointer never returns nullptr
1358:     // Alignment check above is sufficient
1359: 
1360:     // Initialize elements
1361:     for (auto& drone : *tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1362:         drone = TrackedDrone();
1363:     }
1364: 
1365:     // Set tracked_drones_constructed_ flag after initialization
1366:     tracked_drones_constructed_ = true;
1367: 
1368:     bool db_success = false;
1369:     auto db_path = get_freqman_path(settings_.freqman_path);
1370: 
1371:     systime_t load_start = chTimeNow();
1372: 
1373:     // SD mount timeout logic with proper resource cleanup
1374:     systime_t start_time = chTimeNow();
1375:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1376:         if (chTimeNow() - start_time > MS2ST(EDA::Constants::SD_CARD_MOUNT_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
1377:             handle_scan_error("SD card not ready");
1378:             db_loading_active_ = false;
1379:             // Ensure proper cleanup of placement-newed objects on timeout
1380:             if (freq_db_ptr_ && freq_db_constructed_) {
1381:                 freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1382:                 freq_db_constructed_ = false;
1383:                 freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1384:             }
1385:             if (tracked_drones_ptr_ && tracked_drones_constructed_) {
1386:                 tracked_drones_ptr_->std::array<TrackedDrone, EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>::~array();
1387:                 tracked_drones_constructed_ = false;
1388:                 tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1389:             }
1390:             // FIX #16: Always reset initialization complete flag on error
1391:             initialization_complete_ = false;
1392:             freq_db_loaded_ = false;  // Also reset database loaded flag
1393:             return;
1394:         }
1395:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(EDA::Constants::SD_CARD_POLL_INTERVAL_MS);
1396:     }
1397: 
1398:     // Maintain proper lock order: DATA_MUTEX  SD_CARD_MUTEX
1399:     bool should_load = db_loading_active_;
1400:     if (should_load) {
1401:         // FIX: Defensive null check before dereferencing freq_db_ptr_
1402:         // This provides additional safety if initialization somehow fails
1403:         if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1404:             handle_scan_error("Database pointer is null during async loading");
1405:             db_loading_active_ = false;
1406:             return;
1407:         }
1408:         db_success = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
1409: 
1410:         if (db_success) {
1411:             systime_t load_time = chTimeNow() - load_start;
1412:             if (load_time > MS2ST(DB_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
1413:                 handle_scan_error("Database load timeout");
1414:                 db_loading_active_ = false;
1415:                 // FIX #4 & #6: Ensure proper cleanup of placement-newed objects on timeout
1416:                 // Only call destructors if construction succeeded
1417:                 if (freq_db_ptr_ && freq_db_constructed_) {
1418:                     freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1419:                     freq_db_constructed_ = false;
1420:                     freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1421:                 }
1422:             if (tracked_drones_ptr_ && tracked_drones_constructed_) {
1423:                 tracked_drones_ptr_->std::array<TrackedDrone, EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>::~array();
1424:                 tracked_drones_constructed_ = false;
1425:                 tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1426:             }
1427:                 initialization_complete_ = false;
1428:                 freq_db_loaded_ = false;
1429:                 return;
1430:             }
1431: 
1432:             // FIX #H1: Set flags when database loads successfully on first attempt
1433:             // If db_success is true and database is not empty, the code below
1434:             // (lines 1408-1467) won't execute, leaving initialization_complete_ and
1435:             // freq_db_constructed_ flags unset. This causes is_initialization_complete()
1436:             // to always return false, preventing phases 3-6 from completing.
1437:             // FIX: Defensive null check before dereferencing freq_db_ptr_
1438:             if (freq_db_ptr_ && !freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
1439:                 freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1440:                 freq_db_constructed_ = true;
1441:                 initialization_complete_ = true;
1442:                 db_loading_active_ = false;
1443:                 return;
1444:             }
1445:         }
1446:     }
1447: 
1448:     bool should_init = db_loading_active_;
1449:     if (should_init && (!db_success || freq_db_ptr_->empty())) {
1450: 
1451:         // Phase 1: Acquire data_mutex for database modifications
1452:         {
1453:             MutexLock data_lock(data_mutex, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
1454:             
1455:             // FIX: Defensive null check before dereferencing freq_db_ptr_
1456:             // This provides additional safety if initialization somehow fails
1457:             if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1458:                 handle_scan_error("Database pointer is null during database initialization");
1459:                 db_loading_active_ = false;
1460:                 return;
1461:             }
1462:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
1463: 
1464:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
1465:                 bool still_loading = db_loading_active_;
1466:                 // DIAMOND FIX #6: Early return if loading was stopped externally
1467:                 // Note: No flag reset needed here - the caller who stopped loading
1468:                 // should have already reset the flags. This is a cooperative cancellation.
1469:                 if (!still_loading) {
1470:                     return;
1471:                 }
1472: 
1473:                 if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(item.freq)) {
1474:                     continue;  // Skip invalid frequencies
1475:                 }
1476: 
1477:                 freqman_entry entry{};
1478:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
1479:                 entry.description = item.desc;
1480:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
1481:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
1482:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
1483:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
1484:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
1485:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
1486:             }
1487: 
1488:             current_db_index_ = 0;
1489:             freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1490:         }  // data_lock released here
1491: 
1492:         // Phase 2: Acquire sd_card_mutex for sync_database()
1493:         {
1494:             MutexLock sd_lock(sd_card_mutex, LockOrder::SD_CARD_MUTEX);
1495:             sync_database();
1496:         }  // sd_lock released here
1497: 
1498:         // Set freq_db_constructed_ flag at end of thread
1499:         freq_db_constructed_ = true;
1500:         
1501:         // Set initialization_complete_ flag at end of thread
1502:         initialization_complete_ = true;
1503:     }
1504: }
1505: 
1506: // Async database loading (non-blocking UI)
1507: void DroneScanner::initialize_database_async() {
1508:     bool is_loading = db_loading_active_;
1509:     if (is_loading) {
1510:         return;  // Already loading or loaded
1511:     }
1512: 
1513:     // FIX: Initialize database and scanner BEFORE creating the loading thread
1514:     // This ensures freq_db_ptr_ and tracked_drones_ptr_ are properly initialized
1515:     // via placement new before any async operations begin, preventing M0 guru
1516:     // meditation errors from null pointer dereferences.
1517:     initialize_database_and_scanner();
1518: 
1519:     db_loading_active_ = true;
1520: 
1521:     // Use chThdCreateStatic instead of chThdCreateFromHeap
1522: 
1523:     db_loading_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
1524:         db_loading_wa_,                    // Working area
1525:         sizeof(db_loading_wa_),            // Size
1526:         NORMALPRIO - 2,                    // Priority
1527:         db_loading_thread_entry,           // Entry function
1528:         this                               // Argument
1529:     );
1530: 
1531:     // FIX #2: Verify stack size matches constant
1532:     static_assert(sizeof(db_loading_wa_) >= DroneScanner::DB_LOADING_STACK_SIZE,
1533:                  "db_loading_wa_ size mismatch with DB_LOADING_STACK_SIZE");
1534: 
1535:     // FIX #M5: Single thread creation check (removed duplicate)
1536:     // chThdCreateStatic with static stack should never fail, but handle gracefully
1537:     if (db_loading_thread_ == nullptr) {
1538:         handle_scan_error("Failed to create db_loading_thread");
1539:         db_loading_active_ = false;
1540:         freq_db_loaded_ = false;
1541:         return;  // Keep UI responsive - early return on failure
1542:     }
1543: }
1544: 
1545: // Check if async loading finished
1546: bool DroneScanner::is_database_loading_complete() const {
1547:     bool is_loading = db_loading_active_;
1548:     // FIX: Check that freq_db_ptr_ is not null in addition to checking freq_db_loaded_ flag
1549:     // This ensures the database is properly initialized before reporting completion
1550:     return !is_loading && freq_db_loaded_ && (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr);
1551: }
1552: 
1553: bool DroneScanner::is_initialization_complete() const {
1554:     return initialization_complete_;
1555: }
1556: 
1557: Frequency DroneScanner::get_current_scanning_frequency() const {
1558: 
1559:     if (!freq_db_ptr_ || !freq_db_loaded_) {
1560:         return 433000000;  // Default fallback frequency
1561:     }
1562: 
1563:     size_t db_entry_count = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
1564:     if (db_entry_count > 0 && current_db_index_ < db_entry_count) {
1565:         return (*freq_db_ptr_)[current_db_index_].frequency_a;
1566:     }
1567: 
1568:     return 433000000;  // Default fallback frequency
1569: }
1570: 
1571: Frequency DroneScanner::get_current_radio_frequency() const {
1572:     return get_current_scanning_frequency();
1573: }

1616:     ScannerStateSnapshot snapshot;
1617:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1618:     snapshot.max_detected_threat = max_detected_threat_;
1619:     snapshot.approaching_count = approaching_count_;
1620:     snapshot.static_count = static_count_;
1621:     snapshot.receding_count = receding_count_;

1630: TrackedDrone DroneScanner::getTrackedDrone(size_t index) const {
1631:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1632:     if (index < tracked_count_) {
1633:         return tracked_drones()[index];
1634:     }
1635:     return TrackedDrone{};
1636: }
1637: 
1638: void DroneScanner::handle_scan_error([[maybe_unused]] const char* error_msg) {
1639:     if (error_msg) {
1640:         last_scan_error_ = error_msg;
1641:     }
1642: }
1643: 
1644: DroneScanner::DroneSnapshot DroneScanner::get_tracked_drones_snapshot() const {
1645:     // Snapshot is point-in-time and may be stale
1646:     DroneSnapshot snapshot;
1647:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1648:     snapshot.count = tracked_count_;
1649:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_ && i < EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1650:         snapshot.drones[i] = tracked_drones()[i];
1651:     }
1652:     return snapshot;
1653: }
1654: 
1655: bool DroneScanner::try_get_tracked_drones_snapshot(DroneSnapshot& out_snapshot) const {
1656:     // FIX: Use RAII MutexTryLock for automatic unlock on all paths
1657:     // FIX #9: Snapshot is point-in-time and may be stale
1658:     // The lock is released when the function returns, so the returned data
1659:     // represents the state at the moment of the snapshot and may not reflect
1660:     // subsequent changes to tracked_drones_.
1661:     MutexTryLock lock(data_mutex);
1662: 
1663:     if (lock.is_locked()) {
1664:         out_snapshot.count = tracked_count_;
1665:         for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_ && i < EDA::Constants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1666:             out_snapshot.drones[i] = tracked_drones()[i];
1667:         }
1668:         return true;
1669:     }
1670:     return false;
1671: }
1672: 
1673:     // Implementation of safe read methods
1674: 
1675: int32_t DroneScanner::get_detection_rssi_safe(size_t freq_hash) const {
1676:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex); // Lock reading while scanner can write
1677:     return detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1678: }
1679: 
1680: uint8_t DroneScanner::get_detection_count_safe(size_t freq_hash) const {
1681:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1682:     return detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1683: }

1685: // DroneDetectionLogger implementations
1686: DroneDetectionLogger::DroneDetectionLogger()
1687:     : worker_thread_(nullptr),
1688:       mutex_(),
1689:       data_ready_(),
1690:       worker_should_run_(false),
1691:       csv_log_(),
1692:       session_active_(false),
1693:       session_start_(0),
1694:       logged_count_(0),
1695:       dropped_logs_(0),
1696:       header_written_(false),
1697:       ring_buffer_(),
1698:       head_(0),
1699:       tail_(0),
1700:       is_full_(false),
1701:       line_buffer_() {
1702:     chMtxInit(&mutex_);
1703:     memset(line_buffer_, 0, sizeof(line_buffer_));
1704:     
1705:     chSemInit(&data_ready_, 0);
1706:     
1707:     start_session();
1708: }
1709: 
1710: DroneDetectionLogger::~DroneDetectionLogger() {
1711:     stop_worker();
1712:     end_session();
1713: }
1714: 
1715: void DroneDetectionLogger::start_session() {
1716:     if (session_active_) return;
1717:     session_active_ = true;
1718:     session_start_ = chTimeNow();
1719:     logged_count_ = 0;
1720:     dropped_logs_ = 0;
1721:     header_written_ = false;
1722: }
1723: 
1724: void DroneDetectionLogger::end_session() {
1725:     if (!session_active_) return;
1726:     session_active_ = false;
1727: }
1728: 
1729: // Producer method - called by scanner thread
1730: bool DroneDetectionLogger::log_detection_async(const DetectionLogEntry& entry) {
1731:     MutexLock lock(mutex_);
1732:     if (is_full_) {
1733:         // Circular buffer - overwrite oldest entry
1734:         dropped_logs_++;
1735: 
1736:         // Overwrite oldest entry (tail position)
1737:         tail_ = (tail_ + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1738:     }
1739: 
1740:     size_t current_head = head_;
1741:     ring_buffer_[current_head] = entry;
1742:     head_ = (current_head + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1743: 
1744:     if (head_ == tail_) {
1745:         is_full_ = true;
1746:     }
1747: 
1748:     chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1749:     return true;
1750: }
1751: 
1752: void DroneDetectionLogger::start_worker() {
1753:     if (worker_thread_) return;
1754: 
1755:     worker_should_run_ = true;
1756:     // Create worker thread with static stack
1757:     worker_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
1758:         worker_wa_,
1759:         sizeof(worker_wa_),
1760:         NORMALPRIO - 1,
1761:         worker_thread_entry,
1762:         this
1763:     );
1764:     
1765:     static_assert(sizeof(worker_wa_) >= DroneDetectionLogger::WORKER_STACK_SIZE,
1766:                  "worker_wa_ size mismatch with WORKER_STACK_SIZE");
1767: 
1768:     if (worker_thread_ == nullptr) {
1769:         worker_should_run_ = false;
1770:         return;
1771:     }
1772: 
1773:     start_session();
1774: }
1775: 
1776: // Stack safety guard for embedded systems
1777: // DIAMOND FIX #C4 (REVISED): Stack canary on stack frame (not thread_local)
1778: namespace StackSafety {
1779:     // Stack canary magic value (stored in Flash)
1780:     constexpr uint32_t STACK_CANARY_MAGIC = 0xDEADBEEF;
1781: 
1782:     // Stack canary placed on stack (NOT thread_local)
1783:     class StackCanary {
1784:         uint32_t canary_value_;
1785:         
1786:     public:
1787:         // Initialize canary on construction (placed on stack)
1788:         StackCanary() noexcept : canary_value_(STACK_CANARY_MAGIC) {}
1789:         
1790:         // Check if canary was corrupted
1791:         bool is_valid() const noexcept {
1792:             return canary_value_ == STACK_CANARY_MAGIC;
1793:         }
1794:         
1795:         // Get canary value (for debugging)
1796:         uint32_t get_value() const noexcept {
1797:             return canary_value_;
1798:         }
1799:     };
1800: 
1801:     // Stack guard with RAII
1802:     class StackGuard {
1803:         StackCanary canary_;
1804:         const char* function_name_;
1805:         
1806:     public:
1807:         explicit StackGuard(const char* name) noexcept 
1808:             : canary_(), function_name_(name) {
1809:             // Canary initialized on stack
1810:         }
1811:         
1812:         ~StackGuard() noexcept {
1813:             if (!canary_.is_valid()) {
1814:                 // Stack overflow detected
1815:                 // Use lightweight handler (no logging to avoid recursion)
1816:                 handle_stack_overflow();
1817:             }
1818:         }
1819:         
1820:         bool is_stack_safe() const noexcept {
1821:             return canary_.is_valid();
1822:         }
1823:         
1824:         StackGuard(const StackGuard&) = delete;
1825:         StackGuard& operator=(const StackGuard&) = delete;
1826: 
1827:     private:
1828:         static void handle_stack_overflow() noexcept {
1829:             // Lightweight handler - no heap allocation, no logging
1830:             // Stack overflow detected - canary corrupted
1831:         }
1832:     };
1833: }
1834: 
1835: void DroneDetectionLogger::stop_worker() {
1836:     if (!worker_thread_) return;
1837: 
1838:     worker_should_run_ = false;
1839:     chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1840:     
1841:     // Thread termination timeout (1 second)
1842:     systime_t timeout = chTimeNow() + MS2ST(EDA::Constants::THREAD_TERMINATION_TIMEOUT_MS);  // 1 second timeout
1843:     while (chTimeNow() < timeout && worker_thread_ != nullptr) {
1844:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(EDA::Constants::THREAD_TERMINATION_POLL_INTERVAL_MS);  // Small sleep to yield CPU
1845:     }
1846:     worker_thread_ = nullptr;
1847:     
1848:     end_session();
1849: }
1850: 
1851: msg_t DroneDetectionLogger::worker_thread_entry(void* arg) {
1852:     static_cast<DroneDetectionLogger*>(arg)->worker_loop();
1853:     return 0;
1854: }
1855: 
1856: void DroneDetectionLogger::worker_loop() {
1857:     while (true) {
1858:         bool should_run = worker_should_run_;
1859:         if (!should_run) break;
1860: 
1861:         // Check initialization state - wait until initialization is complete
1862:         bool init_complete = initialization_complete_;
1863:         if (!init_complete) {
1864:             // FIX #L5: Use constant instead of magic number
1865:             chThdSleepMilliseconds(EDA::Constants::SD_CARD_POLL_INTERVAL_MS);
1866:             continue;
1867:         }
1868: 
1869:         // FIX #L4: Use constant instead of magic number (1 second timeout)
1870:         chSemWaitTimeout(&data_ready_, MS2ST(EDA::Constants::SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS));
1871:         
1872:         should_run = worker_should_run_;
1873:         if (!should_run) break;
1874: 
1875:         DetectionLogEntry entry_to_write;
1876:         bool has_data = false;
1877: 
1878:         {
1879:             MutexLock lock(mutex_);
1880:             // Diamond Code: Direct volatile access is safe because mutex_ provides thread safety
1881:             if (head_ != tail_ || is_full_) {
1882:                 entry_to_write = ring_buffer_[tail_];
1883:                 tail_ = (tail_ + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1884:                 is_full_ = false;
1885:                 has_data = true;
1886: 
1887:                 bool has_more_data = (head_ != tail_);
1888:                 // FIX #12: Signal semaphore while still holding mutex
1889:                 // This prevents race condition where buffer state changes between
1890:                 // checking has_more_data and signaling the semaphore
1891:                 if (has_more_data) {
1892:                     chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1893:                 }
1894:             }
1895:         }
1896: 
1897:         if (has_data) {
1898:             write_entry_to_sd(entry_to_write);
1899:         }
1900:     }
1901: }
1902: 
1903: constexpr systime_t SD_WRITE_TIMEOUT_MS = 1000;
1904: 
1905: bool DroneDetectionLogger::write_entry_to_sd(const DetectionLogEntry& entry) {
1906:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1907:         return false;
1908:     }
1909: 
1910:     // Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1911:     SDCardLock lock(sd_card_mutex);
1912: 
1913:     if (!ensure_csv_header()) return false;
1914: 
1915:     // Use class member buffer (reduces stack pressure)
1916:     int len = snprintf(line_buffer_, sizeof(line_buffer_),
1917:         "%" PRIu32 ",%" PRIu32 ",%" PRId32 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu32 ",%" PRIu8 "\n",
1918:         entry.timestamp,
1919:         static_cast<uint32_t>(entry.frequency_hz),
1920:         entry.rssi_db,
1921:         static_cast<uint8_t>(entry.threat_level),
1922:         static_cast<uint8_t>(entry.drone_type),
1923:         entry.detection_count,
1924:         entry.confidence_percent,
1925:         entry.width_bins,
1926:         static_cast<uint32_t>(entry.signal_width_hz),
1927:         entry.snr);
1928: 
1929:     if (len < 0 || static_cast<size_t>(len) >= sizeof(line_buffer_)) {
1930:         return false;
1931:     }
1932: 
1933:     // Add timeout to SD write operation
1934:     systime_t write_start = chTimeNow();
1935:     
1936:     // DIAMOND FIX: Zero-heap write using raw buffer
1937:     auto error = csv_log_.write_raw(line_buffer_, static_cast<File::Size>(len));
1938: 
1939:     systime_t write_time = chTimeNow() - write_start;
1940:     if (write_time > MS2ST(SD_WRITE_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
1941:     }
1942: 
1943:     if (error && error->ok()) {
1944:         logged_count_++;
1945:         return true;
1946:     }
1947:     return false;
1948: }
1949: 
1950: bool DroneDetectionLogger::ensure_csv_header() {
1951:     if (header_written_) return true;
1952: 
1953:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1954:         return false;
1955:     }
1956: 
1957:     // Static string literal stored in Flash
1958:     static const char* const header =
1959:         "timestamp_ms,frequency_hz,rssi_db,threat_level,drone_type,detection_count,confidence_percent,width_bins,signal_width_hz,snr\n";
1960: 
1961:     auto error = csv_log_.append(generate_log_filename());
1962:     if (error && !error->ok()) return false;
1963: 
1964:     // Zero-heap write using raw buffer
1965:     const size_t header_len = strlen(header);
1966:     error = csv_log_.write_raw(header, static_cast<File::Size>(header_len));
1967: 
1968:     if (error && error->ok()) {
1969:         header_written_ = true;
1970:         return true;
1971:     }
1972:     return false;
1973: }
1974: 
1975: // Return static const char* to eliminate heap allocation
1976: const char* DroneDetectionLogger::generate_log_filename() const {
1977:     return "EDA_LOG.CSV";
1978: }

2028: void DroneHardwareController::initialize_radio_state() {
2029:     // Load baseband coprocessor image before accessing receiver resources
2030:     baseband::run_image(portapack::spi_flash::image_tag_wideband_spectrum);
2031: 
2032:     // Add error handling for all radio operations
2033: 
2034:     receiver_model.enable();
2035:     receiver_model.set_modulation(ReceiverModel::Mode::SpectrumAnalysis);
2036:     receiver_model.set_sampling_rate(get_configured_sampling_rate());
2037:     receiver_model.set_baseband_bandwidth(get_configured_bandwidth());
2038:     receiver_model.set_squelch_level(0);
2039: 
2040:         // Use safe defaults - RF Amp controlled by user settings
2041:         receiver_model.set_rf_amp(false);
2042: 
2043:     // LNA Gain: 32dB (Range 0-40) - receives weak signals
2044:     receiver_model.set_lna(32);
2045: 
2046:     // VGA Gain: 32dB (Range 0-62) - signal volume after LNA
2047:     receiver_model.set_vga(32);
2048: 
2049: }

2074: void DroneHardwareController::set_spectrum_center_frequency(Frequency center_freq) {
2075:     // FIX: Validate frequency before setting
2076:     if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(center_freq)) {
2077:         // Invalid frequency - do nothing, keep previous value
2078:         return;
2079:     }
2080:     center_frequency_ = center_freq;
2081: }
2082: 
2083: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Using DiamondCore validation with overflow protection
2084: // DIAMOND FIX: Revision #8 - Add SPI Retry Logic (LOW)
2085: // Add 3-retry logic with 10ms delay for improved SPI communication reliability
2086: bool DroneHardwareController::tune_to_frequency(Frequency frequency_hz) {
2087:     // Validate frequency range using DiamondCore utilities
2088:     if (!EDA::Validation::validate_frequency(frequency_hz)) {
2089:         return false;
2090:     }
2091:     
2092:     // FIX #17: Removed impossible overflow check
2093:     // The check (frequency + 1MHz < frequency) is ALWAYS FALSE for unsigned arithmetic
2094:     // No overflow can occur with uint64_t addition of 1MHz to valid frequencies
2095:     
2096:     // 3-retry logic with 10ms delay for SPI reliability
2097:     constexpr uint8_t MAX_RETRIES = 3;
2098:     constexpr uint32_t RETRY_DELAY_MS = 10;
2099:     
2100:     for (uint8_t retry = 0; retry < MAX_RETRIES; ++retry) {
2101:         receiver_model.set_target_frequency(frequency_hz);
2102:         
2103:         // Delay between retries only
2104:         if (retry > 0) {
2105:             chThdSleepMilliseconds(RETRY_DELAY_MS);
2106:         }
2107:         
2108:         // Assume success if no exception occurs
2109:         return true;
2110:     }
2111:     
2112:     return false;
2113: }

2151: // ISR-safe: uses CriticalSection instead of mutex

2154:         spectrum_fifo_ = message->fifo;
2155:         if (spectrum_fifo_) {
2156:             ChannelSpectrum spectrum;
2157:             while (spectrum_fifo_->out(spectrum)) {
2158:                 process_channel_spectrum_data(spectrum);
2159:             }
2160:         }
2161:     }
2162: }

2177: void DroneHardwareController::process_channel_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
2178:     // ISR-safe: use critical section instead of mutex
2179:     CriticalSection lock;
2180: 
2181:     size_t count = std::min(spectrum.db.size(), last_spectrum_db_.size());
2182:     std::copy(spectrum.db.begin(), spectrum.db.begin() + count, last_spectrum_db_.begin());
2183: 
2184:     spectrum_updated_ = true;
2185: }
