2203: // UI Implementations
2204: 
2205: SmartThreatHeader::SmartThreatHeader(Rect parent_rect)
2206:     : View(parent_rect),
2207:       threat_progress_bar_({0, 0, screen_width, 16}),
2208:       threat_status_main_({0, 20, screen_width, 16}, "THREAT: LOW | <0 ~0 >0"),
2209:       threat_frequency_({0, 38, screen_width, 16}, "2400.0MHz SCANNING") {
2210:     last_text_[0] = '\0';
2211:     add_children({&threat_progress_bar_, &threat_status_main_, &threat_frequency_});
2212:     update(ThreatLevel::NONE, 0, 0, 0, 2400000000ULL, false);
2213: }
2214: 
2215: void SmartThreatHeader::update(ThreatLevel max_threat, size_t approaching, size_t static_count,
2216:                                 size_t receding, Frequency current_freq, bool is_scanning) {
2217:     // Check-Before-Update Pattern
2218:     bool data_changed = (max_threat != last_threat_) ||
2219:                         (is_scanning != last_is_scanning_) ||
2220:                         (current_freq != last_freq_) ||
2221:                         (approaching != last_approaching_) ||
2222:                         (static_count != last_static_) ||
2223:                         (receding != last_receding_);
2224: 
2225:     if (!data_changed) {
2226:     }
2227: 
2228:     last_threat_ = max_threat;
2229:     last_is_scanning_ = is_scanning;
2230:     last_freq_ = current_freq;
2231:     last_approaching_ = approaching;
2232:     last_static_ = static_count;
2233:     last_receding_ = receding;
2234: 
2235:     size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
2236:     threat_progress_bar_.set_value(total_drones * 10);
2237: 
2238:     // Use StatusFormatter with thread-local buffer
2239:     thread_local char buffer[64];
2240:     const char* threat_name = UnifiedStringLookup::threat_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat));
2241:     if (total_drones > 0) {
2242:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "THREAT: %s | <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2243:                                   threat_name,
2244:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(approaching),
2245:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(static_count),
2246:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(receding));
2247:     } else if (is_scanning) {
2248:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SCANNING: <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2249:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(approaching),
2250:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(static_count),
2251:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(receding));
2252:     } else {
2253:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "READY");
2254:     }
2255:     threat_status_main_.set(buffer);
2256:     threat_status_main_.set_style(&UIStyles::RED_STYLE);
2257:     snprintf(last_text_, sizeof(last_text_), "%s", buffer);
2258:     
2259:     // Cache text length to avoid strlen() in paint()
2260:     last_text_len_ = strlen(last_text_);
2261: 
2262:     // Use FrequencyFormatter
2263:     if (current_freq > 0) {
2264:         // Use thread-local buffer
2265:         thread_local char freq_buf[16];
2266:         FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), current_freq);
2267:         if (is_scanning) {
2268:             StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s SCANNING", freq_buf);
2269:         } else {
2270:             StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s READY", freq_buf);
2271:         }
2272:         threat_frequency_.set(buffer);
2273:     } else {
2274:         threat_frequency_.set("NO SIGNAL");
2275:     }
2276: 
2277:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified color mapping
2278:     static constexpr const Style* const THREAT_STYLES[5] = {
2279:         &UIStyles::LIGHT_STYLE,  // NONE (0)
2280:         &UIStyles::GREEN_STYLE,   // LOW (1)
2281:         &UIStyles::YELLOW_STYLE,  // MEDIUM (2)
2282:         &UIStyles::YELLOW_STYLE,  // HIGH (3)
2283:         &UIStyles::RED_STYLE      // CRITICAL (4)
2284:     };
2285:     uint8_t threat_idx = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat), static_cast<uint8_t>(4));
2286:     threat_frequency_.set_style(THREAT_STYLES[threat_idx]);
2287:     set_dirty();
2288: }

2350: ThreatCard::ThreatCard(size_t card_index, Rect parent_rect)
2351:     : View(parent_rect), card_index_(card_index),
2352:       parent_rect_(parent_rect), is_active_(false),
2353:       last_frequency_(0), last_threat_(ThreatLevel::NONE),
2354:       last_trend_(MovementTrend::UNKNOWN), last_rssi_(-120) {
2355:     last_threat_name_[0] = '\0';
2356:     add_children({&card_text_});

2359: // Use UnifiedStringLookup
2360: void ThreatCard::update_card(const DisplayDroneEntry& drone) {
2361:     // Check-Before-Update Pattern
2362:     bool data_changed = (drone.frequency != last_frequency_) ||
2363:                         (drone.threat != last_threat_) ||
2364:                         (drone.trend != last_trend_) ||
2365:                         (std::abs(drone.rssi - last_rssi_) > 1) || // RSSI hysteresis
2366:                         (strcmp(drone.type_name, last_threat_name_) != 0);
2367: 
2368:     if (!data_changed && is_active_) {
2369:     }
2370: 
2371:     last_frequency_ = drone.frequency;
2372:     last_threat_ = drone.threat;
2373:     last_trend_ = drone.trend;
2374:     last_rssi_ = drone.rssi;
2375:     snprintf(last_threat_name_, sizeof(last_threat_name_), "%s", drone.type_name);
2376:     is_active_ = true;
2377: 
2378:     // Use TrendSymbols for O(1) lookup
2379:     char trend_char = TrendSymbols::from_trend(static_cast<uint8_t>(drone.trend));
2380:     uint32_t mhz = drone.frequency / 1000000;
2381: 
2382:     // Use StatusFormatter with thread-local buffer
2383:     thread_local char buffer[48];
2384:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s %c %luM %ld",
2385:                              drone.type_name, trend_char,
2386:                              (unsigned long)mhz, (long)drone.rssi);
2387:     card_text_.set(buffer);
2388:     
2389:     // Static style (not created on stack each call)
2390:     static const Style CARD_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2391:     card_text_.set_style(&CARD_STYLE);
2392:     
2393:     set_dirty();
2394: }
2395:

2399:     set_dirty();
2400: }

2428: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_scanning_progress(uint32_t progress_percent, uint32_t total_cycles, uint32_t detections) {
2429:     // Early return for invalid states
2430:     if (progress_percent > 100) progress_percent = 100;
2431: 
2432:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::SCANNING);
2433: 
2434:     // Table-driven progress bar - O(1) lookup
2435:     uint8_t raw_idx = (progress_percent * 8) / 100;
2436:     uint8_t bar_idx = (raw_idx < 8) ? raw_idx : 8;
2437:     const auto& bar_entry = PROGRESS_PATTERNS[bar_idx];
2438: 
2439:     // Use StatusFormatter
2440:     char buffer[64];
2441:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s %lu%% C:%lu D:%lu",
2442:                              bar_entry.pattern, (unsigned long)progress_percent,
2443:                              (unsigned long)total_cycles, (unsigned long)detections);
2444:     progress_text_.set(buffer);
2445: 
2446:     // Style from constexpr LUT
2447:     static const Style SCANNING_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(STATUS_STYLES[0].bg_color)};
2448:     progress_text_.set_style(&SCANNING_STYLE);
2449: 
2450:     if (detections > 0) {
2451:         set_display_mode(DisplayMode::ALERT);
2452:         // FIX #4: Use thread-local buffer to reduce stack usage
2453:         thread_local char alert_buffer[64];
2454:         StatusFormatter::format_to(alert_buffer, "[!] DETECTED: %lu threats found!",
2455:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(detections));
2456:         alert_text_.set(alert_buffer);
2457: 
2458:         // Style from constexpr LUT
2459:         static const Style ALERT_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[0].bg_color)};
2460:         alert_text_.set_style(&ALERT_STYLE);
2461:     }
2462:     set_dirty();
2463: }
2464: 
2465: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_alert_status(ThreatLevel threat, size_t total_drones, const char* alert_msg) {
2466:     // Early return for invalid states
2467:     if (!alert_msg) return;
2468: 
2469:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::ALERT);
2470: 
2471:     // Unified icon and style mapping from constexpr LUT
2472:     size_t icon_idx = std::min(static_cast<size_t>(threat), size_t(4));
2473:     const char* alert_icon = ALERT_ICONS[icon_idx];
2474: 
2475:     // FIX #4: Use thread-local buffer to reduce stack usage
2476:     thread_local char buffer[64];
2477:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s ALERT: %lu drones | %s",
2478:                              alert_icon,
2479:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(total_drones),
2480:                              alert_msg);
2481:     alert_text_.set(buffer);
2482: 
2483:     // Table-driven style selection
2484:     // O(1) lookup  runtime : CRITICAL=0 (RED),  =1 (YELLOW)
2485:     static const Style ALERT_TEXT_STYLES[] = {
2486:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[0].bg_color)}, // CRITICAL (RED)
2487:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[1].bg_color)}  // MEDIUM (YELLOW)
2488:     };
2489:     size_t style_idx = (threat >= ThreatLevel::CRITICAL) ? 0 : 1;
2490:     alert_text_.set_style(&ALERT_TEXT_STYLES[style_idx]);
2491:     set_dirty();
2492: }
2493: 
2494: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_normal_status(const char* primary, const char* secondary) {
2495:     // Early return for invalid states
2496:     if (!primary) return;
2497:     
2498:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::NORMAL);
2499: 
2500:     // Use StatusFormatter
2501:     // Direct character check instead of strlen() - O(1) vs O(n)
2502:     char buffer[48];
2503:     if (!secondary || secondary[0] == '\0') {
2504:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s", primary);
2505:     } else {
2506:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s | %s", primary, secondary);
2507:     }
2508:     normal_text_.set(buffer);
2509:     
2510:     // Static style (not created on stack each call)
2511:     static const Style NORMAL_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2512:     normal_text_.set_style(&NORMAL_STYLE);
2513:     set_dirty();
2514: }
2515: 
2516: void ConsoleStatusBar::set_display_mode(DisplayMode mode) {
2517:     // Early return
2518:     if (mode_ == mode) return;
2519: 
2520:     mode_ = mode;
2521: 
2522:     // Bit mask instead of 3x bool comparison (more compact and faster)
2523:     static constexpr uint8_t VISIBILITY_MASK[3] = {
2524:         0b001, // NORMAL
2525:         0b010, // SCANNING
2526:         0b100  // ALERT
2527:     };
2528:     
2529:     uint8_t mask = VISIBILITY_MASK[static_cast<uint8_t>(mode)];
2530:     progress_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b010));
2531:     alert_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b100));
2532:     normal_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b001));
2533:     
2534:     set_dirty();
2535: }
2536: 
2537: void ConsoleStatusBar::paint(Painter& painter) {
2538:     View::paint(painter);
2539: 
2540:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(mode_);
2541:     const auto& layout = DISPLAY_MODE_LAYOUTS[mode_idx];
2542: 
2543:     if (layout.bar_color != 0x0000) {
2544:         painter.fill_rectangle({parent_rect_.left(), parent_rect_.top(), parent_rect().width(), 2}, Color(layout.bar_color));
2545:     }
2546: }

2552: // Implementation: process_frame_sync
2553: void DroneDisplayController::process_frame_sync() {
2554:     if (spectrum_fifo_) {
2555:         ChannelSpectrum spectrum;
2556:         while (spectrum_fifo_->out(spectrum)) {
2557:             this->process_mini_spectrum_data(spectrum);
2558:         }
2559:     }
2560: }

2562: DroneDisplayController::DroneDisplayController(Rect parent_rect)

2566:       text_threat_summary_({0, 82, screen_width, 16}, "THREAT: NONE"),
2567:       text_status_info_({0, 98, screen_width, 16}, "Ready"),
2568:       text_scanner_stats_({0, 114, screen_width, 16}, "No database"),
2569:        text_trends_compact_({0, 130, screen_width, 16}, ""),
2570:        text_drone_1_({screen_width - 120, 146, 120, 16}, ""),
2571:        text_drone_2_({screen_width - 120, 162, 120, 16}, ""),
2572:        text_drone_3_({screen_width - 120, 178, 120, 16}, ""),
2573:        text_signal_type_({screen_width - 80, 80, 80, 16}, "SIGNAL: --"),
2574:        compact_frequency_ruler_({0, 68, screen_width, 12}),

2578:              buffers_allocated_(false),
2579:             histogram_display_buffer_(),
2580:             histogram_dirty_(false),
2581:       // Initialize mutexes in member initialization list
2582:       // Lock order: SPECTRUM_MUTEX (level 1), HISTOGRAM_MUTEX (level 2)
2583:       spectrum_mutex_(),
2584:       histogram_mutex_(),
2585:             threat_bins_(), threat_bins_count_(0),
2586:              spectrum_gradient_(), spectrum_fifo_(nullptr),
2587:              pixel_index(0), bins_hz_size(0), each_bin_size(DEFAULT_EACH_BIN_SIZE_HZ), min_color_power(DEFAULT_MIN_COLOR_POWER),
2588:              marker_pixel_step(DEFAULT_MARKER_PIXEL_STEP_HZ), max_power(0), range_max_power(0), mode_(DroneDisplayController::DisplayRenderMode::SPECTRUM),
2589:              spectrum_config_()

2597:         &text_status_info_,
2598:         &text_scanner_stats_,
2599:         &text_trends_compact_,
2600:         &text_drone_1_,
2601:         &text_drone_2_,
2602:         &text_drone_3_,
2603:         &text_signal_type_
2604:     });
2605: }
2606: 
2607: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Buffer Management Methods
2608: // Diamond Code Principle: Zero heap allocation, use static storage
2609: // All buffers are allocated at compile time in .bss section
2610: // These methods manage the allocation state flag only
2611: 
2612: // Guard clause: Returns true if display buffers are marked as allocated
2613: bool DroneDisplayController::are_buffers_allocated() const {
2614:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Direct flag access (O(1), zero overhead)
2615:     // Static buffers are always present, only the flag needs checking
2616:     return buffers_allocated_;
2617: }
2618: 
2619: // Guard clause: Allocates display buffers (static, just marks as ready)
2620: bool DroneDisplayController::allocate_buffers_from_pool() {
2621:     // Early return if already allocated
2622:     if (buffers_allocated_) {
2623:         return true;  // Already allocated, success
2624:     }
2625: 
2626:     // Static buffers are pre-allocated at compile time
2627:     // Total: ~1.16 KB (all in static memory)
2628: 
2629:     buffers_allocated_ = true;
2630:     return true;  // Allocation successful
2631: }
2632: 
2633: // Guard clause: Returns true if display buffers are valid for use
2634: bool DroneDisplayController::are_buffers_valid() const {
2635:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Direct flag access (O(1), zero overhead)
2636:     // For static buffers, "valid" means "allocated and ready"
2637:     return buffers_allocated_;
2638: }
2639: 
2640: // Guard clause: Deallocates display buffers (static, just marks as not ready)
2641: void DroneDisplayController::deallocate_buffers() {
2642:     // Early return if not allocated
2643:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
2644:         return;  // Nothing to deallocate
2645:     }
2646: 
2647:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Static buffers don't need deallocation
2648:     // Just clear the flag to mark buffers as unavailable
2649:     // Buffers remain in .bss section, will be reused on next allocation
2650:     buffers_allocated_ = false;
2651: 
2652:     // Clear buffer contents to prevent stale data usage
2653:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Zero-initialize all buffers
2654:     std::fill(spectrum_power_levels().begin(), spectrum_power_levels().end(), 0);
2655: 
2656:     // DIAMOND FIX: Clear histogram display buffer
2657:     // Clear histogram buffer to prevent stale data usage
2658:     std::fill(std::begin(histogram_display_buffer_.bin_counts),
2659:               std::end(histogram_display_buffer_.bin_counts), 0);
2660: }
2661: 
2662: // ============================================================================
2663: // SCANNING FLOW: UI Update
2664: // ============================================================================
2665: // Flow: handle_scanner_update() -> update_detection_display() -> 
2666: //       get_tracked_drones_snapshot() -> sort_drones_by_rssi() -> render_drone_text_display()
2667: //
2668: // UI/DSP Separation Pattern (Diamond Code):
2669: // Phase 1: DATA FETCHING (DSP/Logic Layer) - no UI calls
2670: //   - Fetch all data from scanner into local DisplayData struct
2671: //   - Ensures atomic data fetching and consistent UI rendering
2672: // Phase 2: UI RENDERING (Presentation Layer) - no data fetching
2673: //   - Render UI using fetched data only
2674: //   - No scanner calls during rendering
2675: //
2676: // Thread Safety: Uses snapshot pattern to avoid holding mutex during render
2677: // Memory: Uses static thread_local buffers to avoid stack allocation
2678: void DroneDisplayController::update_detection_display(const DroneScanner& scanner) {
2679:     // Guard clause: Early return if buffers not allocated
2680:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
2681:         return;
2682:     }
2683:     
2684:     // Phase 1: DATA FETCHING (DSP/Logic Layer)
2685:     // Fetch all data from scanner into local variables
2686:     // This ensures no UI calls are made during data fetching
2687:     
2688:     DisplayData data;
2689:     data.is_scanning = scanner.is_scanning_active();
2690:     data.current_freq = scanner.get_current_scanning_frequency();
2691:     data.total_freqs = scanner.get_database_size();
2692:     data.max_threat = scanner.get_max_detected_threat();
2693:     data.approaching_count = scanner.get_approaching_count();
2694:     data.receding_count = scanner.get_receding_count();
2695:     data.static_count = scanner.get_static_count();
2696:     data.total_detections = scanner.get_total_detections();
2697:     data.is_real_mode = scanner.is_real_mode();
2698:     data.scan_cycles = scanner.get_scan_cycles();
2699:     data.has_detections = (data.approaching_count + data.receding_count + data.static_count) > 0;
2700:     
2701:     // Determine color index (logic only, no UI calls)
2702:     data.color_idx = (data.max_threat >= ThreatLevel::HIGH) ? 4 :
2703:                      (data.max_threat >= ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) ? 3 :
2704:                      (data.has_detections) ? 2 :
2705:                      (data.is_scanning) ? 1 : 0;
2706:     
2707:     // Phase 2: UI RENDERING (Presentation Layer)
2708:     // Render UI using fetched data only - no scanner calls
2709:     if (data.is_scanning) {
2710:         if (data.current_freq > 0) {
2711:             // Use static thread-local buffer instead of stack allocation (heap-free)
2712:             static thread_local char freq_buf[16]{};
2713:             FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), data.current_freq);
2714:             big_display_.set(freq_buf);
2715:         } else {
2716:             big_display_.set("2400.0MHz");
2717:         }
2718:     } else {
2719:         big_display_.set("READY");
2720:     }
2721: 
2722:     if (data.total_freqs > 0 && data.is_scanning) {
2723:         uint32_t progress_percent = 50;
2724:         scanning_progress_.set_value(std::min(progress_percent, static_cast<uint32_t>(100)));
2725:     } else {
2726:         scanning_progress_.set_value(0);
2727:     }
2728: 
2729:     if (data.has_detections) {
2730:         // Use static thread-local buffer instead of stack allocation (heap-free)
2731:         static thread_local char summary_buffer[48]{};
2732:         const char* threat_name = UnifiedStringLookup::threat_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(data.max_threat));
2733:         // Use StatusFormatter
2734:         StatusFormatter::format_to(summary_buffer, "THREAT: %s | <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2735:                                   threat_name,
2736:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(data.approaching_count),
2737:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(data.static_count),
2738:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(data.receding_count));
2739:         text_threat_summary_.set(summary_buffer);
2740:         text_threat_summary_.set_style(&UIStyles::RED_STYLE);
2741:     } else {
2742:         text_threat_summary_.set("THREAT: NONE | All clear");
2743:         text_threat_summary_.set_style(&UIStyles::GREEN_STYLE);
2744:     }
2745: 
2746:     // Use static thread-local buffer instead of stack allocation (heap-free)
2747:     static thread_local char status_buffer[48]{};
2748:     if (data.is_scanning) {
2749:         // Use const char* instead of std::string (saves RAM)
2750:         const char* mode_str = data.is_real_mode ? "REAL" : "DEMO";
2751:         StatusFormatter::format_to(status_buffer, "%s - Detections: %lu",
2752:                                   mode_str, static_cast<unsigned long>(data.total_detections));
2753:     } else {
2754:         StatusFormatter::format_to(status_buffer, "Ready - Enhanced Drone Analyzer");
2755:     }
2756:     text_status_info_.set(status_buffer);
2757: 
2758:     // Use static thread-local buffer instead of stack allocation (heap-free)
2759:     static thread_local char stats_buffer[48]{};
2760:     if (data.is_scanning && data.total_freqs > 0) {
2761:         size_t current_idx = 0;
2762:         // Use StatusFormatter
2763:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "Freq: %lu/%lu | Cycle: %lu",
2764:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(current_idx + 1),
2765:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(data.total_freqs),
2766:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(data.scan_cycles));
2767:     } else if (data.total_freqs > 0) {
2768:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "Loaded: %lu frequencies",
2769:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(data.total_freqs));
2770:     } else {
2771:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "No database loaded");
2772:     }
2773:     text_scanner_stats_.set(stats_buffer);
2774: 
2775:     // Use constexpr LUT (stored in Flash)
2776:     big_display_.set_style(&BIG_DISPLAY_STYLES[data.color_idx]);
2777: }
2778: 
2779: // Implementation: DroneDisplayController::set_scanning_status
2780: void DroneDisplayController::set_scanning_status(bool active, const char* message) {
2781:     // Early return for invalid states
2782:     if (!message) return;
2783:     
2784:     // Use StatusFormatter
2785:     char buffer[48];
2786:     if (active) {
2787:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SCAN: %s", message);
2788:         text_status_info_.set(buffer);
2789:         text_status_info_.set_style(&UIStyles::GREEN_STYLE);
2790:     } else {
2791:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "STOP: %s", message);
2792:         text_status_info_.set_style(&UIStyles::LIGHT_STYLE);
2793:     }
2794: }

2796: void DroneDisplayController::update_signal_type_display(const char* signal_type) {
2797:     if (!signal_type) return;
2798:     text_scanner_stats_.set(signal_type);
2799: }
2800: 
2801: void DroneDisplayController::add_detected_drone(Frequency freq, DroneType type, ThreatLevel threat, int32_t rssi) {
2802:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
2803: 
2804:     for (size_t i = 0; i < detected_drones_count_; ++i) {
2805:         if (detected_drones()[i].frequency == freq) {
2806:             detected_drones()[i].rssi = rssi;
2807:             detected_drones()[i].threat = threat;
2808:             detected_drones()[i].type = type;
2809:             detected_drones()[i].last_seen = now;
2810:             snprintf(detected_drones()[i].type_name, sizeof(detected_drones()[i].type_name), "%s", UnifiedStringLookup::drone_type_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(type)));
2811:             detected_drones()[i].display_color = UnifiedColorLookup::drone(static_cast<uint8_t>(type));
2812:             sort_drones_by_rssi();
2813:             render_drone_text_display();
2814:             return;
2815:         }
2816:     }
2817: 
2818:     if (detected_drones_count_ < MAX_UI_DRONES) {
2819:         auto& entry = detected_drones()[detected_drones_count_];
2820:         entry.frequency = freq;
2821:         entry.rssi = rssi;
2822:         entry.threat = threat;
2823:         entry.type = type;
2824:         entry.last_seen = now;
2825:         snprintf(entry.type_name, sizeof(entry.type_name), "%s", UnifiedStringLookup::drone_type_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(type)));
2826:         entry.display_color = UnifiedColorLookup::drone(static_cast<uint8_t>(type));
2827:         entry.trend = MovementTrend::STATIC;
2828:         detected_drones_count_++;
2829:     }
2830:     sort_drones_by_rssi();
2831:     render_drone_text_display();
2832: }
2833: 
2834: void DroneDisplayController::sort_drones_by_rssi() {
2835:     std::sort(detected_drones().begin(), detected_drones().end(),
2836:               [](const DisplayDroneEntry& a, const DisplayDroneEntry& b) {
2837:                   if (a.rssi != b.rssi) return a.rssi > b.rssi;
2838:                   if (a.threat != b.threat) return static_cast<int>(a.threat) > static_cast<int>(b.threat);
2839:                   return a.last_seen > b.last_seen;
2840:               });
2841: }
2842: 
2843: void DroneDisplayController::update_drones_display(const DroneScanner& scanner) {
2844:     // STEP 1: Get a safe copy of data
2845:     // Mutex is locked only for the copying time (microseconds)
2846:     auto snapshot = scanner.get_tracked_drones_snapshot();
2847: 
2848:     // Step 2: Work with local snapshot copy
2849: 
2850:     const systime_t STALE_TIMEOUT = 30000;
2851:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
2852: 
2853:     detected_drones_count_ = 0;
2854: 
2855:     for (size_t i = 0; i < snapshot.count; ++i) {
2856:         const auto& drone_data = snapshot.drones[i];
2857: 
2858:         // Stale check (duplicate logic for UI filtering)
2859:         if ((now - drone_data.last_seen) > STALE_TIMEOUT) continue;
2860: 
2861:         if (detected_drones_count_ < MAX_UI_DRONES) {
2862:             auto& entry = detected_drones()[detected_drones_count_];
2863:             entry.frequency = drone_data.frequency;
2864:             entry.type = static_cast<DroneType>(drone_data.drone_type);
2865:             entry.threat = static_cast<ThreatLevel>(drone_data.threat_level);
2866:             entry.rssi = drone_data.rssi;
2867:             entry.last_seen = drone_data.last_seen;
2868:             snprintf(entry.type_name, sizeof(entry.type_name), "%s", UnifiedStringLookup::drone_type_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(entry.type)));
2869:             entry.display_color = UnifiedColorLookup::drone(static_cast<uint8_t>(entry.type));
2870:             entry.trend = drone_data.get_trend();
2871:             detected_drones_count_++;
2872:         }
2873:     }
2874: 
2875:     // Step 3: Sorting and rendering
2876:     sort_drones_by_rssi();
2877: 
2878:     // Remaining code for updating display_drones_ and calling render
2879:     for (auto& drone : displayed_drones_) {
2880:         drone = DisplayDroneEntry{};
2881:     }
2882:     size_t count = std::min(detected_drones_count_, EDA::Constants::MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES);
2883:     for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
2884:         displayed_drones_[i] = detected_drones()[i];
2885:     }
2886:     highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(displayed_drones_);
2887:     render_drone_text_display();
2888: }
2889: 
2890: void DroneDisplayController::render_drone_text_display() {
2891:     text_drone_1_.set("");
2892:     text_drone_2_.set("");
2893:     text_drone_3_.set("");
2894: 
2895:     size_t drone_count = std::min(displayed_drones_.size(), EDA::Constants::MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES);
2896:     for (size_t i = 0; i < drone_count; ++i) {
2897:         const auto& drone = displayed_drones_[i];
2898:         char buffer[64];
2899:         char freq_buf[16];  // Local buffer instead of std::string (RAM savings)
2900: 
2901:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use TrendSymbols for O(1) lookup
2902:         char trend_symbol = TrendSymbols::from_trend(static_cast<uint8_t>(drone.trend));
2903: 
2904:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven frequency formatting ( if/else)
2905:         // O(1) lookup   if/else ( ~15  )
2906:         const auto& format_entry = FREQ_FORMAT_TABLE[
2907:             (drone.frequency >= 1000000000LL) ? 0 :
2908:             (drone.frequency >= 1000000LL) ? 1 :
2909:             (drone.frequency >= 1000LL) ? 2 : 3
2910:         ];
2911: 
2912:         int64_t int_part = drone.frequency / format_entry.divider;
2913:         int64_t dec_part = (format_entry.decimal_div > 1) ?
2914:                           (drone.frequency % format_entry.divider) / format_entry.decimal_div : 0;
2915: 
2916:         if (format_entry.decimal_div > 1) {
2917:             snprintf(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), format_entry.format,
2918:                      (unsigned long)int_part, (unsigned long)dec_part);
2919:         } else {
2920:             snprintf(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), format_entry.format,
2921:                      (unsigned long)int_part);
2922:         }
2923: 
2924:         // Use StatusFormatter
2925:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, DRONE_DISPLAY_FORMAT,
2926:                                  drone.type_name,
2927:                                  freq_buf,
2928:                                  (long int)drone.rssi,
2929:                                  trend_symbol);
2930: 
2931:         // Helper for indexed access (no bounds check each time)
2932:         Text* target = drone_text_widget(i);
2933:         if (target) {
2934:             target->set(buffer);
2935:         }
2936:     }
2937: }
2938: 
2939: void DroneDisplayController::process_mini_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
2940:     for (size_t bin = 0; bin < MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH; bin++) {
2941:         uint8_t current_bin_power;
2942:         if (bin < spectrum.db.size()) {
2943:             current_bin_power = spectrum.db[bin];
2944:         } else {
2945:             current_bin_power = 0;
2946:         }
2947:         if (process_bins(&current_bin_power)) {
2948:             return;
2949:         }
2950:     }
2951: }
2952: 
2953: bool DroneDisplayController::process_bins(uint8_t* powerlevel) {
2954:     bins_hz_size += each_bin_size;
2955:     if (bins_hz_size >= marker_pixel_step) {
2956:         // Thread-safe buffer access with mutex protection
2957:         // Lock order: DISPLAY_SPECTRUM_MUTEX (level 4)
2958:         MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_, LockOrder::SPECTRUM_MUTEX);
2959: 
2960:         if (pixel_index < spectrum_power_levels().size()) {
2961:             spectrum_power_levels()[pixel_index] = (*powerlevel > min_color_power) ? *powerlevel : 0;
2962:         }
2963:         *powerlevel = 0;
2964: 
2965:         if (!pixel_index) {
2966:             bins_hz_size = 0;
2967:             return true;
2968:         }
2969:         bins_hz_size -= marker_pixel_step;
2970:     }
2971:     return false;
2972: }

2974: void DroneDisplayController::render_bar_spectrum(Painter& painter) {
2975:     const auto& config = BarSpectrumConfig{};
2976: 
2977:     // Clear spectrum area
2978:     const int bar_spectrum_y_start = config.WATERFALL_Y_START;
2979:     const int spectrum_height = config.BAR_HEIGHT_MAX;
2980: 
2981:     painter.fill_rectangle(
2982:         {0, bar_spectrum_y_start, EDA::Constants::MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH, spectrum_height},
2983:         Color::black()
2984:     );
2985: 
2986:     // Validate buffer (static buffer)
2987:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
2988:         return;
2989:     }
2990: 
2991:     // Thread-safe buffer access with mutex protection
2992:     // Lock order: DISPLAY_SPECTRUM_MUTEX (level 4)
2993:         MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_, LockOrder::SPECTRUM_MUTEX);
2994: 
2995:     // Iterate through all spectrum bins
2996:     const auto& levels = spectrum_power_levels();
2997:     const size_t spectrum_width = std::min(levels.size(),
2998:                                         static_cast<size_t>(EDA::Constants::MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH));
2999: 
3000:     for (size_t x = 0; x < spectrum_width; ++x) {
3001:         uint8_t power = levels[x];
3002: 
3003:         // Noise filter: don't draw if signal too weak
3004:         if (power < config.NOISE_THRESHOLD) continue;
3005: 
3006:         // Calculate bar height (0-255  0-spectrum_height)
3007:         int bar_height = (power * spectrum_height) / 255;
3008:         if (bar_height < 1) bar_height = 1;
3009:         if (bar_height > spectrum_height) bar_height = spectrum_height;
3010: 
3011:         // Analyze signal shape (Narrow vs Wide)
3012:         size_t color_idx = get_bar_color_index(x, power);
3013: 
3014:         // Draw bar
3015:         int y_top = (bar_spectrum_y_start + spectrum_height) - bar_height;
3016:         painter.fill_rectangle(
3017:             {static_cast<int>(x), y_top, 1, bar_height},
3018:             config.BAR_COLORS[color_idx]
3019:         );
3020:     }
3021: }
3022: 
3023: // Histogram Display Implementation
3024: // Zero heap allocation, static storage, integer-only math
3025: 
3026: void DroneDisplayController::update_histogram_display(
3027:     const SpectralAnalyzer::HistogramBuffer& analysis_histogram,
3028:     uint8_t noise_floor
3029: ) noexcept {
3030:     // Guard clause: Validate input histogram
3031:     if (analysis_histogram.empty()) {
3032:         // Thread-safe buffer access with mutex protection
3033:         // Lock order: DISPLAY_HISTOGRAM_MUTEX (level 5)
3034:         MutexLock lock(histogram_mutex_, LockOrder::SPECTRUM_MUTEX);
3035:         histogram_display_buffer_.is_valid = false;
3036:         return;
3037:     }
3038: 
3039:     // Copy histogram data from analysis buffer to display buffer
3040:     // Scale from uint16_t to uint8_t (0-255) for display
3041:     uint8_t max_count = 0;
3042: 
3043:     // Thread-safe buffer access with mutex protection
3044:     // Lock order: DISPLAY_HISTOGRAM_MUTEX (level 5)
3045:         MutexLock lock(histogram_mutex_, LockOrder::SPECTRUM_MUTEX);
3046: 
3047:     for (size_t i = 0; i < HISTOGRAM_NUM_BINS; ++i) {
3048:         uint16_t raw_count = (i < analysis_histogram.size()) ? analysis_histogram[i] : 0;
3049:         histogram_display_buffer_.bin_counts[i] =
3050:             static_cast<uint8_t>(std::min(raw_count, static_cast<uint16_t>(255)));
3051: 
3052:         if (histogram_display_buffer_.bin_counts[i] > max_count) {
3053:             max_count = histogram_display_buffer_.bin_counts[i];
3054:         }
3055:     }
3056: 
3057:     histogram_display_buffer_.max_count = max_count;
3058:     histogram_display_buffer_.noise_floor = noise_floor;
3059:     histogram_display_buffer_.is_valid = true;
3060: 
3061:     histogram_dirty_ = true;
3062: }
3063: 
3064: void DroneDisplayController::render_histogram(Painter& painter) noexcept {
3065:     // DIAMOND FIX #5: Protect histogram_dirty_ with histogram_mutex_
3066:     // Thread-safe buffer access with mutex protection
3067:     // Lock order: SPECTRUM_MUTEX (level 2) for histogram data
3068:     MutexLock lock(histogram_mutex_, LockOrder::SPECTRUM_MUTEX);
3069: 
3070:     // Guard clause: Skip rendering if data hasn't changed
3071:     // Check is now protected by histogram_mutex_ to prevent race condition
3072:     if (!histogram_dirty_) {
3073:         return;
3074:     }
3075: 
3076:     // Guard clause: Skip if histogram data is invalid
3077:     if (!histogram_display_buffer_.is_valid) {
3078:         return;
3079:     }
3080: 
3081:     const auto& config = HistogramColorConfig{};
3082: 
3083:     // Clear histogram area
3084:     painter.fill_rectangle(
3085:         {0, HISTOGRAM_Y, HISTOGRAM_WIDTH, HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT},
3086:         Color::black()
3087:     );
3088: 
3089:     // Render 64 bins with color gradient
3090:     const uint8_t max_count = histogram_display_buffer_.max_count;
3091: 
3092:     // Guard clause: Skip rendering if max_count is zero
3093:     if (max_count == 0) {
3094:         histogram_dirty_ = false;
3095:         return;
3096:     }
3097: 
3098:     // Calculate scaling factor for bin height (0-255 -> 0-HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT)
3099:     // Diamond Code: Use 256 as divisor for fast bit shift approximation
3100:     const int scale_factor = HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT;
3101: 
3102:     for (size_t bin_idx = 0; bin_idx < HISTOGRAM_NUM_BINS; ++bin_idx) {
3103:         uint8_t bin_count = histogram_display_buffer_.bin_counts[bin_idx];
3104:         
3105:         // Skip empty bins
3106:         if (bin_count == 0) continue;
3107:         
3108:         // Calculate bin height (integer scaling)
3109:         int bin_height = (static_cast<int>(bin_count) * scale_factor) / 256;
3110:         if (bin_height < 1) bin_height = 1;
3111:         if (bin_height > HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT) bin_height = HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT;
3112:         
3113:         const int bin_x = static_cast<int>(bin_idx * HISTOGRAM_BIN_WIDTH);
3114:         const int bin_width = static_cast<int>(HISTOGRAM_BIN_WIDTH);
3115:         
3116:         // Calculate color level based on signal strength (integer-only)
3117:         uint8_t color_level;
3118:         if (bin_count <= HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_20PCT) {           // 0-20%
3119:             color_level = 0;  // dark_grey (noise floor)
3120:         } else if (bin_count <= HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_40PCT) {
3121:             color_level = 1;  // blue (low signal)
3122:         } else if (bin_count <= HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_60PCT) {
3123:             color_level = 2;  // cyan (medium signal)
3124:         } else if (bin_count <= HISTOGRAM_COLOR_THRESHOLD_80PCT) {
3125:             color_level = 3;  // yellow (high signal)
3126:         } else {
3127:             color_level = 4;  // red (peak signal)
3128:         }
3129:         
3130:         // Bounds check for color array
3131:         if (color_level >= config.NUM_COLOR_LEVELS) {
3132:             color_level = 4;
3133:         }
3134:         
3135:         const int y_top = (HISTOGRAM_Y + HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT) - bin_height;
3136:         painter.fill_rectangle(
3137:             {bin_x, y_top, bin_width, bin_height},
3138:             config.HISTOGRAM_COLORS[color_level]
3139:         );
3140:     }
3141:     
3142:     // Mark histogram as clean (rendered)
3143:     histogram_dirty_ = false;
3144: }
3145: 
3146: void DroneDisplayController::clear_histogram_area(Painter& painter) noexcept {
3147:     // DIAMOND FIX #4: Use class constants instead of hardcoded values
3148:     // Using class constants ensures consistency and maintainability
3149:     const Rect histogram_rect{
3150:         8,  // HISTOGRAM_X (not defined as class constant)
3151:         HISTOGRAM_Y,
3152:         HISTOGRAM_WIDTH,
3153:         HISTOGRAM_HEIGHT
3154:     };
3155: 
3156:     painter.fill_rectangle(histogram_rect, Color::black());
3157: }

3159: void DroneDisplayController::highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(const std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, EDA::Constants::MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES>& drones) {
3160:     threat_bins_count_ = 0;
3161:     for (const auto& drone : drones) {
3162:         if (drone.frequency > 0) {
3163:             size_t bin_x = frequency_to_spectrum_bin(drone.frequency);
3164:             if (bin_x < MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH && threat_bins_count_ < EDA::Constants::MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES) {
3165:                 threat_bins_[threat_bins_count_].bin = bin_x;
3166:                 threat_bins_[threat_bins_count_].threat = drone.threat;
3167:                 threat_bins_count_++;
3168:             }
3169:         }
3170:     }
3171: }

3173: void DroneDisplayController::clear_spectrum_buffers() {
3174:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
3175:         return;
3176:     }
3177:     std::fill(spectrum_power_levels().begin(), spectrum_power_levels().end(), 0);
3178: }
3179: 
3180: void DroneDisplayController::set_spectrum_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
3181:     if (min_freq >= max_freq || min_freq < EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ ||
3182:         max_freq > EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
3183:         spectrum_config_.min_freq = EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_24GHZ_MIN;
3184:         spectrum_config_.max_freq = EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_24GHZ_MAX;
3185:         update_frequency_ruler();
3186:         return;
3187:     }
3188:     spectrum_config_.min_freq = min_freq;
3189:     spectrum_config_.max_freq = max_freq;
3190:     spectrum_config_.bandwidth = (max_freq - min_freq) > EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_WIFI_MIN_WIDTH_HZ ?
3191:                                 EDA::Constants::WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_SLICE_WIDTH : static_cast<uint32_t>(max_freq - min_freq);
3192:     spectrum_config_.sampling_rate = spectrum_config_.bandwidth;
3193:     update_frequency_ruler();
3194: }
3195: 
3196: size_t DroneDisplayController::frequency_to_spectrum_bin(Frequency freq_hz) const {
3197:     const Frequency MIN_FREQ = spectrum_config_.min_freq;
3198:     const Frequency MAX_FREQ = spectrum_config_.max_freq;
3199:     const Frequency FREQ_RANGE = MAX_FREQ - MIN_FREQ;
3200:     if (freq_hz < MIN_FREQ || freq_hz > MAX_FREQ || FREQ_RANGE == 0) {
3201:         return MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH;
3202:     }
3203:     int64_t relative_freq = freq_hz - MIN_FREQ;
3204:     size_t bin = static_cast<size_t>((relative_freq * MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) / FREQ_RANGE);
3205:     return std::min(bin, static_cast<size_t>(MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH - 1));
3206: }

3329: void FrequencyRangeSetupView::focus() {

3337:                                        FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ);

3340:     field_max_.set_text(max_freq_buf);

3343:     char slice_buffer[32];
3344:     uint64_t slice_mhz = settings.wideband_slice_width_hz / 1000000;

3351: void FrequencyRangeSetupView::on_save() {
3352:     // Use const char* from get_text() reference (no new heap allocation)
3353:     const char* min_str = field_min_.get_text().c_str();
3354:     const char* max_str = field_max_.get_text().c_str();
3355:     
3356:     Frequency new_min = static_cast<Frequency>(DiamondCore::FrequencyParser::parse_mhz_string(min_str));
3357:     Frequency new_max = static_cast<Frequency>(DiamondCore::FrequencyParser::parse_mhz_string(max_str));
3358:     
3359:     // Input validation (integer-only)
3360:     if (new_min == 0 || new_max == 0) {
3361:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Invalid frequency format");
3362:         return;
3363:     }
3364:     
3365:     // Get slice width from settings
3366:     uint64_t new_slice_width = controller_.settings().wideband_slice_width_hz;
3367:     
3368:     // Validation - use unified constants from EDA::Constants
3369:     if (new_min >= new_max) {
3370:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Min freq must be < Max freq");
3371:         return;
3372:     }
3373:     
3374:     if (new_min < EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ || 
3375:         new_max > EDA::Constants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
3376:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Frequency out of range (1MHz - 7.2GHz)");
3377:         return;
3378:     }
3379:     
3380:     // Save settings (use existing settings reference)
3381:     controller_.settings().wideband_min_freq_hz = new_min;
3382:     controller_.settings().wideband_max_freq_hz = new_max;
3383: 
3384:     // Save to file with success check
3385:     if (!SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::save(controller_.settings())) {
3386:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Failed to save settings to SD card");
3387:         return;
3388:     }
3389:     
3390:     controller_.update_scanner_range(new_min, new_max);
3391:     
3392:     char buffer[64];
3393:     char min_freq_buf[32];
3394:     char max_freq_buf[32];
3395:     FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(min_freq_buf, sizeof(min_freq_buf), new_min, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
3396:     FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(max_freq_buf, sizeof(max_freq_buf), new_max, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
3397:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "Range updated:\n%s - %s\nBW: %lu MHz",
3398:                                min_freq_buf, max_freq_buf,
3399:                                (unsigned long)(new_slice_width / 1000000));
3400: 
3401:     nav_.display_modal("Success", buffer);
3402:     nav_.pop();
3403: }

3480: EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::~EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView() {

3482:     request_global_shutdown();
3483: 
3484:     // 1. Stop activity (in dependency order)
3485:     scanning_coordinator_.stop_coordinated_scanning();
3486:     scanner_.stop_scanning();
3487:     hardware_.shutdown_hardware();
3488: 
3489:     // Explicit buffer deallocation (before stack objects destroyed)
3490:     display_controller_.deallocate_buffers();
3491: 
3492:     // 2. Stack objects will be automatically destroyed in reverse order

3500: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::paint(Painter& painter) {
3501:     // Stack monitoring to prevent stack overflow
3502:     // paint() method uses ~1.6KB of stack per call
3503:     // STACK OPTIMIZATION: Reduced stack requirement to 1792 bytes (1.75KB)
3504:     StackMonitor stack_monitor;
3505:     constexpr size_t PAINT_STACK_REQUIRED = 1792;  // 1.75KB for paint() method (reduced from 2KB)
3506: 
3507:     // Guard clause: Return early if insufficient stack
3508:     if (!stack_monitor.is_stack_safe(PAINT_STACK_REQUIRED)) {
3509:         // Cannot safely render - skip this frame
3510:         return;
3511:     }
3512: 
3513:     // FIX:    paint
3514:     View::paint(painter);
3515: 
3516:     // FIX #2: Do NOT call step_deferred_initialization() from paint()
3517:     // This prevents nested stack frames that cause M0 stack overflow
3518:     // Initialization is now handled by continue_initialization() called from UI event loop
3519: 
3520:     // FIX:
3521:     if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3522:         painter.fill_rectangle({0, 0, screen_width, screen_height}, Color::black());
3523:         
3524:         // Error header
3525:         painter.draw_string({10, 80}, Style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::red(), Color::black()}, "INIT ERROR");
3526:         
3527:         // Error message
3528:         painter.draw_string({10, 100}, Style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::white(), Color::black()}, 
3529:                            ERROR_MESSAGES[static_cast<uint8_t>(init_error_)]);
3530:         
3531:         // Instructions
3532:         painter.draw_string({10, 130}, Style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::yellow(), Color::black()}, "Press BACK to exit");
3533:         return;
3534:     }
3535:     
3536:     // FIX:
3537:     if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
3538:         size_t phase_idx = static_cast<size_t>(init_state_);
3539:         if (phase_idx < 7) {
3540:             painter.draw_string({10, 80}, Style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::white(), Color::black()}, "Loading...");
3541:             painter.draw_string({10, 100}, Style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::green(), Color::black()}, 
3542:                                INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[phase_idx]);
3543:             
3544:             // Progress bar (6 phases = 16.6% each)
3545:             uint8_t progress = static_cast<uint8_t>(phase_idx * 16);
3546:             if (progress > 100) progress = 100;
3547:             
3548:             // Progress bar background
3549:             painter.fill_rectangle({10, 120, 100, 10}, Color::dark_grey());
3550:             // Filled portion
3551:             painter.fill_rectangle({10, 120, progress, 10}, Color::green());
3552:         }
3553:         return;
3554:     }
3555: 
3556:     // Additional buffer check
3557:     if (display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
3558:         display_controller_.render_bar_spectrum(painter);
3559: 
3560:         // Handle histogram display based on mode
3561:         if (display_controller_.get_display_mode() == ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::DroneDisplayController::DisplayRenderMode::HISTOGRAM) {
3562:             // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Render histogram after bar spectrum
3563:             // Histogram is positioned at y=164-190 (below bar spectrum)
3564:             display_controller_.render_histogram(painter);
3565:         } else {
3566:             // Clear histogram area when not in histogram mode
3567:             display_controller_.clear_histogram_area(painter);
3568:         }
3569:     }
3570: 
3571:     // Stack Overflow Prevention: Do NOT call continue_initialization() from paint()!
3572:     // Calling continue_initialization() from paint() creates nested stack frames that
3573:     // exceed the 4KB stack limit. The message_handler_frame_sync_ already handles
3574:     // initialization by calling step_deferred_initialization() from the UI event loop,
3575:     // not from paint(). The initialization continues naturally via the frame sync handler.
3576: }

3604: 
3605: // Phase names for logging
3606: static const char* const PHASE_NAMES[] = {
3607:     "ALLOC",      // Phase 0: Buffer allocation
3608:     "DB_LOAD",    // Phase 1: Database loading
3609:     "HW_INIT",    // Phase 2: Hardware initialization
3610:     "UI_SETUP",    // Phase 3: UI setup
3611:     "SETTINGS",    // Phase 4: Settings loading
3612:     "FINALIZE"     // Phase 5: Finalization
3613: };

3616: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::update_init_progress_display() {
3617:     // CRITICAL FIX: Update start button text during initialization
3618:     // Note: Button class doesn't have set_enabled() method.
3619:     // Button is protected by init_state_ check in handle_start_stop_button()
3620:     if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
3621:         button_start_stop_.set_text("INITIALIZING...");
3622:     } else {
3623:         button_start_stop_.set_text("START/STOP");
3624:     }
3625:     
3626:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT  Flash  switch ( 3057-3077)
3627:     size_t state_idx = static_cast<size_t>(init_state_);
3628:     
3629:     // Bounds-checked array access
3630:     constexpr size_t MAX_STATE_IDX = 8;  // INITIALIZATION_ERROR = 8
3631:     if (state_idx > MAX_STATE_IDX) {
3632:         state_idx = MAX_STATE_IDX;  // Fallback to error message
3633:     }
3634:     
3635:     // Title: 0=INIT (states 0-6), 1=EDA Ready (state 7), 2=ERROR (state 8)
3636:     size_t title_idx = (state_idx < static_cast<size_t>(InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED)) ? 0 :
3637:                        (state_idx == static_cast<size_t>(InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED)) ? 1 : 2;
3638: 
3639:     status_bar_.update_normal_status(
3640:         INIT_STATUS_TITLES[title_idx],
3641:         INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[state_idx]
3642:     );
3643: }
3644: 
3645: // Static Histogram Callback Implementation (no lambda captures)
3646: // @param histogram Histogram buffer from SpectralAnalyzer (64 bins)
3647: // @param noise_floor Noise floor value from spectral analysis
3648: // @param user_data User data pointer
3649: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::static_histogram_callback(
3650:     const SpectralAnalyzer::HistogramBuffer& histogram,
3651:     uint8_t noise_floor,
3652:     void* user_data
3653: ) noexcept {
3654:     // Guard clause: Validate user_data pointer
3655:     if (!user_data) {
3656:         return;
3657:     }
3658:     
3659:     // Cast user_data pointer back to view instance
3660:     auto* view = static_cast<EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView*>(user_data);
3661:     
3662:     // Guard clause: Skip if display buffers not ready
3663:     if (!view->display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
3664:         return;
3665:     }
3666:     
3667:     // Forward histogram data to display controller
3668:     view->display_controller_.update_histogram_display(histogram, noise_floor);
3669: }
3670: 
3671: // Enhanced Initialization State Machine with Timeout Protection
3672: // Eliminates cascading if/else, adds timeout protection, saves ~150 bytes RAM
3673: // EVENT-DRIVEN INITIALIZATION:
3674: // Phases execute based on actual state completion, not time delays
3675: // Key changes:
3676: // - Removed time-based delay check
3677: // - Each phase checks for actual completion before transitioning state
3678: // - Only one phase executes per call, ensuring proper sequencing
3679: // Benefits:
3680: // - No race conditions between phases
3681: // - Database loading is guaranteed complete before hardware init
3682: // - Settings loading waits for database completion
3683: // - More predictable initialization behavior
3684: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::step_deferred_initialization() noexcept {
3685:     // SAFETY: Guard clause for re-entrancy protection
3686:     // Single-threaded context (UI event loop only) - no synchronization needed
3687:     if (initialization_in_progress_) {
3688:         return;
3689:     }
3690:     initialization_in_progress_ = true;
3691: 
3692:     // SAFETY: Handle ERROR state - no further processing needed
3693:     if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3694:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0,
3695:                                       ERROR_MESSAGES[static_cast<uint8_t>(init_error_)]);
3696:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3697:         return;
3698:     }
3699: 
3700:     // Check timeout (protects from hangs)
3701:     systime_t elapsed = chTimeNow() - init_start_time_;
3702:     if (elapsed > MS2ST(EDA::Constants::INIT_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
3703:         // Proper cleanup in timeout path
3704:         SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings_);
3705:         
3706:         // Database loading thread will complete on its own
3707:         // The initialization state machine will handle the incomplete state
3708:         
3709:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3710:         init_error_ = InitError::GENERAL_TIMEOUT;
3711:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3712:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0, "Init timeout!");
3713:         return;
3714:     }
3715: 
3716:     // Single-level dispatch using LUT - eliminates deep call hierarchy
3717:     // Phase functions are called directly based on current state index
3718:     constexpr size_t NUM_PHASES = 6;
3719:     using PhaseFunc = void (EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::*)();
3720:     
3721:     static constexpr std::array<PhaseFunc, NUM_PHASES> PHASE_FUNCS = {{
3722:         &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_allocate_buffers,
3723:         &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_database,
3724:         &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_init_hardware,
3725:         &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_setup_ui,
3726:         &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_settings,
3727:         &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_finalize
3728:     }};
3729:     
3730:     // Map current state to phase function index
3731:     // CONSTRUCTED (0) -> index 0 -> init_phase_allocate_buffers
3732:     // BUFFERS_ALLOCATED (1) -> index 1 -> init_phase_load_database
3733:     // DATABASE_LOADED (3) -> index 2 -> init_phase_init_hardware
3734:     // HARDWARE_READY (4) -> index 3 -> init_phase_setup_ui
3735:     // UI_LAYOUT_READY (5) -> index 4 -> init_phase_load_settings
3736:     // SETTINGS_LOADED (6) -> index 5 -> init_phase_finalize
3737:     uint8_t state_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(init_state_);
3738:     
3739:     // State-to-index mapping: skip intermediate states
3740:     // DATABASE_LOADING (2) and COORDINATOR_READY (7) are handled by phase functions
3741:     uint8_t phase_idx = state_idx;
3742:     if (state_idx > 2) phase_idx--;  // Skip DATABASE_LOADING (state 2)
3743:     if (state_idx > 6) phase_idx--;  // Skip COORDINATOR_READY (state 7)
3744:     
3745:     // Skip DATABASE_LOADING state - it's an intermediate state handled by init_phase_load_database
3746:     if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADING || init_state_ == InitState::COORDINATOR_READY) {
3747:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3748:         return;
3749:     }
3750:     
3751:     if (phase_idx < NUM_PHASES) {
3752:         // Execute phase function
3753:         (this->*PHASE_FUNCS[phase_idx])();
3754:         
3755:         // Exit if error occurred
3756:         if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3757:             initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3758:             return;
3759:         }
3760:         
3761:         // Update UI status based on phase
3762:         static constexpr const char* const INIT_PHASE_NAMES[NUM_PHASES] = {
3763:             "Allocating buffers...",
3764:             "Loading database...",
3765:             "Initializing hardware...",
3766:             "Setting up UI...",
3767:             "Loading settings...",
3768:             "Finalizing..."
3769:         };
3770:         
3771:         const char* status_msg = INIT_PHASE_NAMES[phase_idx];
3772:         // Special message for database loading
3773:         if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADING && !scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3774:             status_msg = "Loading database...";
3775:         }
3776:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", status_msg);
3777:     }
3778:     
3779:     // Reset flag (allow repeated calls)
3780:     initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3781: }
3782: 
3783: // Phase Initialization Methods (each method checks state before execution)
3784: 
3785: // Phase 1: Allocate display buffers
3786: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_allocate_buffers() {
3787:     if (!display_controller_.allocate_buffers_from_pool()) {
3788:         init_error_ = InitError::ALLOCATION_FAILED;
3789:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3790:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3791:         return;
3792:     }
3793: 
3794:     // DIAMOND FIX #1: Register histogram callback early
3795:     // Connect scanner histogram callback to display controller
3796:     // Diamond Code: Function pointer with user data (no heap allocation, no std::function)
3797:     // Data flow: SpectralAnalyzer  Scanner  DisplayController
3798:     // NOTE: Using static function with 'this' as user data to avoid lambda captures
3799:     // BUG FIX: Moved from init_phase_finalize() to prevent race condition where
3800:     // callback could be invoked before buffers are fully allocated
3801:     scanner_.set_histogram_callback(&EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::static_histogram_callback, this);
3802: 
3803:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 1: Buffers OK");
3804:     init_state_ = InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED;
3805: }
3806: 
3807: // 2: Load database
3808: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_database() {
3809:     // FIX #H2: Ensure DATABASE_LOADED only transitions when actually complete
3810:     // The state machine previously used DATABASE_LOADED to mean "database loading started",
3811:     // not "database loading complete". This created a logical inconsistency where the
3812:     // state machine proceeded to Phase 3 (hardware init) while the database was still loading.
3813: 
3814:     if (init_state_ == InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED) {
3815:         // Start async database loading
3816:         scanner_.initialize_database_async();
3817:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 2: DB loading...");
3818:         init_state_ = InitState::DATABASE_LOADING;
3819:         return;
3820:     }
3821: 
3822:     // Check if database loading is complete
3823:     if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADING) {
3824:         if (scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3825:             // FIX #H2: Only transition to DATABASE_LOADED when actually complete
3826:             // This prevents Phase 3 (hardware init) from starting before DB is ready
3827:             init_state_ = InitState::DATABASE_LOADED;
3828:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 2: DB loaded");
3829:         } else {
3830:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Loading DB...");
3831:             // FIX #H2: Do NOT transition - wait for completion
3832:         }
3833:     }
3834: }
3835: 
3836: // Phase 3: Initialize hardware
3837: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_init_hardware() {
3838:     // FIX #M9: Ensure DATABASE_LOADED state only when truly complete
3839:     // Double-check database loading is complete before hardware init
3840:     if (init_state_ != InitState::DATABASE_LOADED) {
3841:         return;
3842:     }
3843: 
3844:     // FIX #M9: Additional verification - check initialization_complete_ flag
3845:     if (!scanner_.is_initialization_complete()) {
3846:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "DB not ready");
3847:         return;
3848:     }
3849: 
3850:     hardware_.on_hardware_show();
3851:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 3: HW ready");
3852:     init_state_ = InitState::HARDWARE_READY;
3853: }

3855: // Phase 4: Setup UI layout
3856: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_setup_ui() {
3857:     if (init_state_ != InitState::HARDWARE_READY) {
3858:         return;
3859:     }
3860: 
3861:     // FIX: Wait for database to complete before setting up UI
3862:     // Phase 4 (UI Setup) can execute while database is still loading asynchronously.
3863:     // This creates a race condition where UI elements may access uninitialized data.
3864:     if (!scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3865:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Waiting for DB...");
3866:         return;  // Return and retry in next paint() call
3867:     }
3868: 
3869:     // FIX: Additional verification - check initialization_complete_ flag
3870:     if (!scanner_.is_initialization_complete()) {
3871:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "DB not ready");
3872:         return;  // Return and retry in next paint() call
3873:     }
3874: 
3875:     initialize_modern_layout();
3876:     // FIX #L6: Move add_ui_elements() to appropriate phase
3877:     // UI elements should be added after parent View initialization is complete
3878:     add_ui_elements();
3879:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 4: UI ready");
3880:     init_state_ = InitState::UI_LAYOUT_READY;
3881: }

3883: // Phase 5: Load settings
3884: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_settings() {
3885:     // StackGuard for stack safety monitoring
3886:     StackSafety::StackGuard guard("init_phase_load_settings");
3887:     
3888:     if (init_state_ != InitState::UI_LAYOUT_READY) {
3889:         return;
3890:     }
3891: 
3892:     // FIX #M2: Wait for database to complete before loading settings
3893:     // The initialization state machine transitions from DATABASE_LOADED to SETTINGS_LOADED
3894:     // based on time delays only, not actual completion. Phase 5 (settings load) executes
3895:     // while the database is still loading asynchronously, causing a race condition.
3896:     if (!scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3897:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Waiting for DB...");
3898:         return;  // Return and retry in next paint() call
3899:     }
3900: 
3901:     // FIX #M2: Additional verification - check initialization_complete_ flag
3902:     if (!scanner_.is_initialization_complete()) {
3903:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "DB not ready");
3904:         return;  // Return and retry in next paint() call
3905:     }
3906: 
3907:     // 6.4:
3908: 
3909:     // FIX: Use RAII guard to ensure M4 interrupts are always re-enabled
3910:     // This prevents M4Core_IRQHandler from firing while M0 is locked
3911:     // The guard automatically re-enables interrupts on scope exit
3912:     M4InterruptGuard interrupt_guard;
3913: 
3914:     // SD
3915:     systime_t sd_start = chTimeNow();
3916:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
3917:         // FIX #L4: Use constant instead of magic number 1s timeout
3918:         if ((chTimeNow() - sd_start) > MS2ST(EDA::Constants::SD_CARD_MOUNT_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
3919:             // FIX: M4InterruptGuard automatically re-enables interrupts on return
3920:             // FIX #M7: Reset to default settings on SD card timeout
3921:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "No SD - defaults");
3922:             SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings_);
3923:             init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3924:             return;
3925:         }
3926:         // Use constant instead of magic number 50ms
3927:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(EDA::Constants::SD_CARD_POLL_INTERVAL_SHORT_MS);
3928:     }
3929: 
3930:     systime_t settings_start = chTimeNow();
3931:     // Use constant instead of magic number 2s timeout
3932:     constexpr systime_t SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS = MS2ST(EDA::Constants::SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS);
3933: 
3934:     // Removed SDCardLock - FatFS handles locking at driver level
3935:     auto load_result = SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings_);
3936:     bool loaded = load_result.is_ok() && load_result.value;
3937: 
3938:     systime_t elapsed = chTimeNow() - settings_start;
3939:     if (elapsed >= SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS) {
3940:         // FIX: M4InterruptGuard automatically re-enables interrupts on return
3941:         // Reset to default settings on timeout
3942:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("WARN", "Settings timeout");
3943:         SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings_);
3944:         init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3945:         return;
3946:     }
3947: 
3948:     if (!loaded) {
3949:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Using defaults");
3950:         SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings_);
3951:     } else {
3952:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Settings loaded");
3953:     }
3954: 
3955:     // FIX: M4InterruptGuard automatically re-enables interrupts on scope exit
3956: 
3957:     button_audio_.set_text(audio_get_enable_alerts(settings_) ? "AUDIO: ON" : "AUDIO: OFF");
3958:     scanner_.update_scan_range(settings_.wideband_min_freq_hz,
3959:                             settings_.wideband_max_freq_hz);
3960:     
3961:     // FIX: Update coordinator parameters after settings load
3962:     scanning_coordinator_.update_runtime_parameters(settings_);
3963: 
3964:     // DIAMOND FIX: Update scanner's settings from view's settings
3965:     // Required because scanner now stores settings by value (not reference)
3966:     scanner_.update_settings(settings_);
3967: 
3968:     // Scanner initialization verification with proper error feedback
3969:     if (!scanner_.is_initialization_complete()) {
3970:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("WARN", "Scanner not ready");
3971:         // Continue anyway - scanner will retry initialization
3972:     }
3973: 
3974:     // DIAMOND FIX: Update audio cooldown based on settings to prevent UI freeze
3975:     // baseband::send_message() uses busy-wait spin loop (baseband_api.cpp:54-64)
3976:     // Set cooldown = duration + 100ms buffer to ensure M0 can process audio
3977:     const uint32_t audio_cooldown = settings_.audio_alert_duration_ms + 100;
3978:     AudioAlertManager::set_cooldown_ms(audio_cooldown);
3979: 
3980:     // FIX #M10: Transition to SETTINGS_LOADED state
3981:     init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3982: }
3983: 
3984: // 6: Finalize (  FULLY_INITIALIZED)
3985: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_finalize() {
3986:     if (init_state_ != InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED) {
3987:         return;
3988:     }
3989: 
3990:     // DIAMOND FIX #3: Verify initialization is complete before starting
3991:     // start_scanning_thread() is called without verifying that scanner_.is_initialization_complete()
3992:     // returns true. This prevents starting scanning if the scanner is not fully initialized.
3993:     if (!scanner_.is_initialization_complete()) {
3994:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3995:         init_error_ = InitError::DATABASE_ERROR;
3996:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3997:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("ERROR", "Scanner not ready");
3998:         return;
3999:     }
4000: 
4001:     handle_scanner_update();
4002:     init_state_ = InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED;
4003:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("EDA", "Ready");
4004: 
4005:     // FIX: Automatically start scanning thread after initialization
4006:     start_scanning_thread();
4007: }

4013:     init_state_ = InitState::CONSTRUCTED;
4014:     init_start_time_ = chTimeNow();
4015:     last_init_progress_ = 0;
4016:     initialization_in_progress_ = false;
4017:     init_error_ = InitError::NONE;
4018: 
4019:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 0: Ready");
4020:     
4021:     // FIX #2: Call continue_initialization() instead of step_deferred_initialization()
4022:     // This ensures initialization runs from UI event loop, not nested in paint()
4023:     continue_initialization();
4024:     
4025:     // FIX: Force redraw to show status bar
4026:     set_dirty();

4028: 
4029: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::continue_initialization() {
4030:     // FIX #2: Continue deferred initialization from UI event loop
4031:     // This prevents nested stack frames that cause M0 stack overflow
4032:     if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED &&
4033:         init_state_ != InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
4034:         step_deferred_initialization();
4035:         
4036:         // Schedule next call if initialization is not complete
4037:         if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED &&
4038:             init_state_ != InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
4039:             set_dirty();  // Trigger repaint which will call continue_initialization() again
4040:         }
4041:     }
4042: }

4047:     hardware_.stop_spectrum_streaming();
4048:     hardware_.shutdown_hardware();
4049:     hardware_.on_hardware_hide();

4052: 
4053:     View::on_hide();

4055: 
4056: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::start_scanning_thread() {
4057:     // CRITICAL FIX: Verify initialization before starting
4058:     if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
4059:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0, "Not initialized");
4060:         return;
4061:     }
4062: 
4063:     if (scanning_coordinator_.is_scanning_active()) return;
4064: 
4065:     const auto result = scanning_coordinator_.start_coordinated_scanning();
4066: 
4067:     // Handle different start results
4068:     switch (result) {
4069:         case StartResult::SUCCESS:
4070:             // Scanning started successfully
4071:             break;
4072:         case StartResult::ALREADY_ACTIVE:
4073:             // Already active (shouldn't happen due to guard clause above)
4074:             break;
4075:         case StartResult::INITIALIZATION_NOT_COMPLETE:
4076:             // Database initialization not complete yet
4077:             // The UI event loop will retry on next frame sync
4078:             // See message_handler_frame_sync_ in ui_enhanced_drone_analyzer.hpp:1721
4079:             break;
4080:         case StartResult::THREAD_CREATION_FAILED:
4081:             // Thread creation failed - this is a critical error
4082:             // Display error message to user
4083:             display_controller_.text_status_info().set("Thread creation failed");
4084:             break;
4085:     }
4086: }
4087: 
4088: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::stop_scanning_thread() {
4089:     if (!scanning_coordinator_.is_scanning_active()) return;
4090:     scanning_coordinator_.stop_coordinated_scanning();
4091: }

4093: bool EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::handle_start_stop_button() {
4094:     // CRITICAL FIX: Check initialization state before starting scanning
4095:     if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
4096:         // Show error message to user
4097:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0, "Not initialized");
4098:         return false;
4099:     }
4100:     
4101:     if (scanning_coordinator_.is_scanning_active()) {
4102:         ui_controller_.on_stop_scan();
4103:         button_start_stop_.set_text("START/STOP");
4104:     } else {
4105:         ui_controller_.on_start_scan();
4106:         button_start_stop_.set_text("STOP");
4107:     }
4108:     return true;
4109: }

4116: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::initialize_modern_layout() {
4117:     // 2.7: Don't call handle_scanner_update() here!
4118:     // scanner_ may not be fully initialized yet
4119:     // This prevents segfault/black screen during startup
4120:     // handle_scanner_update() will be called after FULLY_INITIALIZED state
4121: 
4122:     // FIX #L7: Add check to ensure parent View is ready before setting parent_rect
4123:     // Verify initialization state before calling set_parent_rect() on ThreatCard objects
4124:     if (init_state_ < InitState::UI_LAYOUT_READY) {
4125:         return;
4126:     }
4127: 
4128:     for (size_t i = 0; i < threat_cards_.size(); ++i) {
4129:         size_t card_y_pos = 165 + i * 20;
4130: 
4131:         if (card_y_pos + 24 > 224) break;
4132: 
4133:         threat_cards_[i].set_parent_rect(Rect{0, static_cast<int>(card_y_pos), screen_width, 24});
4134:     }
4135: }

4141: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup tables for UI state machine
4142: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
4143: // Eliminates branching and std::string allocation
4144: namespace {
4145:     // Signal type mapping from ScanningMode to const char* (Flash storage)
4146:     static constexpr const char* SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[] = {
4147:         "RSSI",      // DATABASE = 0
4148:         "SPECTRAL",  // WIDEBAND_CONTINUOUS = 1
4149:         "HYBRID"     // HYBRID = 2
4150:     };
4151: 
4152:     // Alert message mapping from ThreatLevel to const char* (Flash storage)
4153:     static constexpr const char* ALERT_MSG_LUT[] = {
4154:         "Threats detected",   // NONE/LOW = 0,1
4155:         "Threats detected",   // MEDIUM = 2
4156:         "HIGH THREATS!",      // HIGH = 3
4157:         "CRITICAL THREATS!"   // CRITICAL = 4
4158:     };
4159: }
4160: 
4161: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::handle_scanner_update() {
4162:     // SAFETY: Early exit if buffers are not valid
4163:     if (!display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
4164:         return;
4165:     }
4166:     
4167:     // Early exit if scanner not active
4168:     if (!scanner_.is_scanning_active() &&
4169:         scanner_.get_approaching_count() == 0 &&
4170:         scanner_.get_static_count() == 0 &&
4171:         scanner_.get_receding_count() == 0) {
4172:         const char* primary_msg = "EDA Ready";
4173:         char secondary_buffer[48];
4174:         uint32_t total_detections = scanner_.get_total_detections();
4175:         if (total_detections > 0) {
4176:             StatusFormatter::format_to(secondary_buffer, "Total detections: %lu",
4177:                                       static_cast<unsigned long>(total_detections));
4178:         } else {
4179:             snprintf(secondary_buffer, sizeof(secondary_buffer), "%s", "Awaiting commands");
4180:         }
4181:         status_bar_.update_normal_status(primary_msg, secondary_buffer);
4182:         return;
4183:     }
4184: 
4185:     // THREAD SAFETY FIX: Acquire mutex once for atomic snapshot of scanner state
4186:     // This prevents TOCTOU (Time-Of-Check-Time-Of-Use) issues
4187:     // where the state could change between reads.
4188:     //
4189:     // Lock order: DATA_MUTEX (level 1) for detection data and tracking state
4190:     // The get_state_snapshot() method provides thread-safe access with single mutex acquisition.
4191:     // Acquiring the mutex once here is more efficient than acquiring it separately
4192:     // for each getter call.
4193: 
4194:     const auto snapshot = scanner_.get_state_snapshot();
4195:     const ThreatLevel max_threat = snapshot.max_detected_threat;
4196:     const size_t approaching = snapshot.approaching_count;
4197:     const size_t static_count = snapshot.static_count;
4198:     const size_t receding = snapshot.receding_count;
4199:     const bool is_scanning = snapshot.scanning_active;
4200:     
4201:     Frequency current_freq = scanner_.get_current_scanning_frequency();
4202: 
4203:     // Trigger audio alerts based on threat level (with debouncing)
4204:     // AudioAlertManager::play_alert() has built-in debouncing to prevent baseband queue saturation
4205:     // baseband::send_message() uses busy-wait spin loop
4206:     if (audio_get_enable_alerts(settings_) && max_threat >= ThreatLevel::LOW) {
4207:         size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
4208:         if (total_drones > 0) {
4209:             AudioAlertManager::play_alert(max_threat);
4210:         }
4211:     }
4212: 
4213:     // Update header
4214:     smart_header_.update(max_threat, approaching, static_count, receding,
4215:                         current_freq, is_scanning);
4216: 
4217:     // Update status bar (DoD: table-driven state machine)
4218:     if (is_scanning) {
4219:         uint32_t cycles = scanner_.get_scan_cycles();
4220:         uint32_t progress = std::min(static_cast<uint32_t>(cycles * 5), static_cast<uint32_t>(32));
4221:         status_bar_.update_scanning_progress(progress, cycles,
4222:                                          scanner_.get_total_detections());
4223:     } else {
4224:         size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
4225:         // LUT lookup instead of ternary (Flash string, zero RAM allocation)
4226:         const char* alert_msg = ALERT_MSG_LUT[
4227:             std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat), static_cast<uint8_t>(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL))
4228:         ];
4229:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(max_threat, total_drones, alert_msg);
4230:     }
4231: 
4232:     display_controller_.update_detection_display(scanner_);
4233: 
4234:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup for signal type (Flash storage)
4235:     // Eliminates switch-case and std::string allocation
4236:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanner_.get_scanning_mode());
4237:     const char* signal_type = SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[mode_idx];
4238:     display_controller_.update_signal_type_display(signal_type);
4239: }
