4241: // Button Callback Implementations
4242: // NOTE: Mayhem UI framework uses std::function<void(Button&)> for callbacks
4243: // Alternative approaches considered:
4244: // - Raw function pointers: Not feasible due to 'this' capture requirement
4245: // - Template-based callbacks: Would require framework-wide changes
4246: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::setup_button_handlers() {
4247:     button_start_stop_.on_select = [this](Button&) {
4248:         this->handle_start_stop_button();
4249:     };
4250: 
4251:     button_menu_.on_select = [this](Button&) {
4252:         this->ui_controller_.show_menu();
4253:     };
4254: 
4255:     button_audio_.on_select = [this](Button&) {
4256:         // FIX: Verify initialization state before allowing user interaction
4257:         if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
4258:             return;
4259:         }
4260:         bool current = audio_get_enable_alerts(this->settings_);
4261:         audio_set_enable_alerts(this->settings_, !current);
4262:         this->button_audio_.set_text(audio_get_enable_alerts(this->settings_) ? "AUDIO: ON" : "AUDIO: OFF");
4263:         this->button_audio_.set_style(audio_get_enable_alerts(this->settings_) ? &UIStyles::GREEN_STYLE : &UIStyles::LIGHT_STYLE);
4264:     };
4265: 
4266:     field_scanning_mode_.on_change = [this](size_t index, int32_t value) {
4267:         // FIX: Verify initialization state before allowing user interaction
4268:         if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
4269:             return;
4270:         }
4271:         (void)value;  // Silence unused parameter warning
4272:         this->set_scanning_mode_from_index(index);
4273:     };
4274: }

4284:     display_controller_.set_scanning_status(ui_controller_.is_scanning(),
4285:                                            scanner_.scanning_mode_name());
4286:     update_modern_layout();

4356: void CompactFrequencyRuler::paint(Painter& painter) {
4357:     const auto r = screen_rect();
4358: 
4359:     painter.fill_rectangle(r, Color::black());
4360: 
4361:     if (!visible_) return;
4362: 
4363:     draw_compact_ticks(painter, r);
4364: }
4365: 
4366: void CompactFrequencyRuler::draw_compact_ticks(Painter& painter, const Rect r) {
4367:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4368:     if (range == 0) return;
4369: 
4370:     Frequency tick_interval = calculate_optimal_tick_interval();
4371:     if (tick_interval == 0) return;
4372: 
4373:     // Single style (both use same font/colors)
4374:     static Style label_style{font::fixed_5x8, Color::grey(), Color::black()};
4375: 
4376:     painter.fill_rectangle(
4377:         {r.left(), r.top() + RULER_HEIGHT - 1, r.width(), 1},
4378:         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4379:     );
4380: 
4381:     Frequency first_tick = (min_freq_ / tick_interval) * tick_interval;
4382:     if (first_tick < min_freq_) {
4383:         first_tick += tick_interval;
4384:     }
4385: 
4386:     for (Frequency tick = first_tick; tick <= max_freq_; tick += tick_interval) {
4387:         int x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4388: 
4389:         if (x < r.left() || x > r.right()) {
4390:             continue;
4391:         }
4392: 
4393:         painter.fill_rectangle(
4394:             {x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MAJOR},
4395:             Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4396:         );
4397: 
4398:         char label_buf[32];
4399:         format_compact_label(label_buf, sizeof(label_buf), tick);
4400: 
4401:         auto text_size = label_style.font.size_of(label_buf);
4402:         int text_x = x - text_size.width() / 2;
4403:         int text_y = r.top() + 1;
4404: 
4405:         if (text_x < r.left() + 2) text_x = r.left() + 2;
4406:         if (text_x + text_size.width() > r.right() - 2) {
4407:             text_x = r.right() - text_size.width() - 2;
4408:         }
4409: 
4410:         painter.draw_string({text_x, text_y}, label_style, label_buf);
4411: 
4412:         // Sub-tick logic based on tick_interval only
4413:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 100000000ULL) {
4414:             for (int sub = 1; sub < 5; sub++) {
4415:                 Frequency sub_tick = tick + (tick_interval * sub) / 5;
4416:                 int sub_x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((sub_tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4417: 
4418:                 if (sub_x > r.left() && sub_x < r.right()) {
4419:                     painter.fill_rectangle(
4420:                         {sub_x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MINOR},
4421:                         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4422:                     );
4423:                 }
4424:             }
4425:         }
4426:     }
4427: }
4428: 
4429: // Lookup table for ruler style to formatter mapping (eliminates ~60 lines of switch-case)
4430: namespace {
4431:     static constexpr FrequencyFormatter::Format RULER_FORMAT_LUT[] = {
4432:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_GHZ,   // COMPACT_GHZ = 0
4433:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_MHZ,   // COMPACT_MHZ = 1
4434:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_GHZ,  // STANDARD_GHZ = 2
4435:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ,  // STANDARD_MHZ = 3
4436:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ,  // DETAILED = 4
4437:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::SPACED_GHZ      // SPACED_GHZ = 5
4438:     };
4439: }
4440: 
4441: // Unified frequency formatting using FrequencyFormatter
4442: void CompactFrequencyRuler::format_compact_label(char* buffer, size_t buffer_size, Frequency freq) {
4443:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(ruler_style_);
4444:     if (idx >= 6) idx = 0;
4445:     FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(buffer, buffer_size, freq, RULER_FORMAT_LUT[idx]);
4446: }
4447: 
4448: Frequency CompactFrequencyRuler::calculate_optimal_tick_interval() {
4449:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4450:     if (range == 0) return 0;
4451: 
4452:     // Optimized intervals for PortaPack's small screen (prioritize GHz for SPACED_GHZ)
4453:     static constexpr Frequency intervals[] = {
4454:         5000000000ULL,  4000000000ULL,  3000000000ULL, 2000000000ULL,  // 5G, 4G, 3G, 2G
4455:         1000000000ULL,  // 1G (key for SPACED_GHZ)
4456:         500000000ULL,   250000000ULL,   200000000ULL,            // 500M, 250M, 200M
4457:         100000000ULL,   50000000ULL,    25000000ULL,            // 100M, 50M, 25M
4458:         20000000ULL,    10000000ULL,    5000000ULL,             // 20M, 10M, 5M
4459:         2000000ULL,     1000000ULL,     500000ULL,              // 2M, 1M, 500k
4460:         200000ULL,      100000ULL                                // 200k, 100k
4461:     };
4462: 
4463:     for (auto interval : intervals) {
4464:         int ticks = static_cast<int>(range / interval);
4465:         if (ticks >= target_tick_count_ - 1 && ticks <= target_tick_count_ + 1) {
4466:             return interval;
4467:         }
4468:     }
4469: 
4470:     return range / target_tick_count_;
4471: }
4472: 
4473: bool CompactFrequencyRuler::should_use_mhz_labels() const {
4474:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4475: 
4476:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 50000000ULL) {
4477:         return true;
4478:     }
4479: 
4480:     Frequency center = (min_freq_ + max_freq_) / 2;
4481:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(center) < 1000000000ULL) {
4482:         return true;
4483:     }
4484: 
4485:     if (ruler_style_ == RulerStyle::COMPACT_MHZ ||
4486:         ruler_style_ == RulerStyle::STANDARD_MHZ) {
4487:         return true;
4488:     }
4489: 
4490:     return false;
4491: }

4496:     compact_frequency_ruler_.set_dirty();
4497: }

4502: }

4504: void DroneDisplayController::apply_display_settings(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4505:     if (disp_get_show_frequency_ruler(settings)) {
4506:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(true);
4507: 
4508:         if (disp_get_auto_ruler_style(settings)) {
4509:             compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(RulerStyle::COMPACT_GHZ);
4510:         } else {
4511:             // constexpr LUT in Flash instead of switch
4512:             uint8_t style_idx = (settings.frequency_ruler_style < 7) ?
4513:                                 settings.frequency_ruler_style : 0;
4514:             compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(RULER_STYLE_LUT[style_idx]);
4515:         }
4516: 
4517:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_tick_count(settings.compact_ruler_tick_count);
4518:     } else {
4519:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4520:     }
4521: }
4522: 
4523: // Stack Usage Monitoring
4524: // * * @brief Check stack usage and log warnings if low * @param thread_name Name of the thread for logging * @param stack_size Total stack size for the thread * * @note Uses ChibiOS stack fill pattern (0x55) to estimate free stack space. * Compatible with ChibiOS versions that have CH_DBG_FILL_THREADS enabled. * If stack filling is not enabled, reports 0 free bytes conservatively.
4525: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::check_stack_usage([[maybe_unused]] const char* thread_name, size_t stack_size) {
4526:     Thread* current_thread = chThdSelf();
4527:     
4528:     // Count unused bytes from stack fill pattern (0x55)
4529:     
4530:     size_t free_stack = 0;
4531:     
4532:     // Get stack start address (after Thread structure)
4533:     uint8_t* stack_start = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(current_thread + 1);
4534:     
4535:     // Limit scan to avoid scanning entire stack every time
4536:     const size_t max_scan_bytes = (stack_size > 4096) ? 4096 : stack_size;
4537:     const uint8_t stack_fill_value = 0x55;
4538:     
4539:     for (size_t i = 0; i < max_scan_bytes; ++i) {
4540:         if (stack_start[i] == stack_fill_value) {
4541:             free_stack++;
4542:         } else {
4543:             // Stack used up to this point
4544:             break;
4545:         }
4546:     }
4547:     
4548:     // Conservatively report max_scan_bytes if all fill pattern (avoids large scans)
4549:     
4550:     if (free_stack < MIN_STACK_FREE_THRESHOLD) {
4551:         // Track low stack condition for monitoring
4552:     }
4553: }
4554: 
4555: // Memory Pressure Monitoring
4556: // * * @brief Check memory pressure and log warnings if critical
4557: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::check_memory_pressure() {
4558:     size_t free_heap = HeapMonitor::get_free_heap();
4559: 
4560:     if (free_heap < 8192) {  // Less than 8KB free
4561:         // Log warning - memory running low
4562:     }
4563: 
4564:     if (free_heap < 4096) {  // Less than 4KB free - critical
4565:         // Log error - critical memory condition (implement graceful degradation)
4566:     }
4567: }
4568:

33: // RAII wrapper for File (ensures proper cleanup)
34: class FileRAII {
35: public:
36:     explicit FileRAII(const char* path, bool read_only = false)
37:         : file_(), opened_(file_.open(path, read_only)) {}
38: 
39:     // noexcept for move operations
40:     ~FileRAII() noexcept {
41:         if (opened_) {
42:             file_.close();
43:         }
44:     }
45: 
46:     FileRAII(const FileRAII&) = delete;
47:     FileRAII& operator=(const FileRAII&) = delete;
48: 
49:     FileRAII(FileRAII&& other) noexcept
50:         : file_(std::move(other.file_)), opened_(other.opened_) {
51:         other.opened_ = false;
52:     }
53: 
54:     File& get() noexcept { return file_; }
55:     const File& get() const noexcept { return file_; }
56:     bool is_open() const noexcept { return opened_; }
57: 
58: private:
59:     File file_;
60:     bool opened_ = false;
61: };

63: // EnhancedSettingsManager Implementation

65:     // const reference to prevent unnecessary copies
66: bool EnhancedSettingsManager::save_settings_to_txt(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) noexcept {
67:     // Fix SD Card Race Condition - acquire lock BEFORE checking status
68:     SettingsBufferLock lock;
69:     
70:     // Use constexpr const char* instead of std::string
71:     static constexpr const char* filepath = "/sdcard/ENHANCED_DRONE_ANALYZER_SETTINGS.txt";
72: 
73:     // Create backup for atomic write operation
74:     create_backup_file(filepath);
75: 
76:     File settings_file;
77:     if (!settings_file.open(filepath, false)) {
78:         return false;
79:     }
80: 
81:     auto& file = settings_file;
82: 
83:     // Thread-local buffer for settings serialization (replaces ~20 std::string allocations)
84:     // Optimized: Reduced from 1024 to 512 bytes (512 bytes savings)
85:     static constexpr size_t SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE = 512;
86:     thread_local char settings_buffer[SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE];
87:     size_t offset = 0;
88: 
89:     // Write header with timestamp
90:     const char* header = generate_file_header();
91:     size_t header_len = strlen(header);
92:     auto header_result = file.write(header, header_len);
93:     if (header_result.is_error() || header_result.value() != header_len) {
94:         file.close();
95:         // Log error - restore from backup on write failure
96:         restore_from_backup(filepath);
97:         return false;
98:     }
99: 
100:     // Generate settings content using snprintf (no heap allocations)
101:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
102:                       "spectrum_mode=%s\n", spectrum_mode_to_string(settings.spectrum_mode));
103:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
104:                       "scan_interval_ms=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.scan_interval_ms);
105:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
106:                       "rssi_threshold_db=%d\n", (int)settings.rssi_threshold_db);
107:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
108:                       "enable_audio_alerts=%s\n", audio_get_enable_alerts(settings) ? "true" : "false");
109:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
110:                       "audio_alert_frequency_hz=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.audio_alert_frequency_hz);
111:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
112:                       "audio_alert_duration_ms=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.audio_alert_duration_ms);
113:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
114:                       "hardware_bandwidth_hz=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz);
115:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
116:                       "enable_real_hardware=%s\n", hw_get_enable_real_hardware(settings) ? "true" : "false");
117:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
118:                       "demo_mode=%s\n", hw_get_demo_mode(settings) ? "true" : "false");
119:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
120:                       "freqman_path=%s\n", settings.freqman_path);
121:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
122:                       "user_min_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.user_min_freq_hz);
123:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
124:                       "user_max_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.user_max_freq_hz);
125:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
126:                       "wideband_slice_width_hz=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.wideband_slice_width_hz);
127:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
128:                       "panoramic_mode_enabled=%s\n", scan_get_panoramic_mode_enabled(settings) ? "true" : "false");
129:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
130:                       "wideband_min_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.wideband_min_freq_hz);
131:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
132:                       "wideband_max_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.wideband_max_freq_hz);
133:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
134:                       "settings_version=0.4\n");
135:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
136:                       "last_modified_timestamp=%u\n", (unsigned int)chTimeNow());
137: 
138:     // Write settings content
139:     auto content_result = file.write(settings_buffer, offset);
140:     if (content_result.is_error() || content_result.value() != offset) {
141:         file.close();
142:         // Log error - restore from backup on write failure
143:         restore_from_backup(filepath);
144:         return false;
145:     }
146: 
147:     file.close();
148:     remove_backup_file(filepath);
149:     return true;
150: }

152: // noexcept for simple file existence check
153: bool EnhancedSettingsManager::verify_comm_file_exists() noexcept {
154:     // Use constexpr const char* instead of std::string
155:     static constexpr const char* filepath = "/sdcard/ENHANCED_DRONE_ANALYZER_SETTINGS.txt";
156:     File txt_file;
157:     if (txt_file.open(filepath, true)) {  // read_only
158:         txt_file.close();
159:         return true;
160:     }
161:     return false;

163: 
164:     // const reference to prevent unnecessary copies
165: bool EnhancedSettingsManager::load_settings_from_txt(DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) noexcept {
166:     // Use constexpr const char* instead of std::string
167:     static constexpr const char* filepath = "/sdcard/ENHANCED_DRONE_ANALYZER_SETTINGS.txt";
168: 
169:     File settings_file;
170:     if (!settings_file.open(filepath, true)) {  // read_only
171:         return false;
172:     }
173: 
174:     auto& file = settings_file;
175: 
176:     // Thread-local buffer for settings loading (512 bytes per thread)
177:     // Optimized: Reduced from 1024 to 512 bytes (512 bytes savings)
178:     static constexpr size_t FILE_BUFFER_SIZE = 512;
179:     thread_local char file_buffer[FILE_BUFFER_SIZE];
180:     auto read_result = file.read(file_buffer, FILE_BUFFER_SIZE);
181:     
182:     if (read_result.is_error() || read_result.value() == 0) {
183:         file.close();
184:         return false;
185:     }
186: 
187:     // File Truncation Warning - if file is larger than buffer, data is truncated
188:     const size_t bytes_read = read_result.value();
189:     if (bytes_read < FILE_BUFFER_SIZE) {
190:         file_buffer[bytes_read] = '\0';
191:     } else {
192:         // Buffer was completely filled, ensure null-termination
193:         file_buffer[FILE_BUFFER_SIZE - 1] = '\0';
194:         // DIAMOND FIX: File truncated - error logging
195:         // In production, this should log to a persistent error log
196:         // For now, we note the truncation but continue processing
197:         // WARNING: Settings file exceeds buffer size, data may be lost
198:     }
199: 
200:     // FIX #18: Use non-destructive parsing (replaces strtok)
201:     // strtok modifies buffer, use manual parsing instead
202:     char* line_start = file_buffer;
203:     while (*line_start != '\0') {
204:         // Find line end
205:         char* line_end = strchr(line_start, '\n');
206:         if (line_end == nullptr) {
207:             line_end = strchr(line_start, '\r');
208:         }
209:         
210:         if (line_end == nullptr) {
211:             // Last line - process entire remaining buffer
212:             line_end = line_start + strlen(line_start);
213:         }
214:         
215:         // Temporarily null-terminate line
216:         char saved_char = *line_end;
217:         *line_end = '\0';
218:         
219:         char* line = line_start;
220:         
221:         // Skip empty lines and comments
222:         if (*line == '\0' || *line == '#') {
223:             *line_end = saved_char;  // Restore newline
224:             line_start = (saved_char != '\0') ? line_end + 1 : line_end;
225:             continue;
226:         }
227: 
228:         // Find key-value separator
229:         char* equals = strchr(line, '=');
230:         if (equals != nullptr) {
231:             *equals = '\0';
232:             char* key = line;
233:             char* value = equals + 1;
234: 
235:             // Trim whitespace from key and value
236:             while (*key == ' ' || *key == '\t') key++;
237:             while (*value == ' ' || *value == '\t') value++;
238:             char* value_end = value + strlen(value) - 1;
239:             while (value_end >= value && (*value_end == ' ' || *value_end == '\t' || *value_end == '\r')) {
240:                 *value_end-- = '\0';
241:             }
242: 
243:             // Parse specific settings
244:             if (strcmp(key, "spectrum_mode") == 0) {
245:                 // Use consolidated spectrum mode display names from eda_constants.hpp
246:                 if (strcmp(value, EDA::LUTs::spectrum_mode_display_name(0)) == 0) settings.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::ULTRA_NARROW;
247:                 else if (strcmp(value, EDA::LUTs::spectrum_mode_display_name(1)) == 0) settings.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::NARROW;
248:                 else if (strcmp(value, EDA::LUTs::spectrum_mode_display_name(2)) == 0) settings.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::MEDIUM;
249:                 else if (strcmp(value, EDA::LUTs::spectrum_mode_display_name(3)) == 0) settings.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::WIDE;
250:                 else if (strcmp(value, EDA::LUTs::spectrum_mode_display_name(4)) == 0) settings.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::ULTRA_WIDE;
251:             } else if (strcmp(key, "scan_interval_ms") == 0) {
252:                 // Replace atoi with strtol and check for errors
253:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
254:                 long val = strtol(value, &endptr, 10);
255:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 0 &&
256:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) >= EDA::Constants::MIN_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS &&
257:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) <= EDA::Constants::MAX_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS) {
258:                     settings.scan_interval_ms = static_cast<uint32_t>(val);
259:                 }
260:             } else if (strcmp(key, "rssi_threshold_db") == 0) {
261:                 // Replace atoi with strtol and check for errors
262:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
263:                 long val = strtol(value, &endptr, 10);
264:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= EDA::Constants::RSSI_INVALID_DBM && val <= EDA::Constants::MAX_VALID_RSSI) {
265:                     settings.rssi_threshold_db = static_cast<int32_t>(val);
266:                 }
267:             } else if (strcmp(key, "enable_audio_alerts") == 0) {
268:                 audio_set_enable_alerts(settings, strcmp(value, "true") == 0);
269:             } else if (strcmp(key, "audio_alert_frequency_hz") == 0) {
270:                 // Replace atoi with strtol and check for errors
271:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
272:                 long val = strtol(value, &endptr, 10);
273:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 0 &&
274:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) >= EDA::Constants::MIN_AUDIO_FREQ &&
275:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) <= EDA::Constants::MAX_AUDIO_FREQ) {
276:                     settings.audio_alert_frequency_hz = static_cast<uint32_t>(val);
277:                 }
278:             } else if (strcmp(key, "audio_alert_duration_ms") == 0) {
279:                 // Replace atoi with strtol and check for errors
280:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
281:                 long val = strtol(value, &endptr, 10);
282:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 0 &&
283:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) >= EDA::Constants::MIN_AUDIO_DURATION &&
284:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) <= EDA::Constants::MAX_AUDIO_DURATION) {
285:                     settings.audio_alert_duration_ms = static_cast<uint32_t>(val);
286:                 }
287:             } else if (strcmp(key, "hardware_bandwidth_hz") == 0) {
288:                 // Replace atoi with strtol and check for errors
289:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
290:                 long val = strtol(value, &endptr, 10);
291:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 0 &&
292:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) >= EDA::Constants::MIN_BANDWIDTH &&
293:                     static_cast<uint32_t>(val) <= EDA::Constants::MAX_BANDWIDTH) {
294:                     settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz = static_cast<uint32_t>(val);
295:                 }
296:             } else if (strcmp(key, "enable_real_hardware") == 0) {
297:                 hw_set_enable_real_hardware(settings, strcmp(value, "true") == 0);
298:             } else if (strcmp(key, "demo_mode") == 0) {
299:                 hw_set_demo_mode(settings, strcmp(value, "true") == 0);
300:             } else if (strcmp(key, "freqman_path") == 0) {
301:                 snprintf(settings.freqman_path, sizeof(settings.freqman_path), "%s", value);
302:             } else if (strcmp(key, "user_min_freq_hz") == 0) {
303:                 // Replace atoll with strtoull and check for errors
304:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
305:                 unsigned long long val = strtoull(value, &endptr, 10);
306:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 50000000ULL && val <= 6000000000ULL) {
307:                     settings.user_min_freq_hz = val;
308:                 }
309:             } else if (strcmp(key, "user_max_freq_hz") == 0) {
310:                 // Replace atoll with strtoull and check for errors
311:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
312:                 unsigned long long val = strtoull(value, &endptr, 10);
313:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 50000000ULL && val <= 6000000000ULL) {
314:                     settings.user_max_freq_hz = val;
315:                 }
316:             } else if (strcmp(key, "wideband_slice_width_hz") == 0) {
317:                 // Replace atoi with strtol and check for errors
318:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
319:                 long val = strtol(value, &endptr, 10);
320:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 10000000 && val <= 28000000) {
321:                     settings.wideband_slice_width_hz = static_cast<uint32_t>(val);
322:                 }
323:             } else if (strcmp(key, "panoramic_mode_enabled") == 0) {
324:                 scan_set_panoramic_mode_enabled(settings, strcmp(value, "true") == 0);
325:             } else if (strcmp(key, "wideband_min_freq_hz") == 0) {
326:                 // Replace atoll with strtoull and check for errors
327:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
328:                 unsigned long long val = strtoull(value, &endptr, 10);
329:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 2400000000ULL && val <= 7200000000ULL) {
330:                     settings.wideband_min_freq_hz = val;
331:                 }
332:             } else if (strcmp(key, "wideband_max_freq_hz") == 0) {
333:                 // Replace atoll with strtoull and check for errors
334:                 char* endptr = nullptr;
335:                 unsigned long long val = strtoull(value, &endptr, 10);
336:                 if (endptr != value && *endptr == '\0' && val >= 2400000001ULL && val <= 7200000000ULL) {
337:                     settings.wideband_max_freq_hz = val;
338:                 }
339:             }
340:         }
341: 
342:         // Restore newline and move to next line
343:         *line_end = saved_char;
344:         line_start = (saved_char != '\0') ? line_end + 1 : line_end;
345:     }
346: 
347:     file.close();
348:     return true;
349: }

358: // const pointer, noexcept for file backup
359: void EnhancedSettingsManager::create_backup_file(const char* filepath) noexcept {
360:     // Use RAII wrapper for File to ensure proper cleanup
361:     FileRAII orig_file(filepath, true);
362:     if (!orig_file.is_open()) return;
363: 
364:     // Use fixed-size char array instead of std::string for backup path
365:     static constexpr size_t kMaxPathLen = 256;
366:     char backup_path[kMaxPathLen] = {};
367:     size_t filepath_len = strlen(filepath);
368:     if (filepath_len >= kMaxPathLen - 4) {
369:         return;  // Path too long
370:     }
371:     snprintf(backup_path, kMaxPathLen, "%s", filepath);
372:     size_t current_len = strlen(backup_path);
373:     snprintf(backup_path + current_len, kMaxPathLen - current_len, "%s", ".bak");
374: 
375:     FileRAII backup_file(backup_path, false);
376:     if (!backup_file.is_open()) return;
377: 
378:     // Thread-local buffer for backup/restore operations (512 bytes per thread)
379:     static constexpr size_t BUFFER_SIZE = 512;
380:     thread_local uint8_t buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
381:     size_t total_read = 0;
382: 
383:     while (total_read < orig_file.get().size()) {
384:         size_t to_read = std::min(BUFFER_SIZE, static_cast<size_t>(orig_file.get().size() - total_read));
385:         auto read_result = orig_file.get().read(buffer, to_read);
386:         if (read_result.is_error() || read_result.value() != to_read) break;
387: 
388:         auto write_result = backup_file.get().write(buffer, to_read);
389:         if (write_result.is_error() || write_result.value() != to_read) break;
390: 
391:         total_read += read_result.value();
392:     }
393: }
394: 
395: // const pointer, noexcept for file restore
396: void EnhancedSettingsManager::restore_from_backup(const char* filepath) noexcept {
397:     // Use fixed-size char array instead of std::string for backup path
398:     static constexpr size_t kMaxPathLen = 256;
399:     char backup_path[kMaxPathLen] = {};
400:     size_t filepath_len = strlen(filepath);
401:     if (filepath_len >= kMaxPathLen - 4) {
402:         return;  // Path too long
403:     }
404:     snprintf(backup_path, kMaxPathLen, "%s", filepath);
405:     size_t current_len = strlen(backup_path);
406:     snprintf(backup_path + current_len, kMaxPathLen - current_len, "%s", ".bak");
407: 
408:     // Use RAII wrapper for File to ensure proper cleanup
409:     FileRAII backup_file(backup_path, true);
410:     if (!backup_file.is_open()) return;
411: 
412:     FileRAII original_file(filepath, false);
413:     if (!original_file.is_open()) return;
414: 
415:     // Thread-local buffer for backup/restore operations (512 bytes per thread)
416:     static constexpr size_t BUFFER_SIZE = 512;
417:     thread_local uint8_t buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
418: 
419:     while (true) {
420:         auto read_res = backup_file.get().read(buffer, BUFFER_SIZE);
421:         if (read_res.is_error() || read_res.value() == 0) break;
422:         original_file.get().write(buffer, read_res.value());
423:     }
424: }

426: // const pointer, noexcept for file removal
427: void EnhancedSettingsManager::remove_backup_file(const char* filepath) noexcept {
428:     // Use fixed-size char array instead of std::string for backup path
429:     static constexpr size_t kMaxPathLen = 256;
430:     char backup_path[kMaxPathLen] = {};
431:     size_t filepath_len = strlen(filepath);
432:     if (filepath_len >= kMaxPathLen - 4) {
433:         return;  // Path too long
434:     }
435:     snprintf(backup_path, kMaxPathLen, "%s", filepath);
436:     size_t current_len = strlen(backup_path);
437:     snprintf(backup_path + current_len, kMaxPathLen - current_len, "%s", ".bak");
438:     
439:     // Diamond Code Standard #3 - Replace std::filesystem with FatFS C API
440:     f_unlink(reinterpret_cast<const TCHAR*>(backup_path));
441: }

450:              "# Generated by EDA App (Integrated Settings)\n"
451:              "# Timestamp: %s\n"

464: // noexcept for timestamp generation (thread_local buffer for thread safety)
465: const char* EnhancedSettingsManager::get_current_timestamp() noexcept {
466:     // Return const char* to thread_local buffer (no std::string allocation)
467:     thread_local char buffer[32];
468:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
469:     snprintf(buffer, sizeof(buffer), "%lu", (unsigned long)now);
470:     return buffer;
471: }

549: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const references, noexcept for preset application
550: bool DroneFrequencyPresets::apply_preset(DroneAnalyzerSettings& config, const ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::DronePreset& preset) noexcept {
551:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Guard clause to reduce nesting
552:     if (!preset.is_valid()) return false;
553: 
554:     config.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::MEDIUM;
555:     config.scan_interval_ms = 1000;
556:     config.rssi_threshold_db = static_cast<int32_t>(preset.threat_level) >= static_cast<int32_t>(ThreatLevel::HIGH) ? -80 : -90;
557:     audio_set_enable_alerts(config, true);
558: 
559:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Named constants for magic numbers
560:     static constexpr uint64_t WIDEBAND_MIN_FREQ = 2400000000ULL;
561:     static constexpr uint64_t WIDEBAND_MAX_FREQ = 2500000000ULL;
562:     static constexpr uint64_t FREQ_OFFSET = 10000000ULL;
563:     static constexpr uint64_t USER_MIN_FREQ = 50000000ULL;
564:     static constexpr uint64_t USER_MAX_FREQ = 6000000000ULL;
565:     
566:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(preset.frequency_hz) >= WIDEBAND_MIN_FREQ && static_cast<uint64_t>(preset.frequency_hz) <= WIDEBAND_MAX_FREQ) {
567:         scan_set_enable_wideband_scanning(config, true);
568:         config.wideband_min_freq_hz = WIDEBAND_MIN_FREQ;
569:         config.wideband_max_freq_hz = WIDEBAND_MAX_FREQ;
570:     }
571: 
572:     config.user_min_freq_hz = preset.frequency_hz - FREQ_OFFSET;
573:     config.user_max_freq_hz = preset.frequency_hz + FREQ_OFFSET;
574: 
575:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Guard clauses for frequency clamping
576:     if (config.user_min_freq_hz < USER_MIN_FREQ) {
577:         config.user_min_freq_hz = USER_MIN_FREQ;
578:     }
579:     if (config.user_max_freq_hz > USER_MAX_FREQ) {
580:         config.user_max_freq_hz = USER_MAX_FREQ;
581:     }
582: 
583:     snprintf(config.freqman_path, ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::MAX_NAME_LEN, "%s", "DRONES");
584:     disp_set_show_detailed_info(config, true);
585: 
586:     return true;
587: }

589: // DronePresetSelector Implementation
590: 
591: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Zero-allocation preset filtering using stack allocation
592: // Scott Meyers Item 29: Use object pools to reduce allocation overhead
593: // Replaces std::vector-based filtering with static stack buffer
594: static inline size_t filter_presets_by_type_stack(
595:     const std::array<DronePreset, 5>& presets,
596:     DroneType type, const DronePreset* out_filtered[], size_t max_count) {
597:     size_t found_count = 0;
598:     for (const auto& preset : presets) {
599:         if (found_count >= max_count) break;
600:         if (preset.drone_type == type) {
601:             out_filtered[found_count++] = &preset;
602:         }
603:     }
604:     return found_count;
605: }
606: 
607: // Template implementation must be in header for implicit instantiation
608: // show_preset_menu is now a template function defined in the header
609: 
610: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const reference, noexcept for filtered presets
611: void DronePresetSelector::show_type_filtered_presets(NavigationView& nav, DroneType type) noexcept {
612:     const auto& all_presets = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_all_presets();
613:     
614:     static constexpr size_t MAX_FILTERED = 5;
615:     const char* names[MAX_FILTERED];
616:     const DronePreset* filtered_ptrs[MAX_FILTERED];
617:     
618:     const size_t preset_count = filter_presets_by_type_stack(all_presets, type, filtered_ptrs, MAX_FILTERED);
619:     
620:     for (size_t i = 0; i < preset_count; ++i) {
621:         names[i] = filtered_ptrs[i]->display_name;
622:     }
623: 
624:     struct FilteredPresetsView {
625:         const DronePreset* const* presets;
626:         size_t count;
627:         const DronePreset& operator[](size_t idx) const { return *presets[idx]; }
628:         size_t size() const { return count; }
629:     };
630: 
631:     FilteredPresetsView filtered_view{filtered_ptrs, preset_count};
632:     // CRITICAL FIX: Lambda with capture passed to template - no heap allocation
633:     // The lambda type is deduced at compile time, enabling inline expansion
634:     auto on_selected = [&nav](const DronePreset&) { nav.pop(); };
635: 
636:     using FilteredPresetMenuViewT = PresetMenuViewImpl<FilteredPresetsView, decltype(on_selected)>;
637:     nav.push<FilteredPresetMenuViewT>(names, preset_count, std::move(on_selected), filtered_view);
638: }

641: // Zero heap allocation - functor stores only a pointer
642: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const reference, noexcept for callback creation
643: ConfigUpdaterCallback DronePresetSelector::create_config_updater(DroneAnalyzerSettings& config_to_update) noexcept {
644:     return ConfigUpdaterCallback{config_to_update};
645: }

658:            rssi_threshold_db >= -120 && rssi_threshold_db <= 0 &&
659:            bandwidth_hz > 0;
660: }

670: // DIAMOND FIX: Add noexcept to match header declaration
671: void HardwareSettingsView::focus() noexcept { button_save_.focus(); }
672: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified LUT lookup  SpectrumMode conversion
673: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
674: // RAM: LUT   Flash,  heap allocation
675: // : O(1) lookup  5-branch switch
676: // : EDA::LUTs::spectrum_mode_ui_index() (SSOT)
677: 
678: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for settings load
679: void HardwareSettingsView::load_current_settings() noexcept {
680:     DroneAnalyzerSettings settings;
681:     // FIX #M3: Check return value of load() and handle errors appropriately
682:     auto load_result = SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings);
683:     if (!load_result.is_ok() || !load_result.value) {
684:         SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings);
685:     }
686:     checkbox_real_hardware_.set_value(hw_get_enable_real_hardware(settings));
687:     field_spectrum_mode_.set_selected_index(static_cast<int>(settings.spectrum_mode));
688:     number_bandwidth_.set_value(settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz);
689:     number_min_freq_.set_value(static_cast<rf::Frequency>(settings.user_min_freq_hz));
690:     number_max_freq_.set_value(static_cast<rf::Frequency>(settings.user_max_freq_hz));
691: }
692: 
693: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for settings save
694: void HardwareSettingsView::save_current_settings() noexcept {
695:     DroneAnalyzerSettings settings;
696:     // FIX #M3: Check return value of load() and handle errors appropriately
697:     auto load_result = SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings);
698:     if (!load_result.is_ok() || !load_result.value) {
699:         SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings);
700:     }
701:     
702:     hw_set_enable_real_hardware(settings, checkbox_real_hardware_.value());
703:     hw_set_demo_mode(settings, !checkbox_real_hardware_.value());
704:     settings.spectrum_mode = static_cast<SpectrumMode>(field_spectrum_mode_.selected_index());
705:     settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz = static_cast<uint32_t>(number_bandwidth_.value());
706:     settings.user_min_freq_hz = static_cast<uint64_t>(number_min_freq_.value());

901: // DroneDatabaseManager
902: // Stage 4: Updated to use UnifiedDroneDatabase
903: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const pointer, noexcept for database load
904: DroneDatabaseManager::DatabaseView DroneDatabaseManager::load_database(const char* file_path) noexcept {
905:     DatabaseView view{};
906:     
907:     // Use UnifiedDroneDatabase for loading
908:     auto& db = UnifiedDroneDatabase::instance();
909:     
910:     // Initialize and load from file
911:     if (!db.initialize()) {
912:         return view;
913:     }
914:     
915:     if (!db.load(file_path)) {
916:         // Return empty view if load fails
917:         return view;
918:     }
919:     
920:     // Convert UnifiedDroneDatabase entries to DatabaseView format
921:     size_t db_count = db.size();
922:     size_t count = 0;
923:     
924:     for (size_t i = 0; i < db_count && count < MAX_DATABASE_ENTRIES; ++i) {
925:         const UnifiedDroneEntry* entry = db.get_entry(i);
926:         if (entry == nullptr || entry->frequency_hz == 0) continue;
927:         
928:         view.entries[count].freq = entry->frequency_hz;
929:         
930:         // Copy description safely (max 31 chars + null terminator)
931:         size_t desc_len = 0;
932:         while (desc_len < 31 && entry->description[desc_len] != '\0') {
933:             view.entries[count].description[desc_len] = entry->description[desc_len];
934:             desc_len++;
935:         }
936:         view.entries[count].description[desc_len] = '\0';
937:         
938:         count++;
939:     }
940:     
941:     view.count = count;
942:     return view;
943: }
944: 
945: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const reference, const pointer, noexcept for database save
946: // Stage 4: Updated to use UnifiedDroneDatabase with validation
947: bool DroneDatabaseManager::save_database(const DatabaseView& view, const char* file_path) noexcept {
948:     auto& db = UnifiedDroneDatabase::instance();
949:     
950:     // Clear database for fresh import
951:     db.clear();
952:     
953:     // Validate and add entries
954:     for (size_t i = 0; i < view.count; ++i) {
955:         const auto& entry = view.entries[i];
956:         if (entry.freq == 0) continue;
957:         
958:         // Create UnifiedDroneEntry for validation
959:         UnifiedDroneEntry unified_entry;
960:         unified_entry.frequency_hz = entry.freq;
961:         
962:         // Copy description safely (max 31 chars + null terminator for UnifiedDroneEntry)
963:         size_t desc_len = 0;
964:         while (desc_len < 31 && entry.description[desc_len] != '\0') {
965:             unified_entry.description[desc_len] = entry.description[desc_len];
966:             desc_len++;
967:         }
968:         unified_entry.description[desc_len] = '\0';
969:         
970:         // Validate entry before adding
971:         auto validation = FrequencyValidation::validate_entry(unified_entry);
972:         if (!validation.valid) {
973:             // Skip invalid entries but continue processing
974:             continue;
975:         }
976: 
977:         // Add to unified database
978:         (void)db.add_entry(unified_entry);
979:     }
980:     
981:     // Save to file
982:     bool success = db.save(file_path);
983:     
984:     // Observers are automatically notified by save()
985:     return success;
986: }
987: 
988: // DroneDatabaseListView
989: // Static member definitions (required for ODR compliance)
990: DroneDatabaseManager::DatabaseView DroneDatabaseListView::g_database_view{};
991: Mutex DroneDatabaseListView::g_database_mutex{};
992: // DIAMOND FIX: volatile bool for thread safety (std::atomic not available in embedded environment)
993: // Access is protected by g_database_mutex for consistency with g_database_view
994: volatile bool DroneDatabaseListView::g_database_loaded{false};
995: 
996: DroneDatabaseListView::DroneDatabaseListView(NavigationView& nav)
997:     : View(), nav_(nav) {
998:     add_children({&menu_view_});
999:     // Lock mutex before accessing static member
1000:     MutexLock lock(g_database_mutex, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
1001:     // Lazy initialization: only load database once
1002:     if (!g_database_loaded) {
1003:         g_database_view = DroneDatabaseManager::load_database();
1004:         g_database_loaded = true;
1005:     }
1006:     menu_view_.clear();
1007:     menu_view_.add_item({"[+ ADD NEW FREQUENCY]", Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
1008:     for (size_t i = 0; i < g_database_view.count; ++i) {
1009:         const auto& entry = g_database_view.entries[i];
1010:         constexpr size_t FREQ_BUF_SIZE = 24;
1011:         char freq_buf[FREQ_BUF_SIZE];
1012:         FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), entry.freq);
1013:         
1014:         constexpr size_t TEXT_BUFFER_SIZE = 64;
1015:         char text_buffer[TEXT_BUFFER_SIZE];
1016:         snprintf(text_buffer, sizeof(text_buffer), "%s: %s", freq_buf, entry.description);
1017:         
1018:         // FIX #25: Use text_buffer directly instead of std::string (no heap allocation)
1019:         // The MenuView will copy the string internally
1020:         menu_view_.add_item({text_buffer, Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
1021:     }
1022: }
1023: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for focus
1024: void DroneDatabaseListView::focus() noexcept { menu_view_.focus(); }
1025: 
1026: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for entry selection
1027: void DroneDatabaseListView::on_entry_selected(size_t index) noexcept {
1028:     if (index == 0) {
1029:         DroneDbEntry empty_entry;
1030:         auto on_add = [this](const DroneDbEntry& entry) {
1031:             MutexLock lock(g_database_mutex, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
1032:             if (entry.freq != 0 && g_database_view.count < DroneDatabaseManager::MAX_DATABASE_ENTRIES) {
1033:                 g_database_view.entries[g_database_view.count++] = entry;
1034:                 save_changes_locked();  // Use unlocked version since we already hold the mutex
1035:                 menu_view_.clear();
1036:                 menu_view_.add_item({"[+ ADD NEW FREQUENCY]", Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
1037:                 for (size_t i = 0; i < g_database_view.count; ++i) {
1038:                     const auto& entry = g_database_view.entries[i];
1039:                     constexpr size_t FREQ_BUF_SIZE = 24;
1040:                     char freq_buf[FREQ_BUF_SIZE];
1041:                     FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), entry.freq);
1042:                     
1043:                     constexpr size_t TEXT_BUFFER_SIZE = 64;
1044:                     char text_buffer[TEXT_BUFFER_SIZE];
1045:                     snprintf(text_buffer, sizeof(text_buffer), "%s: %s", freq_buf, entry.description);
1046:                     
1047:                     // FIX #25: Use text_buffer directly instead of std::string (no heap allocation)
1048:                     menu_view_.add_item({text_buffer, Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
1049:                 }
1050:             }
1051:         };
1052:         using EditorViewT = DroneEntryEditorView<decltype(on_add)>;
1053:         nav_.push<EditorViewT>(empty_entry, std::move(on_add));
1054:     } else {
1055:         size_t entry_index = index - 1;
1056:         auto on_edit = [this, entry_index](const DroneDbEntry& entry) {
1057:             MutexLock lock(g_database_mutex, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
1058:             if (entry.freq != 0) {
1059:                 g_database_view.entries[entry_index] = entry;
1060:                 save_changes_locked();  // Use unlocked version since we already hold the mutex
1061:                 menu_view_.clear();
1062:                 menu_view_.add_item({"[+ ADD NEW FREQUENCY]", Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
1063:                 for (size_t i = 0; i < g_database_view.count; ++i) {
1064:                     const auto& entry = g_database_view.entries[i];
1065:                     constexpr size_t FREQ_BUF_SIZE = 24;
1066:                     char freq_buf[FREQ_BUF_SIZE];
1067:                     FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), entry.freq);
1068:                     
1069:                     constexpr size_t TEXT_BUFFER_SIZE = 64;
1070:                     char text_buffer[TEXT_BUFFER_SIZE];
1071:                     snprintf(text_buffer, sizeof(text_buffer), "%s: %s", freq_buf, entry.description);
1072:                     
1073:                     // FIX #25: Use text_buffer directly instead of std::string (no heap allocation)
1074:                     menu_view_.add_item({text_buffer, Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
1075:                 }
1076:             }
1077:         };
1078:         using EditorViewT = DroneEntryEditorView<decltype(on_edit)>;
1079:         nav_.push<EditorViewT>(g_database_view.entries[entry_index], std::move(on_edit));
1080:     }
1081: }
1082: 
1083: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for save
1084: // Note: Assumes g_database_mutex is already held by caller
1085: // This prevents deadlock when called from on_entry_selected() which already holds the lock
1086: void DroneDatabaseListView::save_changes_locked() noexcept {
1087:     (void)DroneDatabaseManager::save_database(g_database_view);
1088: }
1089: 
1090: // Public wrapper that acquires the lock for external callers
1091: void DroneDatabaseListView::save_changes() noexcept {
1092:     MutexLock lock(g_database_mutex, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
1093:     save_changes_locked();
1094: }
1095: 
1096: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: noexcept for key handling
1097: bool DroneDatabaseListView::on_key(const KeyEvent key) noexcept {
1098:     if (key == KeyEvent::Select) {
1099:         size_t index = menu_view_.highlighted_index();
1100:         on_entry_selected(index);
1101:         return true;
1102:     }
1103:     return View::on_key(key);
1104: }

1107: // DISABLED: Duplicate DroneDatabaseParser class
1108: // This class has been replaced by the unified DatabaseParser namespace in
1109: // eda_database_parser.hpp. The new implementation provides:
1110: //   - DatabaseParser::parse_freqman_line() for freqman format
1111: //   - DatabaseParser::parse_csv_line() for CSV format
1112: //   - DatabaseParser::parse_line() for auto-detect format
1113: //   - DatabaseParser::write_freqman_line() for writing freqman format
1114: //   - DatabaseParser::write_csv_line() for writing CSV format
1115: // =============================================================================
1116: #if 0
1117: // CSV Parser for Drone Database - Extracted for separation of concerns
1118: namespace {
1119: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: POD struct for parse result (zero heap allocation)
1120: struct ParseResult {
1121:     DroneDbEntry entry{};
1122:     bool success = false;
1123: };
1124: 
1125: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Static parser class with zero heap allocation
1126: class DroneDatabaseParser {
1127: public:
1128:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Static method with noexcept for performance
1129:     // Parses a single CSV line and returns ParseResult
1130:     // Format: "frequency,description" or "# comment"
1131:     static ParseResult parse_line(const char* line, size_t line_length) noexcept {
1132:         ParseResult result{};
1133:         
1134:         // Handle empty lines
1135:         if (line_length == 0 || line[0] == '\0') {
1136:             return result;
1137:         }
1138:         
1139:         // Handle comment lines (lines starting with #)
1140:         if (line[0] == '#') {
1141:             return result;
1142:         }
1143:         
1144:         // Find comma separator
1145:         const char* comma = static_cast<const char*>(memchr(line, ',', line_length));
1146:         if (!comma) {
1147:             return result;
1148:         }
1149:         
1150:         // Calculate frequency string length
1151:         size_t freq_length = static_cast<size_t>(comma - line);
1152:         if (freq_length == 0) {
1153:             return result;
1154:         }
1155:         
1156:         // Parse frequency
1157:         char freq_str[64];
1158:         size_t copy_len = (freq_length < sizeof(freq_str) - 1) ? freq_length : sizeof(freq_str) - 1;
1159:         for (size_t i = 0; i < copy_len; ++i) {
1160:             freq_str[i] = line[i];
1161:         }
1162:         freq_str[copy_len] = '\0';
1163:         
1164:         result.entry.freq = strtoull(freq_str, nullptr, 10);
1165:         
1166:         // Calculate description pointer and length
1167:         const char* desc = comma + 1;
1168:         size_t desc_offset = static_cast<size_t>(desc - line);
1169:         size_t desc_length = line_length - desc_offset;
1170:         
1171:         // Skip leading spaces
1172:         while (desc_length > 0 && *desc == ' ') {
1173:             desc++;
1174:             desc_length--;
1175:         }
1176:         
1177:         // Safe copy description with bounds checking
1178:         size_t max_desc_len = sizeof(result.entry.description) - 1;
1179:         size_t actual_copy_len = (desc_length < max_desc_len) ? desc_length : max_desc_len;
1180:         
1181:         for (size_t j = 0; j < actual_copy_len && desc[j] != '\0'; ++j) {
1182:             result.entry.description[j] = desc[j];
1183:         }
1184:         result.entry.description[actual_copy_len] = '\0';
1185:         
1186:         // Mark as successful only if frequency is valid
1187:         result.success = (result.entry.freq > 0);
1188:         
1189:         return result;
1190:     }
1191: };
1192: } // anonymous namespace
1193: #endif // DISABLED: Duplicate DroneDatabaseParser - use DatabaseParser from eda_database_parser.hpp
1194: 
1195: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer

2: 
3: // Corresponding header (must be first)
4: #include "ui_signal_processing.hpp"
5: 
6: // C++ standard library headers (alphabetical order)
7: #include <algorithm>
8: #include <limits>
9: 
10: // Third-party library headers
11: #include <ch.h>
12: 
13: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer {
14: 
15: // Implementation: update_detection()
16: // / @brief Update detection entry (mutex-protected writer)
17: // / @note Updates or creates a detection entry for given frequency hash.
18: // / @note Uses linear probing with simple modulo-based hash for collision resolution.
19: // / @note Evicts oldest entry when hash table is full (ring buffer eviction).
20: // / @note SYNCHRONIZATION:
21: // /   - Acquires buffer_mutex_ for exclusive access
22: // /   - Increments global_version_ for concurrent update detection
23: // /   - Stores head_ with release semantics
24: // / @note RED TEAM FIX: Recursion detection prevents deadlock when called recursively.
25: // / @note DIAMOND FIX: Uses DetectionUpdate struct to prevent parameter swapping
26: // / @param update Detection update parameters (frequency_hash, detection_count, rssi_value)
27: 
28: void DetectionRingBuffer::update_detection(const DetectionUpdate& update) noexcept {
29:     const FrequencyHash frequency_hash = update.frequency_hash;
30:     const DetectionCount detection_count = update.detection_count;
31:     const RSSIValue rssi_value = update.rssi_value;
32:     const Timestamp current_time = static_cast<Timestamp>(chTimeNow());
33: 
34:     // Check recursion depth BEFORE acquiring mutex
35:     if (recursion_depth_ > 0) {
36:         // Recursive call detected - return early to prevent deadlock
37:         return;
38:     }
39: 
40:     // DIAMOND FIX #2-3: Replace OrderedScopedLock with MutexLock from eda_locking.hpp
41:     // Lock order: DATA_MUTEX (level 1) for detection data and frequency database
42:     MutexLock lock(buffer_mutex_, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
43: 
44:     // Increment recursion depth after lock acquisition
45:     recursion_depth_++;
46: 
47:     // Increment global version for this update
48:     global_version_++;
49: 
50:     // Hash table lookup (using simple modulo-based hash)
51:     const size_t hash_idx = hash_index(frequency_hash);
52: 
53:     // Linear probe (bounded by HASH_TABLE_SIZE)
54:     for (size_t probe = 0; probe < DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_TABLE_SIZE; ++probe) {
55:         const EntryIndex idx = (hash_idx + probe) & DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_MASK;
56: 
57:         // Check for existing entry
58:         if (entries_[idx].frequency_hash == frequency_hash) {
59:             // Update entry with new version
60:             entries_[idx].version = global_version_;
61:             entries_[idx].rssi_value = rssi_value;
62:             entries_[idx].detection_count = detection_count;
63:             entries_[idx].timestamp = current_time;
64: 
65:             // FIX #7: Decrement recursion depth (lock-based approach)
66:             recursion_depth_--;
67:             return;
68:         }
69: 
70:         // Check for empty slot
71:         if (entries_[idx].frequency_hash == DetectionBufferConstants::EMPTY_HASH_MARKER) {
72:             entries_[idx].version = global_version_;
73:             entries_[idx].frequency_hash = frequency_hash;
74:             entries_[idx].detection_count = detection_count;
75:             entries_[idx].rssi_value = rssi_value;
76:             entries_[idx].timestamp = current_time;
77: 
78:             recursion_depth_--;
79:             return;
80:         }
81:     }
82: 
83:     // Table full, evict oldest entry (ring buffer eviction)
84:     const size_t evict_idx = head_;
85:     entries_[evict_idx].version = global_version_;
86:     entries_[evict_idx].frequency_hash = frequency_hash;
87:     entries_[evict_idx].detection_count = detection_count;
88:     entries_[evict_idx].rssi_value = rssi_value;
89:     entries_[evict_idx].timestamp = current_time;
90:     head_ = (head_ + 1) & DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_MASK;
91: 
92:     recursion_depth_--;
93: }
94: 
95: // IMPLEMENTATION: get_detection_count()
96: // * * @brief Get detection count (mutex-protected reader)
97: // * * FIX #RC-2: Full mutex protection (was lock-free)
98: // * * SYNCHRONIZATION:
99: // * * - Acquires buffer_mutex_ for exclusive access
100: // * * - Ensures consistent read of entry state
101: // * * - Eliminates torn reads and inconsistent state
102: // * * @param frequency_hash Hash of frequency to query
103: // * @return Detection count (0 if not found)
104: DetectionCount DetectionRingBuffer::get_detection_count(FrequencyHash frequency_hash) const noexcept {
105:     // FIX #RC-2: Full mutex protection (was lock-free)
106:     MutexLock lock(buffer_mutex_, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
107: 
108:     // Hash table lookup
109:     const size_t hash_idx = hash_index(frequency_hash);
110: 
111:     // Linear probe (bounded by HASH_TABLE_SIZE)
112:     for (size_t probe = 0; probe < DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_TABLE_SIZE; ++probe) {
113:         const EntryIndex idx = (hash_idx + probe) & DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_MASK;
114: 
115:         // Check for matching entry
116:         if (entries_[idx].frequency_hash == frequency_hash) {
117:             return entries_[idx].detection_count;
118:         }
119: 
120:         // Check for empty slot (not found)
121:         if (entries_[idx].frequency_hash == DetectionBufferConstants::EMPTY_HASH_MARKER) {
122:             return 0;
123:         }
124:     }
125: 
126:     return 0;
127: }
128: 
129: // IMPLEMENTATION: get_rssi_value()
130: // * * @brief Get RSSI value (mutex-protected reader)
131: // * * FIX #RC-2: Full mutex protection (was lock-free)
132: // * * SYNCHRONIZATION:
133: // * * - Acquires buffer_mutex_ for exclusive access
134: // * * - Ensures consistent read of entry state
135: // * * - Eliminates torn reads and inconsistent state
136: // * * @param frequency_hash Hash of frequency to query
137: // * @return RSSI value (DEFAULT_RSSI_DBM if not found)
138: RSSIValue DetectionRingBuffer::get_rssi_value(FrequencyHash frequency_hash) const noexcept {
139:     // FIX #RC-2: Full mutex protection (was lock-free)
140:     MutexLock lock(buffer_mutex_, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
141: 
142:     // Hash table lookup
143:     const size_t hash_idx = hash_index(frequency_hash);
144: 
145:     // Linear probe (bounded by HASH_TABLE_SIZE)
146:     for (size_t probe = 0; probe < DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_TABLE_SIZE; ++probe) {
147:         const EntryIndex idx = (hash_idx + probe) & DetectionBufferConstants::HASH_MASK;
148: 
149:         // Check for matching entry
150:         if (entries_[idx].frequency_hash == frequency_hash) {
151:             return entries_[idx].rssi_value;
152:         }
153: 
154:         // Check for empty slot (not found)
155:         if (entries_[idx].frequency_hash == DetectionBufferConstants::EMPTY_HASH_MARKER) {
156:             return DetectionBufferConstants::DEFAULT_RSSI_DBM;
157:         }
158:     }
159: 
160:     return DetectionBufferConstants::DEFAULT_RSSI_DBM;
161: }
162: 
163: // IMPLEMENTATION: clear()
164: // * * @brief Clear all entries (mutex-protected)
165: // * * Resets all entries to empty state and resets head index.
166: // * * SYNCHRONIZATION:
167: // * * - Acquires buffer_mutex_ for exclusive access
168: // * * - Increments global_version_ for concurrent update detection
169: // * * - Resets head_ with release semantics
170: void DetectionRingBuffer::clear() noexcept {
171:     // DIAMOND FIX #2-3: Replace OrderedScopedLock with MutexLock from eda_locking.hpp
172:     // Lock order: DATA_MUTEX (level 1) for detection data and frequency database
173:     MutexLock lock(buffer_mutex_, LockOrder::DATA_MUTEX);
174: 
175:     // Increment global version
176:     global_version_++;
177: 
178:     // Clear all entries
179:     for (auto& entry : entries_) {
180:         init_entry(entry, global_version_);
181:     }
182: 
183:     // Reset head index
184:     head_ = 0;
185: }
186: 
187: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
